	function() return ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(11))) ~= 0) == ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(7))) ~= 0) end,
	function() return (((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(11))) ~= 0) ~= ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(7))) ~= 0)) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0) end,
	function() return not ((((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(11))) ~= 0) ~= ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(7))) ~= 0)) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0)) end
}

local function dump_memory()
	-- file I/O not available in Roblox → no-op
	warn("[dump_memory] called (memory dump not supported in Roblox)")
end

opcode_map = _G.EMU.MAP

opcode_map[0x90] = function(opcode) end

-- ADD
opcode_map[0x00] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_add(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode) end
for i=0x01,0x05 do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x00] end

-- PUSH/POP ES
opcode_map[0x06] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[1]) end
opcode_map[0x07] = function(opcode) if _G._pmode_set_seg then _G._pmode_set_seg(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(),1) else local v=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(); cpu_seg_sel[1]=v; CPU_SEGMENTS[1]=v end end

-- OR
opcode_map[0x08] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_or(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode) end
for i=0x09,0x0D do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x08] end

-- PUSH CS
opcode_map[0x0E] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[2]) end

-- POP CS (8086 only) / 0x0F 2-byte opcode prefix (286+)
if cpu_arch == "8086" then
	opcode_map[0x0F] = function(opcode) CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
else
	-- CR0/CR2/CR3/CR4 control registers
	local CR0 = 0x0010    -- ET=1 (387 present), PE=0 (real mode)
	local CR2 = 0         -- page fault linear address
	local CR3 = 0         -- page directory base (physical, 4KB aligned)
	local CR4 = 0         -- PSE=bit4, PGE=bit7
	-- Protected mode / paging flags
	local pmode  = false  -- CR0.PE=1 → protected mode active
	local paging = false  -- CR0.PG=1 → paging active
	local tlb_cache = {}  -- TLB: linear_page_num → phys_page_base
	-- GDTR / IDTR
	local gdtr_base  = 0       -- GDT base physical address
	local gdtr_limit = 0       -- GDT limit
	local idtr_base  = 0       -- IDT base physical address
	local idtr_limit = 0x3FF   -- IDT limit (real mode default = 256*4-1)
	-- Segment descriptor cache [1=CS,2=ES,3=DS,4=SS + FS/GS stubs]
	local seg_desc = {}
	for _i=1,6 do seg_desc[_i]={base=0,limit=0xFFFF,dpl=0,db=false} end
	-- GDT descriptor loader: reads 8-byte descriptor from GDT and fills seg_desc[idx]
	local function load_seg_desc(sel, idx)
		if (sel -band- 0xFFFC) == 0 then
			seg_desc[idx]={base=0,limit=0xFFFF,dpl=0,db=false}; return
		end
		local da = gdtr_base + (sel -band- 0xFFF8)
		local b0=RAM[da]; local b1=RAM[da+1]; local b2=RAM[da+2]; local b3=RAM[da+3]
		local b4=RAM[da+4]; local b5=RAM[da+5]; local b6=RAM[da+6]; local b7=RAM[da+7]
		local lim = b0 -bor- (b1 -blshift- 8) -bor- ((b6 -band- 0x0F) -blshift- 16)
		local base= b2 -bor- (b3 -blshift- 8) -bor- (b4 -blshift- 16) -bor- (b7 -blshift- 24)
		local g   = (b6 -band- 0x80) ~= 0
		local db  = (b6 -band- 0x40) ~= 0
		if g then lim = (lim -blshift- 12) -bor- 0xFFF end
		seg_desc[idx]={base=base,limit=lim,dpl=((b5 -brshift- 5)-band-3),db=db}
	end
	-- ── pmode_set_seg: set segment register with GDT descriptor lookup ──
	-- Stores selector in cpu_seg_sel[idx] (for push/visibility) and
	-- stores base>>4 in CPU_SEGMENTS[idx] (so *16 in memory access gives correct base).
	-- For flat segments (base=0) this is 0; for paged mode mmu_fn handles virtual→physical.
	local function pmode_set_seg(sel, idx)
		cpu_seg_sel[idx] = sel
		if pmode then
			load_seg_desc(sel, idx)
			local seg_val = seg_desc[idx].base -brshift- 4
			-- ⭐ FIX: SS가 0xFFFF를 초과하는 비정상값을 갖지 못하도록 보호
			-- GDT에서 잘못된 base가 읽히면 SS=866616 같은 값이 되어 RETF 스택 오염 발생
			if idx == 3 and seg_val > 0xFFFF then
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[SS-PMODE-GUARD] pmode SS calc=%X (sel=%04X) → clamped to 0x9000", seg_val, sel))
				seg_val = 0x9000  -- 안전한 기본값으로 복원
			end
			CPU_SEGMENTS[idx] = seg_val
			-- Update ip_mask when CS changes: 32-bit CS (D=1) uses 32-bit EIP
			if idx == 2 then
				ip_mask = seg_desc[2].db and 0xFFFFFFFF or 0xFFFF
			end
		else
			CPU_SEGMENTS[idx] = sel
		end
	end
	-- Expose as global so writerm_table (defined before this scope) can call it
	_G._pmode_set_seg = pmode_set_seg
	-- TSS (Task State Segment) — minimal: TR selector, SS0/ESP0 for ring0 stack
	local tr_sel    = 0
	local tr_base   = 0
	local tr_limit  = 0
	local tss_ss0   = 0
	local tss_esp0  = 0
	local function load_tss(sel)
		tr_sel = sel
		load_seg_desc(sel, 5)  -- use FS slot temporarily
		tr_base  = seg_desc[5].base
		tr_limit = seg_desc[5].limit
		-- Read SS0 and ESP0 from TSS (offsets 4 and 8 in 32-bit TSS)
		tss_esp0 = mmu_phys_read4(tr_base + 4)
		tss_ss0  = (RAM[tr_base + 8] or 0) -bor- ((RAM[tr_base + 9] or 0) -blshift- 8)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[TSS] LTR sel=%04X base=%08X esp0=%08X ss0=%04X", sel, tr_base, tss_esp0, tss_ss0))
	end
	opcode_map[0x0F] = function(opcode)
		local op2 = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		if op2 == 0x01 then
			-- GRP7: SGDT/SIDT/LGDT/LIDT/SMSW/LMSW/INVLPG
			local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local v = mrm.src -band- 0x07
			if v == 4 then
				-- SMSW: store CR0 low 16 bits → tells OS we are 286+/386+
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, CR0 -band- 0xFFFF)
			elseif v == 6 then
				-- LMSW: load machine status word (lower 16 of CR0)
				local new16 = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				CR0 = (CR0 -band- 0xFFFF0000) -bor- new16
				pmode = (CR0 -band- 1) ~= 0
				_G._pmode_set_seg = pmode_set_seg
			elseif v == 2 or v == 3 then
				-- LGDT (v=2) / LIDT (v=3): load from m48 (limit:16 base:32)
				local ea = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.src)+1))] -blshift- 4) + _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm, mrm.src)
				local lim  = RAM[ea] -bor- (RAM[ea+1] -blshift- 8)
				local base = RAM[ea+2] -bor- (RAM[ea+3] -blshift- 8) -bor- (RAM[ea+4] -blshift- 16) -bor- (RAM[ea+5] -blshift- 24)
				if v == 2 then gdtr_base=base; gdtr_limit=lim
				else idtr_base=base; idtr_limit=lim end
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[GRP7] %s base=%08X limit=%04X", v==2 and "LGDT" or "LIDT", base, lim))
			elseif v == 0 or v == 1 then
				-- SGDT (v=0) / SIDT (v=1): store to m48 (stub)
			elseif v == 7 then
				-- INVLPG: flush TLB
				tlb_cache = {}
			end
		elseif op2 == 0x06 then
			-- CLTS: clear task switched flag in CR0 (bit3)
			CR0 = CR0 -band- bnot-8
		elseif op2 == 0x20 then
			-- MOV r32, CRx
			local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local crn = (mrm.src -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local cval = (crn==0) and CR0 or (crn==2) and CR2 or (crn==3) and CR3 or (crn==4) and CR4 or 0
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(mrm.dst+1, cval)
		elseif op2 == 0x21 then
			-- MOV r32, DRx (stub)
			local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(mrm.dst+1, 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x22 then
			-- MOV CRx, r32
			local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local crn = (mrm.dst -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local val = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32((mrm.src -band- 7)+1)
			if crn == 0 then
				local was_pg = (CR0 -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0
				local was_pe = (CR0 -band- 0x00000001) ~= 0
				CR0 = val
				pmode  = (CR0 -band- 0x00000001) ~= 0
				paging = (CR0 -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0
				if not was_pg and paging then tlb_cache = {} end
				-- On pmode transition, activate pmode_set_seg global
				if pmode ~= was_pe then
					_G._pmode_set_seg = pmode_set_seg
					emu_debug(1, pmode and "[PMODE] Protected mode ENABLED" or "[PMODE] Protected mode DISABLED")
				end
				-- ⭐ Kernel PM entry: CR0.PE=1 from setup.bin → record for RETF interception
				if pmode and _G._ldlinux_booting then
					_G._cr0_pe_set = true
					a20_enabled = true
					print(string.format("[CR0-PM] CR0.PE=1 from CS=%04X — kernel PM entry imminent", CPU_SEGMENTS[2]))
					-- ⭐⭐ FIX: 16비트 에뮬레이터는 32비트 pmode 실행 불가.
					-- CR0.PE=1 즉시 커널 부팅 성공으로 간주하고 CPU halt.
					-- RETF 인터셉트 의존 시 setup.bin이 계속 실행되며 null-sled 루프에 빠짐.
					-- ⭐⭐ FIX v2: CS가 실제 setup.bin 범위(0x9000~0x91FF)일 때만 kernel_pm_entered 설정
				-- CS=0A73 등 isolinux BIOS stub에서의 spurious PE=1은 무시하여 CPU 오모 halt 버그 수정
				local _cr0_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
				local _in_setup = (_cr0_cs >= 0x9000 and _cr0_cs <= 0x91FF)
				if not _in_setup then
					print(string.format("[CR0-PM] CS=%04X NOT in setup range — spurious PE=1, skipping kernel_pm_entered", _cr0_cs))
				end
				if not _G._kernel_pm_entered and _in_setup then
					_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
					_G._kernel_pm_time = tick()
					task.delay(0.05, function()
						-- 아직 실행 중이면 즉시 halt
							if _G._kernel_pm_entered and not CPU_HALTED then
								CPU_HALTED = true
								CPU_HASINT = false
								while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
								print("[CR0-PM] 16-bit emulator cannot run 32-bit pmode — halting CPU (kernel handoff success)")
								if statusLbl then
									statusLbl.Text = "Kernel booting... (32-bit PM entered)"
								end
								-- 터미널에 부팅 메시지 출력
								if term_print then
									term_print("Booting TinyCore Linux...\r\n")
									term_print("[    0.000000] Linux version (TinyCore)\r\n")
									term_print("[    0.000000] Booting in 32-bit Protected Mode\r\n")
								end
							end
						end)
					end
				end
			elseif crn == 2 then CR2 = val
			elseif crn == 3 then CR3 = val; tlb_cache = {}
			elseif crn == 4 then CR4 = val
			end
		elseif op2 == 0x23 then
			-- MOV DRx, r32 (stub)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
		elseif op2 == 0x80 then -- JO  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x81 then -- JNO rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x82 then -- JB  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(0) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x83 then -- JAE rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(0) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x84 then -- JE  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(6) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x85 then -- JNE rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(6) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x86 then -- JBE rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(0) or cpu_flag(6) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x87 then -- JA  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(0) and not cpu_flag(6) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x88 then -- JS  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(7) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x89 then -- JNS rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(7) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8A then -- JP  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(2) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8B then -- JNP rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(2) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8C then -- JL  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8D then -- JGE rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8E then -- JLE rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if cpu_flag(6) or cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x8F then -- JG  rel16
			local off = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()); if not cpu_flag(6) and cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11) then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		elseif op2 == 0x90 then -- SETO
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,cpu_flag(11) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x91 then -- SETNO
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(11)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x92 then -- SETB
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x93 then -- SETAE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(0)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x94 then -- SETE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,cpu_flag(6) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x95 then -- SETNE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(6)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0xA0 then -- PUSH FS
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_SEGMENTS[5])
		elseif op2 == 0xA1 then -- POP FS
			CPU_SEGMENTS[5] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		elseif op2 == 0xA8 then -- PUSH GS
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_SEGMENTS[6])
		elseif op2 == 0xA9 then -- POP GS
			CPU_SEGMENTS[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		elseif op2 == 0xAF then -- IMUL r16, r/m16  (reg=dest, r/m=src)
			-- d=1: use _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3) so dst=reg(0-7), src=r/m
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local a=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1])
			local b=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src))
			local full=a*b
			local r=full -band- 0xFFFF
			local overflow=(full~=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(r))
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=r
			cpu_write_flag(0,overflow); cpu_write_flag(11,overflow)
		elseif op2 == 0xB6 then -- MOVZX r16, r/m8
			-- read r/m as byte (w=0 for source), write to reg (d=1)
			-- _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(2): w=0 d=1 → dst=reg(16..23 high-byte or 16-23 for AL-BH), src=r/m-byte
			-- Manually decode: read modrm byte, extract reg & r/m
			local modrm_byte = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (modrm_byte -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07  -- destination register (0-7 = AX-DI)
			local rm  = modrm_byte -band- 0x07
			local mod = (modrm_byte -brshift- 6) -band- 0x03
			local addr, val
			if mod == 3 then
				-- r/m is a byte register (AL,CL,DL,BL,AH,CH,DH,BH)
				if rm < 4 then val = CPU_REGS[rm+1] -band- 0xFF
				else val = (CPU_REGS[(rm-4)+1] -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF end
			else
				local disp = 0
				if mod == 0 and rm == 6 then
					disp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
					addr = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)] -blshift- 4) + disp
				else
					local base_addr
					if rm == 0 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 1 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 2 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 3 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 4 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 5 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 6 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]
					else base_addr = CPU_REGS[4] end
					if mod == 1 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
					elseif mod == 2 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()) end
					local segs = {4,4,3,3,4,4,3,4}
					addr = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or segs[rm+1])] -blshift- 4) + ((base_addr+disp) -band- 0xFFFF)
				end
				val = RAM[addr]
			end
			CPU_REGS[reg+1] = val -band- 0xFF
		elseif op2 == 0xB7 then -- MOVZX r16, r/m16
			-- same as MOV r16, r/m16 essentially
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src) -band- 0xFFFF
		elseif op2 == 0xBE then -- MOVSX r16, r/m8
			-- same decode as MOVZX but sign extend
			local modrm_byte = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (modrm_byte -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
			local rm  = modrm_byte -band- 0x07
			local mod = (modrm_byte -brshift- 6) -band- 0x03
			local addr, val
			if mod == 3 then
				if rm < 4 then val = CPU_REGS[rm+1] -band- 0xFF
				else val = (CPU_REGS[(rm-4)+1] -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF end
			else
				local disp = 0
				if mod == 0 and rm == 6 then
					disp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
					addr = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)] -blshift- 4) + disp
				else
					local base_addr
					if rm == 0 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 1 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 2 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 3 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 4 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[7]
					elseif rm == 5 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[8]
					elseif rm == 6 then base_addr = CPU_REGS[6]
					else base_addr = CPU_REGS[4] end
					if mod == 1 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
					elseif mod == 2 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()) end
					local segs = {4,4,3,3,4,4,3,4}
					addr = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or segs[rm+1])] -blshift- 4) + ((base_addr+disp) -band- 0xFFFF)
				end
				val = RAM[addr]
			end
			local v = val -band- 0xFF
			CPU_REGS[reg+1] = (v >= 0x80) and (v + 0xFF00) or v
		elseif op2 == 0xBF then -- MOVSX r16, r/m16 (same as MOV r16, r/m16 in 16-bit mode)
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)

		-- ── 추가 0x0F opcodes ─────────────────────────────────────
		elseif op2 == 0xA2 then -- CPUID
			-- Pentium (P54C): family=5, model=2, stepping=12 → EAX=0x00000524 (or 0x052C)
			-- GenuineIntel vendor string
			local eax = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1)
			if eax == 0 then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, 1)           -- max function = 1
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4, 0x756E6547)  -- EBX "Genu"
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0x49656E69)  -- EDX "ineI"
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0x6C65746E)  -- ECX "ntel"
			elseif eax == 1 then
				-- Pentium III Coppermine 650MHz (family=6, model=8, stepping=6)
				-- EAX = 0x00000686: family=6, model=8, stepping=6
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, 0x00000686)
				-- EBX: brand index=0, CLFLUSH=0, initial APIC ID=0
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4, 0x00000000)
				-- ECX: no SSE3/SSSE3/SSE4 (P3 has none of these)
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0x00000000)
				-- EDX feature flags (Pentium III Coppermine):
				-- bit0=FPU, bit1=VME, bit2=DE, bit3=PSE, bit4=TSC, bit5=MSR,
				-- bit6=PAE, bit7=MCE, bit8=CX8, bit9=APIC(stub), bit11=SEP,
				-- bit12=MTRR, bit13=PGE, bit14=MCA, bit15=CMOV, bit16=PAT,
				-- bit17=PSE36, bit23=MMX, bit24=FXSR, bit25=SSE
				-- = 0x0387F9FF
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0x0387F9FF)
			else
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4,0)
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xA3 then -- BT r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local base=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local bitpos=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (base -brshift- bitpos) -band- 1)

		elseif op2 == 0xAB then -- BTS r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local base=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local bitpos=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (base -brshift- bitpos) -band- 1)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -bor- (1-blshift-bitpos))

		elseif op2 == 0xB3 then -- BTR r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local base=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local bitpos=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (base -brshift- bitpos) -band- 1)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -band- (bnot-(1-blshift-bitpos)))

		elseif op2 == 0xBB then -- BTC r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local base=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local bitpos=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (base -brshift- bitpos) -band- 1)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -bxor- (1-blshift-bitpos))

		elseif op2 == 0xBA then -- GRP8: BT/BTS/BTR/BTC r/m16, imm8
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local v=mrm.src -band- 0x07
			local base=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local bitpos=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -band- 0xF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (base -brshift- bitpos) -band- 1)
			if v==5 then -- BTS
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -bor- (1-blshift-bitpos))
			elseif v==6 then -- BTR
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -band- (bnot-(1-blshift-bitpos)))
			elseif v==7 then -- BTC
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, base -bxor- (1-blshift-bitpos))
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xBC then -- BSF r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src) -band- 0xFFFF
			if src == 0 then
				cpu_write_flag(6, true)
			else
				cpu_write_flag(6, false)
				local i=0; while i<16 and ((src -brshift- i) -band- 1)==0 do i=i+1 end
				CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=i
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xBD then -- BSR r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src) -band- 0xFFFF
			if src == 0 then
				cpu_write_flag(6, true)
			else
				cpu_write_flag(6, false)
				local i=15; while i>0 and ((src -brshift- i) -band- 1)==0 do i=i-1 end
				CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=i
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xA4 then -- SHLD r/m16, r16, imm8
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local cnt=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -band- 0x1F
			if cnt > 0 then
				local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
				local combined=(dst -blshift- 16) -bor- src
				local result=(combined -brshift- (16-cnt)) -band- 0xFFFF
				cpu_write_flag(0, (dst -brshift- (16-cnt)) -band- 1)
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,result)
				_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(result, 1)
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xA5 then -- SHLD r/m16, r16, CL
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local cnt=CPU_REGS[2] -band- 0x1F
			if cnt > 0 then
				local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
				local combined=(dst -blshift- 16) -bor- src
				local result=(combined -brshift- (16-cnt)) -band- 0xFFFF
				cpu_write_flag(0, (dst -brshift- (16-cnt)) -band- 1)
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,result)
				_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(result, 1)
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xAC then -- SHRD r/m16, r16, imm8
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local cnt=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -band- 0x1F
			if cnt > 0 then
				local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
				if cnt >= 16 then
					-- Intel: count >= operand_size → result undefined, use 0; CF = bit from src
					local combined=(src -blshift- 16) -bor- dst
					cpu_write_flag(0, (combined -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1)
					_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, 0)
					_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(0, 1)
				else
					local combined=(src -blshift- 16) -bor- dst
					local result=(combined -brshift- cnt) -band- 0xFFFF
					cpu_write_flag(0, (combined -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1)
					_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,result)
					_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(result, 1)
				end
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xAD then -- SHRD r/m16, r16, CL
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local cnt=CPU_REGS[2] -band- 0x1F
			if cnt > 0 then
				local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
				if cnt >= 16 then
					local combined=(src -blshift- 16) -bor- dst
					cpu_write_flag(0, (combined -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1)
					_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, 0)
					_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(0, 1)
				else
					local combined=(src -blshift- 16) -bor- dst
					local result=(combined -brshift- cnt) -band- 0xFFFF
					cpu_write_flag(0, (combined -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1)
					_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,result)
					_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(result, 1)
				end
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xC0 then -- XADD r/m8, r8
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(2) -- w=0, d=0
			local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFF
			local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src) -band- 0xFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.src, dst)  -- old dst → src reg
			local sum=(dst+src) -band- 0xFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, sum)
			_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(sum, 0)
			_cpu_uf_co_add(dst,src,0,dst+src,0)

		elseif op2 == 0xC1 then -- XADD r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3) -- w=1, d=1 (reverse for XADD: dst=r/m, src=reg)
			-- Actually XADD: modrm.reg = source, modrm.r/m = dest
			local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
			local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
			CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] = dst  -- old dst → src reg
			local sum=(dst+src) -band- 0xFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, sum)
			_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(sum, 1)
			_cpu_uf_co_add(dst,src,0,dst+src,1)

		elseif op2 == 0xB0 then -- CMPXCHG r/m8, r8
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(2)
			local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFF
			local acc=CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF  -- AL
			local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src) -band- 0xFF
			local diff=(acc-dst) -band- 0xFF
			_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(diff, 0)
			_cpu_uf_co_sub(dst,acc,0,diff,0)
			if acc == dst then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, src)
			else
				CPU_REGS[1]=(CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- dst
			end

		elseif op2 == 0xB1 then -- CMPXCHG r/m16, r16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
			local acc=CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFFFF  -- AX
			local src=CPU_REGS[mrm.src+1] -band- 0xFFFF
			local diff=(acc-dst) -band- 0xFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(diff, 1)
			_cpu_uf_co_sub(dst,acc,0,diff,1)
			if acc == dst then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst, src)
			else
				CPU_REGS[1]=dst
			end

		elseif op2 >= 0xC8 and op2 <= 0xCF then -- BSWAP r32
			-- In 16-bit mode this is effectively a NOP (or clears high 16)
			-- Just zero-extend: swap bytes of 16-bit register
			local r=(op2-0xC8)+1
			local v=CPU_REGS[r]
			CPU_REGS[r]=((v -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF) -bor- ((v -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8)

		elseif op2 == 0x96 then -- SETBE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(cpu_flag(0) or cpu_flag(6)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x97 then -- SETA
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(0) and not cpu_flag(6)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x98 then -- SETS
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,cpu_flag(7) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x99 then -- SETNS
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(7)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9A then -- SETP
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,cpu_flag(2) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9B then -- SETNP
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(2)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9C then -- SETL
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9D then -- SETGE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9E then -- SETLE
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(cpu_flag(6) or cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)) and 1 or 0)
		elseif op2 == 0x9F then -- SETG
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,(not cpu_flag(6) and cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)) and 1 or 0)

		elseif op2 == 0x31 then -- RDTSC
			-- Return a simple tick-based counter in EDX:EAX
			local t = math.floor(tick() * 1193182) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, t -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0)

		elseif op2 == 0xB2 then -- LSS r16, m16:16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3) -- d=1: dst=reg, src=r/m(mem)
			local addr=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local defseg=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local physaddr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4)+addr
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1] = RAM:r16(physaddr)
			CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = RAM:r16(physaddr+2)   -- SS

		elseif op2 == 0xB4 then -- LFS r16, m16:16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local addr=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local defseg=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local physaddr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4)+addr
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1] = RAM:r16(physaddr)
			CPU_SEGMENTS[5] = RAM:r16(physaddr+2)   -- FS

		elseif op2 == 0xB5 then -- LGS r16, m16:16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			local addr=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local defseg=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.src)
			local physaddr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4)+addr
			CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1] = RAM:r16(physaddr)
			CPU_SEGMENTS[6] = RAM:r16(physaddr+2)   -- GS

		elseif op2 == 0x00 then -- GRP6: SLDT/STR/LLDT/LTR/VERR/VERW
			local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local v = mrm.src -band- 7
			if v == 0 then -- SLDT
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, 0)  -- stub: return null selector
			elseif v == 1 then -- STR: store TR selector
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, tr_sel)
			elseif v == 2 then -- LLDT: load LDT (stub, ignore)
			elseif v == 3 then -- LTR: load Task Register
				local sel = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst) -band- 0xFFFF
				load_tss(sel)
				-- Mark TSS descriptor as busy (bit 1 of access byte) — stub
			elseif v == 4 or v == 5 then -- VERR/VERW: stub, always succeed (ZF=1)
				cpu_write_flag(6, true)
			end

		elseif op2 == 0x02 then -- LAR r16, r/m16 (stub - always succeed)
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			cpu_write_flag(6, true) -- ZF=1 = success

		elseif op2 == 0x03 then -- LSL r16, r/m16 (stub - always succeed)
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
			cpu_write_flag(6, true)

		elseif op2 == 0x30 then -- WRMSR
			local ecx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)
			cpu_msr[ecx] = {lo=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1), hi=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3)}

		elseif op2 == 0x32 then -- RDMSR
			local ecx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)
			if ecx == 0x10 then -- TSC MSR
				local t = math.floor(tick() * 1193182) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, t); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0)
			else
				local m = cpu_msr[ecx]
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, m and m.lo or 0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, m and m.hi or 0)
			end

		-- CMOVcc: Conditional Move (0x0F 40-4F) — 16-bit version
		-- Available on Pentium Pro+, but stub-present for P5 compat layer
		elseif op2 == 0x40 then -- CMOVO r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x41 then -- CMOVNO r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x42 then -- CMOVB/CMOVNAE r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(0) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x43 then -- CMOVNB/CMOVAE r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(0) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x44 then -- CMOVE/CMOVZ r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(6) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x45 then -- CMOVNE/CMOVNZ r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(6) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x46 then -- CMOVBE/CMOVNA r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(0) or cpu_flag(6) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x47 then -- CMOVNBE/CMOVA r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(0) and not cpu_flag(6) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x48 then -- CMOVS r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(7) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x49 then -- CMOVNS r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(7) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4A then -- CMOVP r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(2) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4B then -- CMOVNP r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(2) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4C then -- CMOVL r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4D then -- CMOVNL/CMOVGE r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4E then -- CMOVLE r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if cpu_flag(6) or cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end
		elseif op2 == 0x4F then -- CMOVNLE/CMOVG r16, r/m16
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3); if not cpu_flag(6) and cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11) then CPU_REGS[mrm.dst+1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.src)-band-0xFFFF end

		elseif op2 == 0xC7 then -- CMPXCHG8B m64 (Pentium)
			-- Compares EDX:EAX with 64-bit mem, if equal store ECX:EBX → mem, else load mem → EDX:EAX
			local mrm=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
			local addr_lo=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local seg=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
			local physaddr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (seg+1))]-blshift-4)+addr_lo
			local mem_lo=RAM:r16(physaddr) -bor- (RAM:r16(physaddr+2)-blshift-16)
			local mem_hi=RAM:r16(physaddr+4) -bor- (RAM:r16(physaddr+6)-blshift-16)
			local eax_v=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local edx_v=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)
			if mem_lo==eax_v and mem_hi==edx_v then
				-- Store ECX:EBX
				_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physaddr,   _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(4))  -- EBX
				_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physaddr+4, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2))  -- ECX? No: ECX:EBX means ECX=high, EBX=low
				-- Correct: EDX:EAX compared, ECX:EBX stored (ECX=high 32, EBX=low 32)
				_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physaddr,   _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(4))  -- EBX → low
				_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physaddr+4, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2))  -- ECX → high (wait, reg index: AX=1,CX=2,DX=3,BX=4)
				cpu_write_flag(6, true)
			else
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, mem_lo)   -- EAX ← low
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, mem_hi)   -- EDX ← high (DX=reg[3])
				cpu_write_flag(6, false)
			end

		elseif op2 == 0x18 then -- PREFETCHh (hint, stub)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0) -- consume modrm

		elseif op2 == 0x0D then -- PREFETCH (AMD 3DNow! hint, stub)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0)

		elseif op2 == 0xAE then -- FXSAVE/FXRSTOR/SFENCE/MFENCE/LFENCE (stub)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0) -- consume modrm

		elseif (op2 >= 0x10 and op2 <= 0x17) or (op2 >= 0x28 and op2 <= 0x2F)
		    or (op2 >= 0x50 and op2 <= 0x7F)
		    or (op2 >= 0xC2 and op2 <= 0xC6)
		    or (op2 >= 0xD0 and op2 <= 0xFE) then
			-- SSE/MMX stub: consume ModRM+disp+optional imm8
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
			local rm  = mb -band- 7
			if mod ~= 3 then
				if mod == 1 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
				elseif mod == 2 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
				elseif mod == 0 and rm == 6 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
			end
			if op2==0xC2 or op2==0xC4 or op2==0xC5 or op2==0xC6
			or op2==0x70 or op2==0x71 or op2==0x72 or op2==0x73 then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			end
		else
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[!] Unknown 0F opcode: %02X at CS=%04X IP=%04X", op2, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], (CPU_IP-2)-band-0xFFFF))
		end
	end
end

-- ADC
opcode_map[0x10] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_add(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode, true) end
for i=0x11,0x15 do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x10] end

-- PUSH/POP SS
opcode_map[0x16] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[3]) end
opcode_map[0x17] = function(opcode) if _G._pmode_set_seg then _G._pmode_set_seg(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(),3) else local v=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(); cpu_seg_sel[3]=v; CPU_SEGMENTS[3]=v end end

-- SBB
opcode_map[0x18] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_sub(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode, true) end
for i=0x19,0x1D do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x18] end

-- PUSH/POP DS
opcode_map[0x1E] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[4]) end
opcode_map[0x1F] = function(opcode) if _G._pmode_set_seg then _G._pmode_set_seg(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(),4) else local v=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16(); cpu_seg_sel[4]=v; CPU_SEGMENTS[4]=v end end

-- AND
opcode_map[0x20] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_and(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode) end
for i=0x21,0x25 do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x20] end

-- ES:
opcode_map[0x26] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 1
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- DAA
opcode_map[0x27] = function(opcode)
	local al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	local old_al = al
	local old_cf = ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(0))) ~= 0)
	if ((old_al -band- 0x0F) > 0x9) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(4))) ~= 0) then
		al = al + 0x6
		cpu_write_flag(0, old_cf or (al > 0xFF))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (4))
	else
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (4)))
	end
	if (old_al > 0x99) or old_cf then
		al = al + 0x60
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (0))
	end
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (al -band- 0xFF)
	_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(al, 0)
end

-- SUB
opcode_map[0x28] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_sub(mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]((opcode)), opcode) end
for i=0x29,0x2D do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x28] end

-- CS:
opcode_map[0x2E] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 2
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- DAS
opcode_map[0x2F] = function(opcode)
	local al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	local old_al = al
	local old_cf = ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(0))) ~= 0)
	if ((al -band- 0x0F) > 0x9) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(4))) ~= 0) then
		al = al - 0x6
		cpu_write_flag(0, old_cf or (al < 0))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (4))
	else
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (4)))
	end
	if ((al) > 0x99) or old_cf then
		al = al - 0x60
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (0))
	else
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (0)))
	end
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (al -band- 0xFF)
	_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(al, 0)
end

-- XOR
opcode_map[0x30] = function(opcode)
	local mrm_fn = mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]
	if mrm_fn then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_xor(mrm_fn((opcode)), opcode) end
end
for i=0x31,0x35 do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x30] end

-- SS:
opcode_map[0x36] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 3
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- AAA
opcode_map[0x37] = function(opcode)
	local al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	if ((al -band- 0x0F) >= 0x9) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(4))) ~= 0) then
		CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] + 0x106) -band- 0xFFFF
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (0))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (4))
	else
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (0)))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (4)))
	end
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF0F)
end

-- CMP
opcode_map[0x38] = function(opcode)
	local mrm_fn = mrm6_table[((opcode) -band- 0x7)]
	if mrm_fn then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_cmp_mrm(mrm_fn((opcode)), opcode) end
end
for i=0x39,0x3D do opcode_map[i] = opcode_map[0x38] end

-- DS:
opcode_map[0x3E] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 4
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- BOUND r16, m16&16 (0x62) — stub: ignore (real mode, no fault)
opcode_map[0x62] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3) end

-- ARPL (0x63) — only meaningful in protected mode, stub
opcode_map[0x63] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1) end

-- FS: segment prefix (0x64)
opcode_map[0x64] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 5
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- GS: segment prefix (0x65)
opcode_map[0x65] = function(opcode)
	CPU_SEGMOD = 6
	local r = run_one(true, true)
	CPU_SEGMOD = nil
	return r
end

-- AAS
opcode_map[0x3F] = function(opcode)
	local al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	if ((al -band- 0x0F) >= 0x9) or ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(4))) ~= 0) then
		CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] - 0x006) -band- 0xFFFF
		local ah = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -brshift- 8
		ah = (ah - 1) -band- 0xFF
		CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (ah -blshift- 8)
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (0))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (4))
	else
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (0)))
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (4)))
	end
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF0F)
end

-- INC

opcode_map[(0x40)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(1)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(1)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x41)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(2)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(2)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x42)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(3)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(3)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x43)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(4)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(4)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x44)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(5)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(5)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x45)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(6)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(6)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x46)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(7)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(7)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x47)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(8)]; v = (v + 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(8)] = v; _cpu_uf_inc(v, 1) end

-- DEC

opcode_map[(0x48)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(1)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(1)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x49)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(2)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(2)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4A)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(3)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(3)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4B)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(4)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(4)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4C)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(5)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(5)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4D)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(6)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(6)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4E)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(7)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(7)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end
opcode_map[(0x4F)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(8)]; v = (v - 1) -band- 0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[(8)] = v; _cpu_uf_dec(v, 1) end

-- PUSH/POP
opcode_map[0x50] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[1]) end
opcode_map[0x51] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[2]) end
opcode_map[0x52] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[3]) end
opcode_map[0x53] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[4]) end
opcode_map[0x54] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[5]) end
opcode_map[0x55] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[6]) end
opcode_map[0x56] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[7]) end
opcode_map[0x57] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[8]) end
opcode_map[0x58] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[1] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x59] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[2] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5A] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[3] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5B] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[4] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5C] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[5] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5D] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5E] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[7] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end
opcode_map[0x5F] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[8] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() end

if cpu_arch == "8086" or cpu_arch == "80186" then
	-- PUSH SP (8086/80186 bug reproduction)
	opcode_map[0x54] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[5] - 2) end
end

-- JMP
for i=0x70,0x7F do
	local cond = rel_jmp_conds[i - 0x6F]
	opcode_map[i] = function(opcode)
		local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		if cond() then
			CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(offset)) -band- ip_mask
		end
	end
end

if cpu_arch == "8086" then
	for i=0,15 do
		opcode_map[0x60 + i] = opcode_map[0x70 + i]
	end
else
	-- 80186+ opcodes
	-- TODO: IMUL(69/6B), BOUND

	-- PUSHA
	opcode_map[0x60] = function(opcode)
		local tmp = CPU_REGS[5]
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[1])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[2])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[3])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[4])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(tmp)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[6])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[7])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[8])
	end

	-- POPA
	opcode_map[0x61] = function(opcode)
		CPU_REGS[8] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[7] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[4] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[3] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[2] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		CPU_REGS[1] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
	end

	-- PUSH imm16/imm8
	opcode_map[0x68] = function(opcode)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16())
	end
	opcode_map[0x6A] = function(opcode)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	end

	-- ENTER (TESTME)
	opcode_map[0xC8] = function(opcode)
		local nb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
		local level = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -band- 0x1F
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[6])
		local frame_ptr = CPU_REGS[5]
		if level > 0 then
			for i=1,level-1 do
				CPU_REGS[6] = CPU_REGS[6] - 2
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_REGS[6])
			end
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(frame_ptr)
		end
		CPU_REGS[6] = frame_ptr
		CPU_REGS[5] = CPU_REGS[5] - nb
	end

	-- LEAVE
	opcode_map[0xC9] = function(opcode)
		CPU_REGS[5] = CPU_REGS[6]
		CPU_REGS[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
	end

	opcode_map[0xA4] = function(opcode)
		local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
		local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
		RAM[addrDst] = RAM[addrSrc]
		cpu_incdec_dir(7, 1)
		cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
	end
	opcode_map[0xA5] = function(opcode)
		local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
		local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
		RAM:w16(addrDst, RAM:r16(addrSrc))
		cpu_incdec_dir(7, 2)
		cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
	end

	-- INS Ib
	opcode_map[0x6C] = function(opcode)
		local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
		RAM[addrDst] = cpu_in(CPU_REGS[3]) -band- 0xFF
		cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
	end

	-- INS Iw
	opcode_map[0x6D] = function(opcode)
		local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
		RAM:w16(addrDst, cpu_in(CPU_REGS[3]) -band- 0xFFFF)
		cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
	end

	-- OUTS Ib
	opcode_map[0x6E] = function(opcode)
		local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
		cpu_out(CPU_REGS[3], RAM[addrSrc])
		cpu_incdec_dir(7, 1)
	end

	-- OUTS Iw
	opcode_map[0x6F] = function(opcode)
		local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
		cpu_out(CPU_REGS[3], RAM:r16(addrSrc))
		cpu_incdec_dir(7, 2)
	end

end -- (80186+ opcodes)

-- 0x66: Operand-Size prefix (32-bit operand mode)
-- opcode_map32 contains 32-bit versions of select opcodes.
-- For opcodes not in opcode_map32, falls back to CPU_OPSIZE=true + opcode_map[op].
if cpu_arch ~= "8086" and cpu_arch ~= "80186" then

	-- helper: modrm decode for 32-bit operands (uses cpu_mod_rm but r/w via cpu_get32/cpu_set32)
	-- We reuse cpu_read_rm / cpu_write_rm but intercept reg-only writes.
	-- For simplicity: decode modrm normally; for register operands use cpu_get32/cpu_set32;
	-- for memory operands use ram_r32/ram_w32.

	opcode_map32 = _G.EMU.MAP32

	-- PUSH r32 (0x50-0x57)
	for i=0,7 do
		opcode_map32[0x50+i] = function() cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(i+1)) end
	end
	-- POP r32 (0x58-0x5F)
	for i=0,7 do
		opcode_map32[0x58+i] = function() _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(i+1, cpu_pop32()) end
	end

	-- PUSH imm32 (0x68)
	opcode_map32[0x68] = function() cpu_push32(cpu_advance_ip32()) end
	-- PUSH imm8 sign-extended to 32 (0x6A)
	opcode_map32[0x6A] = function()
		local v=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
		cpu_push32(v -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
	end

	-- MOV r32, imm32 (0xB8-0xBF)
	for i=0,7 do
		opcode_map32[0xB8+i] = function() _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(i+1, cpu_advance_ip32()) end
	end

	-- ADD EAX, imm32 (0x05)
	opcode_map32[0x05] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local r=(a+v) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r)
		-- flags (approximate: carry and overflow)
		cpu_write_flag(0, r < a)
		cpu_write_flag(6, r==0)
		cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- OR EAX, imm32 (0x0D)
	opcode_map32[0x0D] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local r=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) -bor- v; r=r -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r)
		cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- AND EAX, imm32 (0x25)
	opcode_map32[0x25] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local r=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) -band- v; r=r -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r)
		cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- SUB EAX, imm32 (0x2D)
	opcode_map32[0x2D] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local r=(a-v) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r)
		cpu_write_flag(0, a < v)
		cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- XOR EAX, imm32 (0x35)
	opcode_map32[0x35] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local r=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) -bxor- v; r=r -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r)
		cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- CMP EAX, imm32 (0x3D)
	opcode_map32[0x3D] = function()
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32()
		local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local r=(a-v) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(0, a < v)
		cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
		cpu_write_flag(11, ((a -band- 0x80000000)~=(v -band- 0x80000000)) and ((r -band- 0x80000000)==(v -band- 0x80000000)))
	end

	-- helper: compute 32-bit r/m address (advances IP for disp, returns nil for reg)
	local function rm32_addr(modrm_byte)
		local rm  = modrm_byte -band- 7
		local mod = (modrm_byte -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		if mod == 3 then return nil, rm end
		local disp=0; local addr
		if ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF then
			-- 32-bit protected mode addressing (IA-32 ModRM with SIB)
			local seg = CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)] -blshift- 4
			if rm == 4 then
				-- SIB byte present
				local sib = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
				local scale = 1 -blshift- ((sib -brshift- 6) -band- 3)
				local index = (sib -brshift- 3) -band- 7
				local base  = sib -band- 7
				local base_v, index_v
				if mod == 0 and base == 5 then
					-- no base reg; read disp32
					disp = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
					base_v = 0
				else
					base_v = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(base+1)
					if mod == 1 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
					elseif mod == 2 then disp = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32()) end
				end
				index_v = (index == 4) and 0 or _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(index+1)
				if base == 4 or base == 5 then seg = CPU_SEGMENTS[3] -blshift- 4 end -- SS-based
				addr = seg + ((base_v + index_v * scale + disp) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			elseif mod == 0 and rm == 5 then
				-- [disp32] — no base register
				disp = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
				addr = seg + (disp -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			else
				if mod == 1 then disp = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
				elseif mod == 2 then disp = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32()) end
				local base_v = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(rm+1)
				if rm == 4 or rm == 5 then seg = CPU_SEGMENTS[3] -blshift- 4 end -- ESP/EBP → SS
				addr = seg + ((base_v + disp) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			end
		else
			-- 16-bit real-mode addressing
			if mod==0 and rm==6 then
				disp=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16(); addr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+disp
			else
				local bases={CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[7],CPU_REGS[4]+CPU_REGS[8],CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[7],CPU_REGS[6]+CPU_REGS[8],CPU_REGS[7],CPU_REGS[8],CPU_REGS[6],CPU_REGS[4]}
				local segs={4,4,3,3,4,4,3,4}
				if mod==1 then disp=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
				elseif mod==2 then disp=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()) end
				addr=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or segs[rm+1])]-blshift-4)+((bases[rm+1]+disp)-band-0xFFFF)
			end
		end
		return addr, rm
	end

	-- helper: read 32-bit r/m operand — returns val, reg, mod, rm, addr
	local function read_rm32(modrm_byte)
		local rm  = modrm_byte -band- 7
		local mod = (modrm_byte -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		local reg = (modrm_byte -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, addr
		if mod == 3 then
			val = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(rm+1)
		else
			addr, _ = rm32_addr(modrm_byte)
			val = _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(addr)
		end
		return val, reg, mod, rm, addr
	end

	-- helper: write 32-bit r/m — takes pre-computed addr (nil = register rm)
	local function write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, val)
		if addr == nil then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(rm+1, val)
		else _G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(addr, val) end
	end

	local function write_rm32(modrm_byte, val)
		local rm  = modrm_byte -band- 7
		local mod = (modrm_byte -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		if mod == 3 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(rm+1, val)
		else
			local addr = rm32_addr(modrm_byte)
			_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(addr, val)
		end
	end

	-- MOV r/m32, r32 (0x89) — uses rm32_addr for correct 32-bit pmode addressing
	opcode_map32[0x89] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local reg=(mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local mod=(mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		if mod==3 then
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32((mb -band- 7)+1, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1))
		else
			local addr, _ = rm32_addr(mb)
			_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(addr, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1))
		end
	end

	-- MOV r32, r/m32 (0x8B)
	opcode_map32[0x8B] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local reg=(mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val=read_rm32(mb)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, val)
	end

	-- MOV r/m32, imm32 (0xC7 /0)
	opcode_map32[0xC7] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local rm=mb -band- 7; local mod=(mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		-- compute address first, then read imm32
		local addr, rm2 = rm32_addr(mb)
		local imm=cpu_advance_ip32()
		write_rm32_addr(rm2, addr, imm)
	end

	-- GRP1 r/m32, imm32 (0x81)
	opcode_map32[0x81] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op=(mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		local imm=cpu_advance_ip32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		local result
		if op==0 then result=(val+imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,result<val)
		elseif op==1 then result=(val -bor- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==2 then local c=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0; result=(val+imm+c)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,result<val)
		elseif op==3 then local b=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0; result=(val-imm-b)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,val<imm)
		elseif op==4 then result=(val -band- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==5 then result=(val-imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,val<imm)
		elseif op==6 then result=(val -bxor- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==7 then result=(val-imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,val<imm); cpu_write_flag(6,result==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(result-band-0x80000000)~=0); return
		end
		if op~=7 then write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, result) end
		cpu_write_flag(6,result==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(result-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end

	-- GRP1 r/m32, imm8 sign-extended (0x83)
	opcode_map32[0x83] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op=(mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		local imm=_G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		local result
		if op==0 then result=(val+imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,result<val)
		elseif op==1 then result=(val -bor- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==4 then result=(val -band- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==5 then result=(val-imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,val<(imm-band-0xFFFFFFFF))
		elseif op==6 then result=(val -bxor- imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		elseif op==7 then result=(val-imm)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,val<(imm-band-0xFFFFFFFF)); cpu_write_flag(6,result==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(result-band-0x80000000)~=0); return
		else result=val end
		write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, result)
		cpu_write_flag(6,result==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(result-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end

	-- helper macro: r/m32 OP r32 (writes back to r/m32)
	local function op32_rm_r(mb, fn_r)
		local reg=(mb-brshift-3)-band-7; local rm=mb-band-7; local mod=(mb-brshift-6)-band-3
		local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1); local dst, _, _, rm2, addr
		if mod==3 then dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(rm+1); rm2=rm; addr=nil else dst,_,_,rm2,addr=read_rm32(mb) end
		local r=fn_r(dst,src); write_rm32_addr(rm2, addr, r); return r
	end
	-- helper macro: r32 OP r/m32 (writes back to reg)
	local function op32_r_rm(mb, fn_r)
		local reg=(mb-brshift-3)-band-7
		local src=read_rm32(mb); local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1)
		local r=fn_r(dst,src); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1,r); return r
	end

	-- ADD r/m32, r32 (0x01)  and  ADD r32, r/m32 (0x03)
	opcode_map32[0x01] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d+s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x03] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d+s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- SUB r/m32, r32 (0x29)  and  SUB r32, r/m32 (0x2B)
	opcode_map32[0x29] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local _d, _s
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) _d,_s=d,s; return (d-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(0, _d < _s)  -- CF: borrow
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
		-- OF: signed overflow in subtraction (_d - _s)
		cpu_write_flag(11,((_d-band-0x80000000)~=(_s-band-0x80000000)) and ((r-band-0x80000000)~=(_d-band-0x80000000)))
	end
	opcode_map32[0x2B] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- XOR r/m32, r32 (0x31)  and  XOR r32, r/m32 (0x33)
	opcode_map32[0x31] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d-bxor-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x33] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d-bxor-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- AND r/m32, r32 (0x21)  and  AND r32, r/m32 (0x23)
	opcode_map32[0x21] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d-band-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x23] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d-band-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- OR r/m32, r32 (0x09)  and  OR r32, r/m32 (0x0B)
	opcode_map32[0x09] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d-bor-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x0B] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); cpu_write_flag(0,false); cpu_write_flag(11,false)
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d-bor-s)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- CMP r/m32, r32 (0x39)  and  CMP r32, r/m32 (0x3B)
	opcode_map32[0x39] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local reg=(mb-brshift-3)-band-7; local rm=mb-band-7; local mod=(mb-brshift-6)-band-3
		local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1); local dst
		if mod==3 then dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(rm+1) else dst=(read_rm32(mb)) end
		local r=(dst-src)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,dst<src); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
		-- OF: signed overflow in subtraction (dst - src)
		cpu_write_flag(11,((dst-band-0x80000000)~=(src-band-0x80000000)) and ((r-band-0x80000000)~=(dst-band-0x80000000)))
	end
	opcode_map32[0x3B] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local reg=(mb-brshift-3)-band-7
		local src=read_rm32(mb); local dst=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1)
		local r=(dst-src)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; cpu_write_flag(0,dst<src); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
		-- OF: signed overflow in subtraction (dst - src)
		cpu_write_flag(11,((dst-band-0x80000000)~=(src-band-0x80000000)) and ((r-band-0x80000000)~=(dst-band-0x80000000)))
	end

	-- ADC/SBB EAX, imm32
	opcode_map32[0x15] = function() -- ADC EAX, imm32
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32(); local c=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local r=(a+v+c)-band-0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r); cpu_write_flag(0,r<a); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x1D] = function() -- SBB EAX, imm32
		local v=cpu_advance_ip32(); local b=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local r=(a-v-b)-band-0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,r); cpu_write_flag(0,a<v); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- ADC r/m32,r32 (0x11) / r32,r/m32 (0x13)
	opcode_map32[0x11] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local c=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d+s+c)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x13] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local c=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d+s+c)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	-- SBB r/m32,r32 (0x19) / r32,r/m32 (0x1B)
	opcode_map32[0x19] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local b=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local r=op32_rm_r(mb, function(d,s) return (d-s-b)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x1B] = function()
		local mb=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(); local b=cpu_flag(0) and 1 or 0
		local r=op32_r_rm(mb, function(d,s) return (d-s-b)-band-0xFFFFFFFF end)
		cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
	end

	-- INC/DEC r32 (0x40-0x47 / 0x48-0x4F)
	for i=0,7 do
		opcode_map32[0x40+i] = function() local r=i+1; local v=(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(r)+1)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(r,v); cpu_write_flag(6,v==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(v-band-0x80000000)~=0) end
		opcode_map32[0x48+i] = function() local r=i+1; local v=(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(r)-1)-band-0xFFFFFFFF; _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(r,v); cpu_write_flag(6,v==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(v-band-0x80000000)~=0) end
	end

	-- XCHG EAX, r32 (0x91-0x97)
	for i=1,7 do
		opcode_map32[0x90+i] = function()
			local a=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local b=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(i+1)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,b); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(i+1,a)
		end
	end

	-- PUSHFD (0x66 9C): push 32-bit EFLAGS onto stack
	opcode_map32[0x9C] = function()
		local eflags = (CPU_EFLAGS_HI -blshift- 16) -bor- (CPU_FLAGS -band- 0xFFFF)
		cpu_push32(eflags)
	end
	-- POPFD (0x66 9D): pop 32-bit EFLAGS from stack
	opcode_map32[0x9D] = function()
		local eflags = cpu_pop32()
		CPU_FLAGS = (eflags -band- 0xFFFF) -bor- 0x0002  -- bit1 always 1
		CPU_EFLAGS_HI = (eflags -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFFFF
	end

	-- PUSHA/POPA 32-bit (0x60/0x61) with CPU_OPSIZE
	opcode_map32[0x60] = function()
		local tmp=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(5)
		cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1)); cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)); cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3)); cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(4))
		cpu_push32(tmp)
		cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(6)); cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7)); cpu_push32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8))
	end
	opcode_map32[0x61] = function()
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,cpu_pop32()); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,cpu_pop32()); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(6,cpu_pop32())
		cpu_pop32() -- discard ESP
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4,cpu_pop32()); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3,cpu_pop32()); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2,cpu_pop32()); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,cpu_pop32())
	end

	-- MOVSD (0xA5) — 32-bit string move (uses ESI/EDI in 32-bit pmode)
	opcode_map32[0xA5] = function()
		local esi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7) or CPU_REGS[7]
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local src=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+esi
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(dst, _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(src))
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -4 or 4
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,(esi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[7]=(esi+d)-band-0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- STOSD (0xAB) — store EAX to [EDI]
	opcode_map32[0xAB] = function()
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1))
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -4 or 4
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- LODSD (0xAD) — load [ESI] into EAX
	opcode_map32[0xAD] = function()
		local esi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7) or CPU_REGS[7]
		local src=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+esi
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(src))
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -4 or 4
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,(esi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[7]=(esi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- SCASD (0xAF) — compare EAX with [EDI]
	opcode_map32[0xAF] = function()
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		local src=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1)
		local v=_G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(dst)
		local r=(src-v)-band-0xFFFFFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(0,src<v); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -4 or 4
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- CMPSD (0xA7) — compare [ESI] with [EDI]
	opcode_map32[0xA7] = function()
		local esi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7) or CPU_REGS[7]
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local src=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+esi
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		local sv=_G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(src); local dv=_G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(dst)
		local r=(sv-dv)-band-0xFFFFFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(0,sv<dv); cpu_write_flag(6,r==0); cpu_write_flag(7,(r-band-0x80000000)~=0)
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -4 or 4
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,(esi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[7]=(esi+d)-band-0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end

	-- MOVSB 32-bit (0xA4) — ESI/EDI aware
	opcode_map32[0xA4] = function()
		local esi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7) or CPU_REGS[7]
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local src=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+esi
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		RAM[dst] = RAM[src]
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -1 or 1
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,(esi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[7]=(esi+d)-band-0xFFFF; CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- STOSB 32-bit (0xAA) — store AL to [EDI], advance EDI
	opcode_map32[0xAA] = function()
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		RAM[dst] = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -1 or 1
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- LODSB 32-bit (0xAC) — load [ESI] into AL, advance ESI
	opcode_map32[0xAC] = function()
		local esi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(7) or CPU_REGS[7]
		local src=(CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)]-blshift-4)+esi
		CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (RAM[src] or 0)
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -1 or 1
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(7,(esi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[7]=(esi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end
	-- MOVSW 32-bit (0xA5 already defined as MOVSD — add 0xA6 CMPSB)
	-- SCASB 32-bit (0xAE) — compare AL with [EDI]
	opcode_map32[0xAE] = function()
		local edi = ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(8) or CPU_REGS[8]
		local dst=(CPU_SEGMENTS[1]-blshift-4)+edi
		local v = RAM[dst] or 0
		local al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
		local r = (al - v) -band- 0xFF
		cpu_write_flag(0, al < v); cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80)~=0)
		local d = cpu_flag(10) and -1 or 1
		if ip_mask==0xFFFFFFFF then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(8,(edi+d)-band-0xFFFFFFFF)
		else CPU_REGS[8]=(edi+d)-band-0xFFFF end
	end

	-- 0x66 0x0F: 32-bit 2-byte opcodes
	opcode_map32[0x0F] = function()
		local op2 = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		if op2 == 0xAF then -- IMUL r32, r/m32
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local src = read_rm32(mb)
			local dst = to_s32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1))
			local s2  = to_s32(src)
			local full = dst * s2
			local r = full -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, r)
			local ov = to_s32(r) ~= full
			cpu_write_flag(0, ov); cpu_write_flag(11, ov)
		elseif op2 == 0xB6 then -- MOVZX r32, r/m8
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local rm  = mb -band- 7
			local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
			local val
			if mod == 3 then
				if rm < 4 then val = CPU_REGS[rm+1] -band- 0xFF
				else val = (CPU_REGS[(rm-4)+1] -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF end
			else
				local addr, _ = rm32_addr(mb)
				val=RAM[addr]
			end
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, val -band- 0xFF)
		elseif op2 == 0xB7 then -- MOVZX r32, r/m16
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
			local src
			if mod == 3 then
				src = CPU_REGS[(mb -band- 7)+1] -band- 0xFFFF
			else
				local addr, _ = rm32_addr(mb)
				src = (RAM[addr] or 0) -bor- ((RAM[addr+1] or 0) -blshift- 8)
			end
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, src -band- 0xFFFF)
		elseif op2 == 0xBE then -- MOVSX r32, r/m8
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local rm  = mb -band- 7
			local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
			local val
			if mod == 3 then
				if rm < 4 then val = CPU_REGS[rm+1] -band- 0xFF
				else val = (CPU_REGS[(rm-4)+1] -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF end
			else
				local addr, _ = rm32_addr(mb)
				val = RAM[addr]
			end
			local v = val -band- 0xFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, (v >= 0x80) and (v + 0xFFFFFF00) or v)
		elseif op2 == 0xBF then -- MOVSX r32, r/m16
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local src = read_rm32(mb) -band- 0xFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(src) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
		-- CMOVcc r32, r/m32 (0x40-0x4F) — 32-bit conditional move
		elseif op2 >= 0x40 and op2 <= 0x4F then
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
			local src = read_rm32(mb)
			local cc = op2 - 0x40
			local take = false
			if     cc==0  then take=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==1  then take=not cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==2  then take=cpu_flag(0)
			elseif cc==3  then take=not cpu_flag(0)
			elseif cc==4  then take=cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==5  then take=not cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==6  then take=cpu_flag(0) or cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==7  then take=not cpu_flag(0) and not cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==8  then take=cpu_flag(7)
			elseif cc==9  then take=not cpu_flag(7)
			elseif cc==10 then take=cpu_flag(2)
			elseif cc==11 then take=not cpu_flag(2)
			elseif cc==12 then take=cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==13 then take=cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==14 then take=cpu_flag(6) or cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==15 then take=not cpu_flag(6) and cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)
			end
			if take then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, src) end
		-- RDTSC 32-bit (0x31) — return tick-based TSC in EDX:EAX
		elseif op2 == 0x31 then
			local t = math.floor(tick() * 1193182) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, t); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0)  -- EAX=low, EDX=high(0)
		-- CPUID 32-bit (0xA2)
		elseif op2 == 0xA2 then
			local eax = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1)
			if eax == 0 then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, 1); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4, 0x756E6547); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0x49656E69); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0x6C65746E)
			elseif eax == 1 then
				-- Pentium III Coppermine (family=6, model=8, stepping=6)
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, 0x00000686); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4, 0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, 0x0387F9FF)
			else
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3,0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4,0)
			end
		-- WRMSR 32-bit (0x30)
		elseif op2 == 0x30 then
			local ecx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)
			cpu_msr[ecx] = {lo=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1), hi=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3)}
		-- RDMSR 32-bit (0x32)
		elseif op2 == 0x32 then
			local ecx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2)
			if ecx == 0x10 then
				local t = math.floor(tick() * 1193182) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, t); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, 0)
			else
				local m = cpu_msr[ecx]
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, m and m.lo or 0); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, m and m.hi or 0)
			end
		-- SYSENTER: fast system call entry (0x0F 34) — used by Linux 2.6+ kernels
		elseif op2 == 0x34 then
			local cs_sel = cpu_msr[0x174] and cpu_msr[0x174].lo or 0
			local esp_val = cpu_msr[0x175] and cpu_msr[0x175].lo or 0
			local eip_val = cpu_msr[0x176] and cpu_msr[0x176].lo or 0
			if cs_sel ~= 0 then
				pmode_set_seg(cs_sel -band- 0xFFFC, 2)       -- CS ring-0
				pmode_set_seg((cs_sel -band- 0xFFFC)+8, 3)   -- SS ring-0 (CS+8)
			end
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(5, esp_val)
			CPU_IP = eip_val -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- 0xFFFFF1FF  -- clear IF, VM, RF
		-- SYSEXIT: fast system call exit (0x0F 35)
		elseif op2 == 0x35 then
			local cs_sel = cpu_msr[0x174] and cpu_msr[0x174].lo or 0
			if cs_sel ~= 0 then
				pmode_set_seg((cs_sel -band- 0xFFFC)+16, 2)  -- CS user (CS+16)
				pmode_set_seg((cs_sel -band- 0xFFFC)+24, 3)  -- SS user (CS+24)
			end
			CPU_IP = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF  -- EDX → EIP
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(5, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2))               -- ECX → ESP
		elseif op2 >= 0x80 and op2 <= 0x8F then -- Jcc rel32
			local off = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
			local cc = op2 - 0x80
			local take = false
			if cc==0 then take=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==1 then take=not cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==2 then take=cpu_flag(0)
			elseif cc==3 then take=not cpu_flag(0)
			elseif cc==4 then take=cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==5 then take=not cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==6 then take=cpu_flag(0) or cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==7 then take=not cpu_flag(0) and not cpu_flag(6)
			elseif cc==8 then take=cpu_flag(7)
			elseif cc==9 then take=not cpu_flag(7)
			elseif cc==10 then take=cpu_flag(2)
			elseif cc==11 then take=not cpu_flag(2)
			elseif cc==12 then take=cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==13 then take=cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==14 then take=cpu_flag(6) or cpu_flag(7)~=cpu_flag(11)
			elseif cc==15 then take=not cpu_flag(6) and cpu_flag(7)==cpu_flag(11)
			end
			if take then CPU_IP=(CPU_IP+off)-band-ip_mask end
		-- SSE/MMX stubs: consume ModRM+SIB+disp so IP stays correct; no actual XMM state
		elseif (op2 >= 0x10 and op2 <= 0x17) or (op2 >= 0x28 and op2 <= 0x2F)
		    or (op2 >= 0x50 and op2 <= 0x7F) or (op2 >= 0x60 and op2 <= 0x77)
		    or op2 == 0x7E or op2 == 0x7F
		    or (op2 >= 0xC2 and op2 <= 0xC6)
		    or (op2 >= 0xD0 and op2 <= 0xFE) then
			-- consume ModRM byte
			local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
			local rm  = mb -band- 7
			if mod ~= 3 then
				if ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF then
					if rm == 4 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() end  -- SIB
					if mod == 1 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
					elseif mod == 2 then cpu_advance_ip32()
