					elseif mod == 0 and rm == 5 then cpu_advance_ip32() end
				else
					if mod == 1 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
					elseif mod == 2 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
					elseif mod == 0 and rm == 6 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
				end
			end
			-- ops with trailing imm8
			if op2==0xC2 or op2==0xC4 or op2==0xC5 or op2==0xC6
			or op2==0x70 or op2==0x71 or op2==0x72 or op2==0x73 then
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
			end
		else
			-- fallback to 16-bit 0x0F handler with CPU_OPSIZE
			CPU_OPSIZE = true
			local fn = opcode_map[0x0F]
			-- re-push op2 by adjusting IP back
			CPU_IP = (CPU_IP - 1) -band- ip_mask
			if fn then fn(0x0F) end
			CPU_OPSIZE = false
		end
	end

	-- GRP2 r/m32, imm8 (0xC1) — 32-bit shift/rotate by immediate
	opcode_map32[0xC1] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		local cnt = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -band- 0x1F
		if cnt == 0 then return end
		local r
		if op == 4 then -- SHL
			r = (val * (2^cnt)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val * (2^(cnt-1))) -band- 0x80000000 ~= 0)
		elseif op == 5 then -- SHR
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1 ~= 0)
			r = val -brshift- cnt
		elseif op == 7 then -- SAR
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1 ~= 0)
			local sv = to_s32(val)
			r = math.floor(sv / (2^cnt)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		elseif op == 0 then -- ROL
			local c = cnt -band- 31
			r = ((val -blshift- c) -bor- (val -brshift- (32-c))) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, r -band- 1 ~= 0)
		elseif op == 1 then -- ROR
			local c = cnt -band- 31
			r = ((val -brshift- c) -bor- (val -blshift- (32-c))) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (r -brshift- 31) -band- 1 ~= 0)
		else r = val end
		if r then
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(6, r == 0)
			cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0)
			cpu_write_flag(2, parity_table[r -band- 0xFF] ~= 0)
		end
	end

	-- GRP2 r/m32, 1 (0xD1) — 32-bit shift/rotate by 1
	opcode_map32[0xD1] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		local r
		if op == 4 then -- SHL 1
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val -brshift- 31) -band- 1 ~= 0)
			r = (val * 2) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		elseif op == 5 then -- SHR 1
			cpu_write_flag(0, val -band- 1 ~= 0)
			r = val -brshift- 1
		elseif op == 7 then -- SAR 1
			cpu_write_flag(0, val -band- 1 ~= 0)
			local sv = to_s32(val)
			r = math.floor(sv / 2) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		elseif op == 0 then -- ROL 1
			local msb = (val -brshift- 31) -band- 1
			r = ((val -blshift- 1) -bor- msb) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, r -band- 1 ~= 0)
		elseif op == 1 then -- ROR 1
			local lsb = val -band- 1
			r = ((val -brshift- 1) -bor- (lsb -blshift- 31)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (r -brshift- 31) -band- 1 ~= 0)
		else r = val end
		if r then
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(6, r == 0)
			cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0)
		end
	end

	-- GRP2 r/m32, CL (0xD3) — 32-bit shift/rotate by CL
	opcode_map32[0xD3] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local cnt = CPU_REGS[2] -band- 0x1F  -- CL & 31
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		if cnt == 0 then return end
		local r
		if op == 4 then -- SHL CL
			r = (val * (2^cnt)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val * (2^(cnt-1))) -band- 0x80000000 ~= 0)
		elseif op == 5 then -- SHR CL
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1 ~= 0)
			r = val -brshift- cnt
		elseif op == 7 then -- SAR CL
			cpu_write_flag(0, (val -brshift- (cnt-1)) -band- 1 ~= 0)
			local sv = to_s32(val)
			r = math.floor(sv / (2^cnt)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		else r = val end
		if r then
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(6, r == 0)
			cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0)
		end
	end

	-- TEST r/m32, r32 (0x85) — 32-bit AND without storing result
	opcode_map32[0x85] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val = read_rm32(mb)
		local src = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1)
		local r = (val -band- src) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(0, false); cpu_write_flag(11, false)
		cpu_write_flag(6, r == 0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0)
	end

	-- TEST EAX, imm32 (0xA9)
	opcode_map32[0xA9] = function()
		local imm = cpu_advance_ip32()
		local r = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) -band- imm) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(0, false); cpu_write_flag(11, false)
		cpu_write_flag(6, r == 0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000) ~= 0)
	end

	-- LEA r32, m (0x8D) — load effective address (32-bit result)
	opcode_map32[0x8D] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local rm  = mb -band- 7
		local mod = (mb -brshift- 6) -band- 3
		local addr, _ = rm32_addr(mb)
		if addr ~= nil then
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, addr -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
		end
	end

	-- XCHG r/m32, r32 (0x87)
	opcode_map32[0x87] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local reg = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		local src = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(reg+1)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(reg+1, val)
		write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, src)
	end

	-- CALL near rel32 (0xE8)
	opcode_map32[0xE8] = function()
		local rel = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
		cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + rel) -band- ip_mask
	end

	-- JMP near rel32 (0xE9)
	opcode_map32[0xE9] = function()
		local rel = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + rel) -band- ip_mask
	end

	-- Jcc rel32 (0x0F 80-8F handled in 0x0F section; here fallthrough to 16-bit)
	-- JMP short rel8 (0xEB) — same in both 16/32
	-- Conditional jumps rel32 via 0x66 prefix (0x66 0x0F 80-8F)
	-- handled via opcode_map32[0x0F] fallback

	-- REP with 32-bit operand (0x66 0xF3 or 0x66 0xF2)
	-- REP MOVSD, REP STOSD, REP LODSD etc.
	opcode_map32[0xF3] = function()
		-- REP: read next opcode, if it's a 32-bit string op handle it directly
		local old_ip = CPU_IP
		local str_op = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		-- Use ECX in 32-bit pmode, CX in 16-bit mode
		local use32cx = (ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF)
		local cx = use32cx and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2) or CPU_REGS[2]
		if cx == 0 then return end
		CPU_IP = old_ip
		local fn32 = opcode_map32[str_op]
		if fn32 then
			-- 32-bit string operation with REP
			local skipConds = str_op ~= 0xA7 and str_op ~= 0xAF
			cx = use32cx and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2) or CPU_REGS[2]
			while cx ~= 0 do
				CPU_IP = old_ip + 1  -- skip str_op byte
				fn32()
				cx = (cx - 1) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
				if use32cx then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, cx) else CPU_REGS[2] = cx -band- 0xFFFF end
				if cx == 0 then break end
				if not skipConds then
					local cont = (CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-6)) ~= 0
					if not cont then break end
				end
			end
		else
			-- fallback: set CPU_OPSIZE for 16-bit REP handler
			CPU_OPSIZE = true
			if not cpu_rep(function() return (CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-6)) ~= 0 end) then end
			CPU_OPSIZE = false
		end
	end
	opcode_map32[0xF2] = function()
		local old_ip = CPU_IP
		local str_op = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local use32cx = (ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF)
		local cx = use32cx and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2) or CPU_REGS[2]
		if cx == 0 then return end
		CPU_IP = old_ip
		local fn32 = opcode_map32[str_op]
		if fn32 then
			cx = use32cx and _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(2) or CPU_REGS[2]
			while cx ~= 0 do
				CPU_IP = old_ip + 1
				fn32()
				cx = (cx - 1) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
				if use32cx then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(2, cx) else CPU_REGS[2] = cx -band- 0xFFFF end
				if cx == 0 then break end
				local cont = not ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-6)) ~= 0)
				if not cont then break end
			end
		else
			CPU_OPSIZE = true
			if not cpu_rep(function() return not ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-6)) ~= 0) end) then end
			CPU_OPSIZE = false
		end
	end

	-- IMUL r32, r/m32 (0x0F 0xAF with CPU_OPSIZE)  — handled in 0x0F section via CPU_OPSIZE check

	-- CWDE (0x98 in 32-bit mode): sign-extend AX to EAX
	opcode_map32[0x98] = function()
		local ax = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, (ax >= 0x8000) and (ax -bor- 0xFFFF0000) or ax)
	end
	-- CDQ (0x99 in 32-bit mode): sign-extend EAX to EDX:EAX
	opcode_map32[0x99] = function()
		local eax = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, (eax >= 0x80000000) and 0xFFFFFFFF or 0)
	end

	-- LEAVE 32-bit (0xC9): MOV ESP,EBP; POP EBP
	opcode_map32[0xC9] = function()
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(5, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(6))  -- ESP = EBP
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(6, cpu_pop32())   -- EBP = pop32
	end

	-- IRETD (32-bit IRET with 0x66 prefix → opcode_map32[0xCF])
	opcode_map32[0xCF] = function()
		-- Pop 32-bit EIP, CS, EFLAGS
		local neweip = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		local newcs  = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFF
		CPU_FLAGS = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		pmode_set_seg(newcs, 2)
		CPU_IP = neweip
	end

	-- PUSHFD / POPFD (0x66 9C/9D): push/pop 32-bit EFLAGS
	opcode_map32[0x9C] = function()
		local ef32 = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (CPU_EFLAGS_HI -blshift- 16)
		cpu_push32(ef32)
	end
	opcode_map32[0x9D] = function()
		local ef32 = cpu_pop32()
		CPU_FLAGS = ef32 -band- 0xFFFF
		CPU_EFLAGS_HI = (ef32 -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFFFF
	end

	-- CALL near rel32 (0xE8) and JMP near rel32 (0xE9) — only if in 32-bit mode
	opcode_map32[0xE8] = function()
		local off = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
		cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + off) -band- ip_mask
	end
	opcode_map32[0xE9] = function()
		local off = to_s32(cpu_advance_ip32())
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + off) -band- ip_mask
	end

	-- RET near (0xC3) and RET near imm16 (0xC2) 32-bit versions
	opcode_map32[0xC3] = function() CPU_IP = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF end
	opcode_map32[0xC2] = function()
		local n = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
		CPU_IP = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(5, (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(5) + n) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
	end

	-- GRP5 32-bit (0xFF in 32-bit mode): INC/DEC/CALL/JMP/PUSH r/m32
	opcode_map32[0xFF] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local v = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		if v == 0 then -- INC r/m32
			local r = (val + 1) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
		elseif v == 1 then -- DEC r/m32
			local r = (val - 1) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
		elseif v == 2 then -- CALL near abs r/m32
			cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
			CPU_IP = val -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		elseif v == 3 then -- CALL far m16:32 (selector:offset32 at memory)
			if addr then
				local newIp = _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(addr)
				local newCs = (RAM[addr+4] or 0) -bor- ((RAM[addr+5] or 0) -blshift- 8)
				if pmode then
					cpu_push32(cpu_seg_sel[2]); cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
					pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
				else
					_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[2]); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_IP)
					cpu_seg_sel[2]=newCs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2]=newCs
				end
				CPU_IP = newIp
			end
		elseif v == 4 then -- JMP near abs r/m32
			CPU_IP = val -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		elseif v == 5 then -- JMP far m16:32
			if addr then
				local newIp = _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(addr)
				local newCs = (RAM[addr+4] or 0) -bor- ((RAM[addr+5] or 0) -blshift- 8)
				CPU_IP = newIp
				if pmode then pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
				else cpu_seg_sel[2]=newCs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2]=newCs end
			end
		elseif v == 6 then -- PUSH r/m32
			cpu_push32(val)
		end
	end

	-- MOV EAX, [moffs32] (0xA1) and MOV [moffs32], EAX (0xA3) — 32-bit direct memory
	opcode_map32[0xA1] = function()
		local addr = cpu_advance_ip32()
		local phys = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)] -blshift- 4) + addr
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, _G.EMU.CPU.ram_r32(phys))
	end
	opcode_map32[0xA3] = function()
		local addr = cpu_advance_ip32()
		local phys = (CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or 4)] -blshift- 4) + addr
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(phys, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1))
	end

	-- POP r/m32 (0x8F /0) — 32-bit version
	opcode_map32[0x8F] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local v = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		if v == 0 then
			-- compute dest address first (displacement consumed before pop)
			local _, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
			local val = cpu_pop32()
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, val)
		end
	end

	-- GRP3 32-bit (0xF7): TEST/NOT/NEG/MUL/IMUL/DIV/IDIV r/m32
	opcode_map32[0xF7] = function()
		local mb = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local op = (mb -brshift- 3) -band- 7
		local val, _, mod, rm, addr = read_rm32(mb)
		if op == 0 or op == 1 then -- TEST r/m32, imm32
			local imm = cpu_advance_ip32()
			local r = (val -band- imm) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
			cpu_write_flag(0, false); cpu_write_flag(11, false)
		elseif op == 2 then -- NOT r/m32
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, (bnot-(val)) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
		elseif op == 3 then -- NEG r/m32
			local r = (0 - val) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			write_rm32_addr(rm, addr, r)
			cpu_write_flag(0, val ~= 0); cpu_write_flag(6, r==0); cpu_write_flag(7, (r -band- 0x80000000)~=0)
		elseif op == 4 then -- MUL EAX, r/m32 → EDX:EAX
			local v = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) * val  -- may exceed 32 bits
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, v -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, math.floor(v / 0x100000000) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
			local ov = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3) ~= 0
			cpu_write_flag(0, ov); cpu_write_flag(11, ov)
		elseif op == 5 then -- IMUL EAX, r/m32 → EDX:EAX
			local sv = to_s32(val); local sa = to_s32(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1))
			local full = sv * sa
			local lo = full -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			local hi = math.floor(full / 0x100000000) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, lo); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, hi)
			local ov = to_s32(lo) ~= full
			cpu_write_flag(0, ov); cpu_write_flag(11, ov)
		elseif op == 6 then -- DIV EDX:EAX / r/m32
			if val == 0 then cpu_exception(0, -1) return end
			local dividend = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1) + _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3) * 0x100000000
			local q = math.floor(dividend / val) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
			local r = dividend - q * val
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, q); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, r -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
		elseif op == 7 then -- IDIV EDX:EAX / r/m32
			if val == 0 then cpu_exception(0, -1) return end
			local eax = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(1); local edx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(3)
			local dividend = to_s32(edx) * 0x100000000 + eax
			local divisor = to_s32(val)
			local q = math.floor(dividend / divisor)
			local r = dividend - q * divisor
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, q -band- 0xFFFFFFFF); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(3, r -band- 0xFFFFFFFF)
		end
	end

	opcode_map[0x66] = function(opcode)
		local next_op = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		if ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF then
			-- In 32-bit pmode: 0x66 selects 16-bit operand size override
			-- Run the 16-bit handler from opcode_map (its natural operand size)
			local fn16 = opcode_map[next_op]
			if fn16 then CPU_OPSIZE = false; fn16(next_op) end
		else
			-- In 16-bit mode: 0x66 selects 32-bit operand size override
			local fn32 = opcode_map32[next_op]
			if fn32 then
				fn32()
			else
				-- fallback: set CPU_OPSIZE and call 16-bit handler
				CPU_OPSIZE = true
				local fn = opcode_map[next_op]
				if fn then fn(next_op) end
				CPU_OPSIZE = false
			end
		end
	end

	-- 0x67: Address-Size prefix (stub — ignore, most real-mode code doesn't use it)
	opcode_map[0x67] = function(opcode)
		CPU_ADDRSIZE = true
		local next_op = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local fn = opcode_map[next_op]
		if fn then fn(next_op) end
		CPU_ADDRSIZE = false
	end

	-- 0x69: IMUL r16, r/m16, imm16  (r16=dest=dst, r/m=src)
	opcode_map[0x69] = function(opcode)
		local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)  -- d=1: dst=reg, src=r/m
		local imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
		local a = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.src))
		local b = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(imm)
		local full = a * b
		local r = full -band- 0xFFFF
		local overflow = full ~= _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(r)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, r)
		cpu_write_flag(0, overflow)
		cpu_write_flag(11, overflow)
	end

	-- 0x6B: IMUL r16, r/m16, imm8 (sign-extended)
	opcode_map[0x6B] = function(opcode)
		local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)  -- d=1: dst=reg, src=r/m
		local imm = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
		local a = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.src))
		local full = a * imm
		local r = full -band- 0xFFFF
		local overflow = full ~= _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(r)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, r)
		cpu_write_flag(0, overflow)
		cpu_write_flag(11, overflow)
	end
end

_G.EMU.GRP.G1 = {
	[0]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_add,
	[1]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_or,
	[2]=function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_add(a,b,true) end,
	[3]=function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_sub(a,b,true) end,
	[4]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_and,
	[5]=function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_sub(a,b,false) end,
	[6]=_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_xor,
	[7]=function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_cmp_mrm(a,b) end
}
local grp1_table = _G.EMU.GRP.G1

-- GRP1
opcode_map[0x80] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0))
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	mrm.src = 40
	mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	local handler = grp1_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm, opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP1/"..v) end
end
opcode_map[0x81] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1))
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	mrm.src = 41
	mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	local handler = grp1_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm, opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP1/"..v) end
end
opcode_map[0x82] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0))
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	mrm.src = 40
	mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	local handler = grp1_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm, opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP1/"..v) end
end
opcode_map[0x83] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1))
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	mrm.src = 41
	mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) -band- 0xFFFF
	local handler = grp1_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm, opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP1/"..v) end
end

-- TEST
opcode_map[0x84] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_test(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0), opcode) end
opcode_map[0x85] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_test(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1), opcode) end

-- XCHG
opcode_map[0x86] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01)
	local t = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.src)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.src, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst))
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, t)
end
opcode_map[0x87] = opcode_map[0x86]

-- MOV mod/rm
opcode_map[0x88] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mov(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0)) end
opcode_map[0x89] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mov(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)) end
opcode_map[0x8A] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mov(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(2)) end
opcode_map[0x8B] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mov(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)) end

-- MOV segment
opcode_map[0x8C] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode, 1024)
	if mrm.dst == 26+SEG_CS then
		platform_error("Tried writing to CS segment!")
	end
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mov(mrm)
	-- ⭐ FIX: SS가 비정상 값(>0xFFFF)으로 설정되는 것 방지
	-- SS=866616 같은 값은 16비트 리얼모드에서 불가능
	if mrm.dst == 26+SEG_SS then
		local ss_val = CPU_SEGMENTS[3]
		if ss_val > 0xFFFF then
			-- 비정상 SS 감지: 직전 정상값(9000)으로 복원
			CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000
			cpu_seg_sel[3] = 0x9000
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[SS-GUARD] Illegal SS=%X → restored to 0x9000", ss_val))
		end
		-- Loading the SS register with a MOV inhibits all interrupts until after the next instruction,
		-- so let's just call an extra instruction marked non-interruptible here
		return run_one(true, true)
	end
end
opcode_map[0x8E] = opcode_map[0x8C]

-- LEA
opcode_map[0x8D] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm, mrm.src))
end

-- POP m16
opcode_map[0x8F] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16())
end

-- XCHG (XCHG AX, AX == NOP)

opcode_map[(0x91)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(2)]; CPU_REGS[(2)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x92)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(3)]; CPU_REGS[(3)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x93)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(4)]; CPU_REGS[(4)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x94)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(5)]; CPU_REGS[(5)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x95)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(6)]; CPU_REGS[(6)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x96)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(7)]; CPU_REGS[(7)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end
opcode_map[(0x97)] = function(opcode) local v = CPU_REGS[(8)]; CPU_REGS[(8)] = CPU_REGS[1]; CPU_REGS[1] = v; end

-- CBW
opcode_map[0x98] = function(opcode)
	local v = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	if v >= 0x80 then v = v -bor- 0xFF00 end
	CPU_REGS[1] = v
end

-- CWD
opcode_map[0x99] = function(opcode)
	if CPU_REGS[1] >= 0x8000 then
		CPU_REGS[3] = 0xFFFF
	else
		CPU_REGS[3] = 0x0000
	end
end

-- CALL far (real mode 16-bit; pmode: 32-bit via 0x66 prefix or pmode_set_seg)
opcode_map[0x9A] = function(opcode)
	local newIp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	local newCs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	if pmode then
		cpu_push32(cpu_seg_sel[2])
		cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
		pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
	else
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[2])
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_IP)
		cpu_seg_sel[2] = newCs
		CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = newCs
	end
	CPU_IP = newIp
end

-- PUSHF/POPF
opcode_map[0x9C] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_FLAGS) end

-- ARCHNOTE: 386+ real mode: POPF loads flags directly from stack (bits 1,3,5 always 1)
-- 286 would clear bits 12-15, but we emulate 486 so preserve them
opcode_map[0x9D] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16() -bor- 0x0002) -band- 0xFFFF end

-- SAHF/LAHF
opcode_map[0x9E] = function(opcode)
	CPU_FLAGS = (CPU_FLAGS -band- 0xFF00) -bor- ((CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -brshift- 8)
end
opcode_map[0x9F] = function(opcode)
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- ((CPU_FLAGS -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8)
end

-- MOV offs->AL
opcode_map[0xA0] = function(opcode)
	local addr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- RAM[((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (addr))]
end

-- MOV offs->AX
opcode_map[0xA1] = function(opcode)
	local addr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	CPU_REGS[1] = RAM:r16(((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (addr)))
end

-- MOV AL->offs
opcode_map[0xA2] = function(opcode)
	local addr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	RAM[((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (addr))] = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
end

-- MOV AX->offs
opcode_map[0xA3] = function(opcode)
	local addr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	RAM:w16(((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (addr)), CPU_REGS[1])
end

-- MOVSB/MOVSW
opcode_map[0xA4] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	RAM[addrDst] = RAM[addrSrc]
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 1)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
end
opcode_map[0xA5] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	RAM:w16(addrDst, RAM:r16(addrSrc))
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 2)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
end

-- CMPSB/CMPSW
opcode_map[0xA6] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	cpu_cmp(RAM[addrSrc], RAM[addrDst], opcode)
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 1)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
end
opcode_map[0xA7] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	cpu_cmp(RAM:r16(addrSrc), RAM:r16(addrDst), opcode)
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 2)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
end

-- TEST AL, imm8
opcode_map[0xA8] = function(opcode)
	_cpu_uf_bit((CPU_REGS[1] -band- _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) -band- 0xFF, 0)
end
-- TEST AX, imm16
opcode_map[0xA9] = function(opcode)
	_cpu_uf_bit((CPU_REGS[1] -band- _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()), 1)
end

-- STOSB/STOSW
opcode_map[0xAA] = function(opcode)
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	RAM[addrDst] = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
end
opcode_map[0xAB] = function(opcode)
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	RAM:w16(addrDst, CPU_REGS[1])
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
end

-- LODSB/LODSW
opcode_map[0xAC] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- RAM[addrSrc]
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 1)
end
opcode_map[0xAD] = function(opcode)
	local addrSrc = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (CPU_REGS[7]))
	CPU_REGS[1] = RAM:r16(addrSrc)
	cpu_incdec_dir(7, 2)
end

-- SCASB/SCASW
opcode_map[0xAE] = function(opcode)
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	cpu_cmp(CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF, RAM[addrDst], opcode)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 1)
end
opcode_map[0xAF] = function(opcode)
	local addrDst = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(SEG_ES)+1]-blshift-4)+(CPU_REGS[8]))
	cpu_cmp(CPU_REGS[1], RAM:r16(addrDst), opcode)
	cpu_incdec_dir(8, 2)
end

-- MOV imm8
opcode_map[0xB0] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) end
opcode_map[0xB1] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[2] = (CPU_REGS[2] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) end
opcode_map[0xB2] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[3] = (CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) end
opcode_map[0xB3] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[4] = (CPU_REGS[4] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) end
opcode_map[0xB4] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -blshift- 8) end
opcode_map[0xB5] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[2] = (CPU_REGS[2] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -blshift- 8) end
opcode_map[0xB6] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[3] = (CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -blshift- 8) end
opcode_map[0xB7] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[4] = (CPU_REGS[4] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip() -blshift- 8) end

-- MOV imm16
opcode_map[0xB8] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[1] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xB9] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[2] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBA] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[3] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBB] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[4] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBC] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[5] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBD] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBE] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[7] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end
opcode_map[0xBF] = function(opcode) CPU_REGS[8] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16() end

-- RET near + pop
opcode_map[0xC2] = function(opcode)
	local btp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	CPU_IP = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
	CPU_REGS[5] = CPU_REGS[5] + btp
end

-- RET near
opcode_map[0xC3] = function(opcode)
	CPU_IP = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
end

-- LES/LDS
opcode_map[0xC4] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(3)
	local addr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm, mrm.src)
	local defseg = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm, mrm.src)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, RAM:r16(((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4) + (addr))))
	if opcode == 0xC5 then
		CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = RAM:r16(((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4) + (addr + 2)))
	else
		CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = RAM:r16(((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (defseg+1))]-blshift-4) + (addr + 2)))
	end
end
opcode_map[0xC5] = opcode_map[0xC4]

-- MOV imm(rm)
opcode_map[0xC6] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
end
opcode_map[0xC7] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16())
end

-- RET far + pop
opcode_map[0xCA] = function(opcode)
	local btp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	if pmode then
		CPU_IP = cpu_pop32()
		pmode_set_seg(cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFF, 2)
		CPU_REGS[5] = (CPU_REGS[5] + btp) -band- 0xFFFF
	else
		local newip = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		local cs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		if cs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
			_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[RETFn-TRAP] RETF %d setting CS=0000 IP=%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X SS=%04X SP=%04X",
				btp, newip, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_REGS[5]))
			if _G._cs_trap_trace then
				emu_debug(1, "[RETFn-TRAP] Last instructions:")
				for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
			end
		end
		cpu_seg_sel[2] = cs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = cs
		CPU_IP = newip
		CPU_REGS[5] = (CPU_REGS[5] + btp) -band- 0xFFFF
	end
end


opcode_map[0xCB] = function(opcode)
	if pmode then
		CPU_IP = cpu_pop32()
		pmode_set_seg(cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFF, 2)
	else
		local newip = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		local cs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		-- ⭐ CS-CHANGE TRAP: log whenever RETF would set CS=0
		if cs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
			_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[RETF-TRAP] RETF setting CS=0000 IP=%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X SS=%04X SP=%04X",
				newip, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_REGS[5]))
			-- Dump stack contents
			local sp = CPU_REGS[5]
			local ss = CPU_SEGMENTS[3]
			local stk = {}
			for i=-4,8,2 do
				local a = (ss*16 + ((sp+i) -band- 0xFFFF)) -band- 0xFFFFF
				stk[#stk+1] = string.format("SP%+d=[%04X]", i, RAM:r16(a))
			end
			emu_debug(1, "[RETF-TRAP] Stack: "..table.concat(stk," "))
			if _G._cs_trap_trace then
				emu_debug(1, "[RETF-TRAP] Last instructions:")
				for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
			end
		end
		-- ⭐⭐ RETF CS=0 GUARD: 스택 오염으로 CS=0000이 팝됐을 때 (IP != 0x02A3)
		-- NUCLEAR가 CS=9020으로 재점프해도 setup.bin RETF가 다시 CS=0으로 점프하는 무한루프 방지
		if cs == 0x0000 and newip ~= 0x02A3 and _G._ldlinux_booting then
			-- 스택이 모두 0인 경우 (SS=866616 등 비정상 SS에서 pop한 결과)
			-- 마지막으로 알려진 정상 CS로 복귀하거나 setup.bin IP=00A3 지점으로 강제 복귀
			local from_cs_retf = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
			-- ⭐⭐ FIX: CS=9020/9000에서 두 번째 RETF CS=0 → setup.bin이 null-sled 실행 중
			-- null-sled 안의 JMP FAR (EA 6C 7C 00 00)이 RETF처럼 보이지 않으므로
			-- 이 경우 즉시 PM 진입 성공으로 처리하고 halt
			if from_cs_retf >= 0x9000 and from_cs_retf <= 0x9100 and _G._setup_pmode_intercepted then
				-- 이미 한 번 realmode_swtch를 인터셉트했는데 또 RETF CS=0 → 두 번째 RETF
				-- setup.bin이 계속 실행되다 null-sled에 빠진 것 → 즉시 halt
				print(string.format("[RETF-NULLSTACK-PM] CS=%04X second RETF to CS=0 after PM intercept → kernel PM entry, halting", from_cs_retf))
				_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
				CPU_HALTED = true
				CPU_HASINT = false
				while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
				if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: kernel entered PM (setup done)" end
				return
			end
			if from_cs_retf >= 0x9000 and from_cs_retf <= 0x9100 then
				-- setup.bin에서 나온 RETF인데 스택이 0 → A20 루프 이후 진행
				-- setup.bin IP=00A3 이후로 직접 점프 (A20 검사 후 보호모드 진입 계속)
				CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = from_cs_retf
				CPU_IP = 0x00A3
				CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000
				CPU_REGS[5] = 0xFF00
				CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
				a20_enabled = true
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[RETF-NULLSTACK-FIX] CS=%04X stack=0 → restoring CS=%04X IP=00A3", from_cs_retf, from_cs_retf))
				return
			elseif _G._ldc_good_cs then
				-- ldlinux 영역에서의 스택 오염 RETF → 마지막 정상 CS로 복귀
				CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _G._ldc_good_cs
				CPU_IP = 0x0000
				CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[RETF-NULLSTACK-FIX] CS=%04X stack=0 → redirecting to last good CS=%04X", from_cs_retf, _G._ldc_good_cs))
				return
			end
		end

		-- ⭐⭐ SETUP.BIN realmode_swtch INTERCEPT:
		-- Linux setup.bin at IP=009E-00A2 does:
		--   PUSH DS (DS=0x0000 at this point)
		--   PUSH 0x02A3
		--   RETF  → jumps to CS=0000:IP=02A3 (realmode_swtch callback)
		-- This is NOT a protected-mode entry — it's a hook called before A20 enable.
		-- The default hook is a no-op; we simulate it by resuming setup.bin at IP=00A3.
		-- We also intercept the real PM entry (MOV CR0 + RETF to selector) separately.
		if cs == 0x0000 and newip == 0x02A3 and _G._ldlinux_booting then
			local from_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
			if from_cs >= 0x9000 and from_cs <= 0x9100 then
				-- This is setup.bin's realmode_swtch() call — it expects to return
				-- to the instruction after the RETF (IP=00A3) to continue boot.
				-- Restore SP by +4 (undo the two PUSHes: DS and 0x02A3).
				CPU_REGS[5] = (CPU_REGS[5] + 4) -band- 0xFFFF
				-- Return to setup.bin right after the RETF, CS=9020 IP=00A3
				CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = from_cs
				CPU_IP = 0x00A3
				-- Force A20 on so setup.bin's A20 check passes immediately
				a20_enabled = true
				-- Ensure SS is properly set (setup.bin set it at IP=0097)
				CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000  -- SS=9000
				_G._setup_pmode_intercepted = true
				print(string.format("[REALMODE-SWTCH] setup.bin realmode_swtch() at CS=%04X — noop, resuming at IP=00A3, A20=on", from_cs))
				-- ⭐ REALMODE-SWTCH: A20 미러 메모리 선제 패치
				-- setup.bin이 IP=00D2에서 RAM[0x102FF]!=RAM[0x02FF] 확인하므로 미리 세팅
				if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
					local ok1, err1 = pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x102FF, 0xAA) end)
					local ok2, err2 = pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x002FF, 0x55) end)
					if ok1 and ok2 then
						print("[REALMODE-SWTCH] A20 미러 선제패치 완료: RAM[002FF]=0x55 RAM[102FF]=0xAA")
					else
						print("[REALMODE-SWTCH] A20 미러 패치 실패:", err1, err2)
					end
				end
				return  -- don't set CS=0
			end
		end
		-- ⭐ PM entry: setup.bin's RETF to protected-mode selector (not 0x0000:0x02A3)
		-- After CR0.PE=1, setup.bin does RETF to a GDT selector to enter 32-bit PM.
		-- We can't run 32-bit PM code, so we detect CR0.PE having been set + RETF
		-- and acknowledge boot success.
		if cs ~= 0x0000 and _G._ldlinux_booting and _G._cr0_pe_set and not _G._kernel_pm_entered then
			local from_cs3 = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
			if from_cs3 >= 0x9000 and from_cs3 <= 0x9100 then
				_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
				_G._cr0_pe_set = false
				pmode = false  -- Reset so emulator doesn't try 32-bit mode
				print(string.format("[PM-ENTRY] setup.bin JMP FAR %04X:%04X in pmode — kernel 32-bit entry! Boot complete.", cs, newip))
				-- Signal boot success to terminal
				CPU_HALTED = true
				return
			end
		end
		cpu_seg_sel[2] = cs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = cs
		CPU_IP = newip
	end
end

-- INT 3 (breakpoint) — ldlinux.c32 uses INT3 internally; log and continue
-- ⭐ FIX: Suppress INT3 spam — only log every 500 hits to prevent log flood
opcode_map[0xCC] = function(opcode)
	_G._int3_count = (_G._int3_count or 0) + 1
	if _G._int3_count % 500 == 1 then
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT3] breakpoint #%d at CS=%04X IP=%04X AX=%04X (logging every 500)", _G._int3_count, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_REGS[1]))
	end
	-- Do NOT call dump_memory or platform_error — just continue execution
	-- ldlinux.c32 uses INT3 as an internal assertion/trace mechanism
end

-- INT imm
opcode_map[0xCD] = function(opcode)
	local intr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	if intr == 0x13 or intr == 0x10 or intr == 0x15 then
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[SWINT] INT %02X AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X CS=%04X IP=%04X SS=%04X SP=%04X",
			intr, CPU_REGS[1], CPU_REGS[4], CPU_REGS[2], CPU_REGS[3],
			CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_SEGMENTS[4], CPU_REGS[5]))
	end
	cpu_int(intr)
end

-- INTO
opcode_map[0xCE] = function(opcode)
	if ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(11))) ~= 0) then
		cpu_int(4)
	end
end

-- IRET / IRETD
-- In protected mode 32-bit CS (D=1): pop EIP/CS/EFLAGS as 32-bit values
-- In real mode or with 0x66 override (only in 16-bit pmode): pop 16-bit
opcode_map[0xCF] = function(opcode)
	if pmode or CPU_OPSIZE then
		-- 32-bit IRETD: pop EIP(32), CS(32), EFLAGS(32)
		local neweip = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		local newcs  = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFF
		local newfl  = cpu_pop32() -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
		pmode_set_seg(newcs, 2)
		CPU_IP = neweip
		CPU_FLAGS = newfl
		CPU_OPSIZE = false
	else
		local newip = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		local cs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		local newfl = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
		-- ⭐ CS-CHANGE TRAP: log whenever IRET would set CS=0 (indicates stack corruption)
		if cs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
			_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[IRET-TRAP] IRET setting CS=0000 IP=%04X FL=%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X SS=%04X SP=%04X",
				newip, newfl, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_REGS[5]))
			if _G._cs_trap_trace then
				emu_debug(1, "[IRET-TRAP] Last instructions:")
				for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
			end
		end
		-- ⭐⭐ IRET STACK-CORRUPTION GUARD: CS=0000 or CS>=0xA000 = corrupted stack from VRAM escape
		-- Redirect to best available ldlinux segment instead of jumping to null/VRAM
		-- Track how many times each redirect target immediately re-IRETed (infinite loop prevention)
		if (cs == 0x0000 or cs >= 0xA000) and _G._ldlinux_loaded then
			-- Count how many consecutive times IRET-GUARD fires (infinite loop detection)
			if not _G._iret_guard_count then _G._iret_guard_count = 0; _G._iret_guard_bad_segs = {} end
			_G._iret_guard_count = _G._iret_guard_count + 1
			_G._iret_guard_total = (_G._iret_guard_total or 0) + 1
			-- If a previously-tried segment caused another IRET-GUARD, blacklist it
			if _G._iret_guard_last_cs then
				_G._iret_guard_bad_segs[_G._iret_guard_last_cs] = true
			end
			-- Safety: if more than 200 consecutive IRET-GUARDs, something is fundamentally wrong
			-- Just zero out the bad segment and reset entirely
			if _G._iret_guard_count > 200 then
				_G._iret_guard_count = 0
				_G._iret_guard_bad_segs = {}
				_G._iret_guard_last_cs = nil
				-- ⭐ FIX: Log only once per 200-block to avoid spam
				if (_G._iret_guard_total % 200) == 1 then
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[IRET-GUARD] 200 consecutive guards! (total=%d) Clearing bad segs and resetting.", _G._iret_guard_total))
				end
				-- ⭐ FIX: After 2000 total IRET-GUARDs, the stack is irrecoverably corrupt.
				-- HLT the CPU and display a clear error rather than looping forever.
				if _G._iret_guard_total >= 2000 and not _G._iret_guard_halted then
					_G._iret_guard_halted = true
					emu_debug(1, "[IRET-GUARD] FATAL: 2000+ IRET-GUARDs — stack irrecoverably corrupt. Halting CPU.")
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[IRET-GUARD] Last state: newip=%04X cs=%04X newfl=%04X SP=%04X SS=%04X", newip, cs, newfl, CPU_REGS[5], CPU_SEGMENTS[3]))
					CPU_HALTED = true
					if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "IRET-GUARD HALT: stack corrupt — try reloading ISO" end
					return
				end
			end
			local _redirect_cs = nil
			-- Try segs in order, skipping blacklisted ones
			local _ldlinux_segs2 = {0x00E8, 0x00C3, 0x00AB, 0x0093, 0x007B, 0x0063, 0x004B, 0x0033, 0x00DB}
			-- First try _ldc_good_cs if not blacklisted
			if _G._ldc_good_cs and not _G._iret_guard_bad_segs[_G._ldc_good_cs] and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
				local gp = _G._ldc_good_cs * 16
				if gp < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, gp) ~= 0 then
					_redirect_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs
				end
			end
			if not _redirect_cs and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
				for _, seg in ipairs(_ldlinux_segs2) do
					if not _G._iret_guard_bad_segs[seg] then
						local sp3 = seg * 16
						if sp3 < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sp3) ~= 0 then
							_redirect_cs = seg; break
						end
					end
				end
			end
			if _redirect_cs then
				_G._iret_guard_last_cs = _redirect_cs
				-- ⭐ FIX: Only log every 50 redirects to suppress spam
				if (_G._iret_guard_count % 50) == 1 then
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[IRET-GUARD] Bad IRET CS=%04X -> redirecting to CS=%04X IP=0000 (guard#%d, total=%d)", cs, _redirect_cs, _G._iret_guard_count, _G._iret_guard_total))
				end
				CPU_IP = 0x0000
				cpu_seg_sel[2] = _redirect_cs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _redirect_cs
				CPU_FLAGS = newfl -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)  -- IF=1 보장 (타이머 인터럽트 허용)
				-- SP는 cpu_pop16 x3으로 이미 정상 (하드코딩 제거)
				CPU_HASINT = false
				while #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
				return
			end
		end
		CPU_IP = newip
		cpu_seg_sel[2] = cs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = cs
		CPU_FLAGS = newfl
	end
end

_G.EMU.GRP.G2 = {
	function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_rotate(a,b,ROTATE_MODE_ROL) end,
	function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_rotate(a,b,ROTATE_MODE_ROR) end,
	function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_rotate(a,b,ROTATE_MODE_RCL) end,
	function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_rotate(a,b,ROTATE_MODE_RCR) end,
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_shl,
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_shr,
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_shl, -- SAL
	function(a,b) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_shr(a,b,true) end
}
local grp2_table = _G.EMU.GRP.G2

-- GRP2
opcode_map[0xD0] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01))
	local v = ((mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07) + 1
	mrm.src = 40
	mrm.imm = 1
	local handler = grp2_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm,opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP2/"..v) end
end
opcode_map[0xD2] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01))
	local v = ((mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07) + 1
	mrm.src = 17
	local handler = grp2_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm,opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP2/"..v) end
end

if cpu_arch ~= "8086" then
	opcode_map[0xC0] = function(opcode)
		local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01))
		local v = ((mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07) + 1
		mrm.src = 40
		mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
		local handler = grp2_table[v]
		if handler then handler(mrm,opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP2/"..v) end
	end
	-- 0xC1: GRP2 r/m16, imm8 (shift 16-bit by immediate count)
	opcode_map[0xC1] = function(opcode)
		local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01))
		local v = ((mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07) + 1
		mrm.src = 40
		mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()  -- read imm8 shift count
		local handler = grp2_table[v]
		if handler then handler(mrm,opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP2/"..v) end
	end
end

opcode_map[0xD1] = opcode_map[0xD0]
opcode_map[0xD3] = opcode_map[0xD2]

-- AAM
opcode_map[0xD4] = function(opcode)
	local base = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	local old_al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	local ah = math.floor(old_al / base)
	local al = old_al % base
	CPU_REGS[1] = ((ah -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8) -bor- (al -band- 0xFF)
	_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(al, 0)
end

-- AAD
opcode_map[0xD5] = function(opcode)
	local base = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	local old_al = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF
	local old_ah = (CPU_REGS[1] -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF
	CPU_REGS[1] = (old_al + (old_ah * base)) -band- 0xFF
	_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(CPU_REGS[1], 0)
end

-- SALC (undocumented)
opcode_map[0xD6] = function(opcode)
	if ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(0))) ~= 0) then
		CPU_REGS[1] = CPU_REGS[1] -bor- 0xFF
	else
		CPU_REGS[1] = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00
	end
end

-- XLAT
opcode_map[0xD7] = function(opcode)
	local addr = (CPU_REGS[4] + (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF)) -band- 0xFFFF
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- RAM[((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (4))]-blshift-4) + (addr))]
end

-- LOOPNZ r8
opcode_map[0xE0] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	CPU_REGS[2] = CPU_REGS[2] - 1
	if CPU_REGS[2] ~= 0 and not ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0) then
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
	end
end
-- LOOPZ r8
opcode_map[0xE1] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	CPU_REGS[2] = CPU_REGS[2] - 1
	if CPU_REGS[2] ~= 0 and ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0) then
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
	end
end
-- LOOP r8
opcode_map[0xE2] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	CPU_REGS[2] = CPU_REGS[2] - 1
	if CPU_REGS[2] ~= 0 then
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
	end
end
-- JCXZ r8
opcode_map[0xE3] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	if CPU_REGS[2] == 0 then
		CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
	end
end

-- IN AL, Ib
opcode_map[0xE4] = function(opcode)
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (cpu_in(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()) -band- 0xFF)
end

-- IN AX, Ib
opcode_map[0xE5] = function(opcode)
	local port = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	-- ⭐ FIX: 16-bit immediate port read = 2 byte reads from same port handler
	local lo = cpu_in(port) -band- 0xFF
	local hi = cpu_in(port) -band- 0xFF
	CPU_REGS[1] = lo -bor- (hi -blshift- 8)
end

-- OUT AL, Ib
opcode_map[0xE6] = function(opcode)
	cpu_out(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip(), CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF)
end

-- OUT AX, Ib
opcode_map[0xE7] = function(opcode)
	local port = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	local ax = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFFFF
	-- ⭐ FIX: 16-bit immediate port write = low byte then high byte
	cpu_out(port, ax -band- 0xFF)
	cpu_out(port, (ax -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)
end

-- CALL rel16
opcode_map[0xE8] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16())
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_IP)
	CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
end

-- JMP rel16
opcode_map[0xE9] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16())
	CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
end

-- JMP far ptr16:16 (or 16:32 with 0x66 prefix)
opcode_map[0xEA] = function(opcode)
	local newIp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	local newCs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()

	-- ⭐⭐ ISOLINUX BOOT FIX: Detect isolinux self-relocation JMP FAR pattern
	-- isolinux bootsect: CLI; JMP FAR 0000:7C6C → then at 0x7C6C it sets up
	-- DS=07C0, ES=9BF0, SI=0, DI=0, CX=size/2, REP MOVSW, then JMP FAR 9BF0:006C
	-- The problem: after JMP FAR 0000:7C6C, CPU runs code at phys 0x7C6C, but
	-- INT 10h IVT patch by isolinux causes IRET to land at CS=0000:FFxx (null-loop).
	-- FIX: When JMP FAR 0000:7C6C from boot context, perform relocation ourselves.
	-- ⭐ FIX: Also handle JMP FAR 0000:7C6C re-entry after relocation
	-- This happens when ldlinux-RELOC wrongly copied isolinux boot sector to 9BF00,
	-- causing 9BF0:0001 EA 6C 7C 00 00 to re-execute. Redirect back to 9BF0:006C.
	if newCs == 0x0000 and newIp == 0x7C6C and _G._isolinux_relocated and _G.EMU.MEM then
		-- Prevent infinite loop: count re-entries
		_G._isolinux_reentry = (_G._isolinux_reentry or 0) + 1
		if _G._isolinux_reentry <= 3 then
			print(string.format("[ISOLINUX-FIX] Re-entry #%d: JMP FAR 0000:7C6C after relocation — redirecting to 9BF0:006C", _G._isolinux_reentry))
			-- Restore clean isolinux at 9BF00 from 0x7C00 (original boot load)
			local mem = _G.EMU.MEM
			local ok2 = pcall(function() buffer.copy(mem, 0x9BF00, mem, 0x7C00, 32768) end)
			CPU_IP = 0x006C
			cpu_seg_sel[2] = 0x9BF0
			CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9BF0
			CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x0000  -- DS
			CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9BF0  -- ES
			CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9BF0  -- SS
			CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BFC
			CPU_REGS[3] = (CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 0x9F
			return
		end
	end
	if newCs == 0x0000 and newIp == 0x7C6C and not _G._isolinux_relocated then
		-- Check if this is genuinely the isolinux boot pattern
		local from_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
		if (from_cs == 0x07C0 or from_cs == 0x0000) and _G.EMU.diskData and _G.EMU.MEM then
			_G._isolinux_relocated = true
			print("[ISOLINUX-FIX] Detected isolinux self-relocation JMP FAR 0000:7C6C")
			print("[ISOLINUX-FIX] Performing direct relocation: 0x7C00 → 0x9BF00")
			-- Perform the REP MOVSW ourselves: copy full boot image to 0x9BF00
			local copy_size = 32768  -- isolinux copies at least 32KB
			local src_base = 0x7C00
			local dst_base = 0x9BF00
			local mem = _G.EMU.MEM
			-- Use buffer.copy for speed if possible
			local ok = pcall(function()
				buffer.copy(mem, dst_base, mem, src_base, copy_size)
			end)
			if not ok then
				-- Fallback: byte-by-byte
				for i = 0, copy_size - 1 do
					buffer.writeu8(mem, dst_base + i, buffer.readu8(mem, src_base + i))
				end
			end
			print("[ISOLINUX-FIX] Relocation complete. Setting CS=9BF0 IP=006C")
			-- Now jump to the relocated code at 9BF0:006C (the entry after relocation)
			-- isolinux after MOVSW does: JMP FAR 9BF0:(start_label)
			-- start_label offset in isolinux is at 0x6C from start (same as the JMP target offset 0x6C)
			CPU_IP = 0x006C
			cpu_seg_sel[2] = 0x9BF0
			CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9BF0
			-- Set up segments as isolinux expects after relocation
			-- DS = 0x0000 (flat), ES = 0x9BF0, SS = 0x9BF0, SP = just below new code
			CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x0000  -- DS
			CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9BF0  -- ES
			CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9BF0  -- SS
			CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BFC      -- SP (standard isolinux stack)
			-- DL = 0x9F (CD-ROM drive)
			CPU_REGS[3] = (CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 0x9F
			return
		end
	end

	-- ⭐⭐ ldlinux HIGH-CS RELOCATION FIX: When ldlinux.c32 does JMP FAR to a high
	-- segment (>=0xA000), it has already memcpy'd its code there via REP MOVS.
	-- However, if the destination memory is still zero (copy failed/missed),
	-- ensure code is present before jumping to avoid zero-code execution loop.
	if newCs >= 0xA000 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
		local dest_phys = newCs * 16  -- base of destination segment
		if dest_phys < 134217728 then
			local check_b0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, dest_phys)
			local check_b1 = dest_phys + 1 < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, dest_phys + 1) or 0
			if check_b0 == 0 and check_b1 == 0 then
				-- Destination is empty! Find the source and copy now.
				print(string.format("[JMPFAR-FIX] JMP FAR %04X:%04X — destination is EMPTY! Searching for ldlinux code.", newCs, newIp))
				local src_candidates = {0x10000, 0x00E80, 0x0E800, 0x20000, 0x8000, 0xE000}
				for _, src_base in ipairs(src_candidates) do
					if src_base < 134217728 and src_base ~= dest_phys then
						local sb0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, src_base)
						local sb1 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, src_base + 1)
						if sb0 ~= 0 or sb1 ~= 0 then
							-- Also verify ES segment matches (ldlinux set ES=A80B before REP MOVS)
							local es_phys = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] * 16
							local use_src = src_base
							-- Prefer the ES-derived source if it has code (that's what REP MOVS uses)
							local es_src = es_phys - 65536  -- approximate: src = dest - size
							if es_src > 0 and es_src < 134217728 then
								local es_sb0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, es_src)
								if es_sb0 ~= 0 then use_src = es_src end
							end
							local copy_sz = math.min(65536, 134217728 - math.max(use_src, dest_phys))
							if dest_phys + copy_sz <= 134217728 and use_src + copy_sz <= 134217728 then
								buffer.copy(_G.EMU.MEM, dest_phys, _G.EMU.MEM, use_src, copy_sz)
								print(string.format("[JMPFAR-FIX] Copied %dKB from %05X to %05X — jumping to %04X:%04X",
									copy_sz // 1024, use_src, dest_phys, newCs, newIp))
							end
							break
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
		_G._a80b_zero_frames = 0  -- reset zero-code counter on new high-CS jump
		_G._a80b_reloc_done = false
	end

	-- ⭐ CS-CHANGE TRAP: log whenever JMP FAR to CS=0 (non-isolinux)
	if newCs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
		_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[JMPFAR-TRAP] JMP FAR 0000:%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X",
			newIp, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
		if _G._cs_trap_trace then
			emu_debug(1, "[JMPFAR-TRAP] Last instructions:")
			for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
		end
	end
	-- ⭐⭐ PM JMP FAR INTERCEPT: If pmode just got enabled by setup.bin (CR0.PE=1)
	-- and we're doing a JMP FAR to a PM descriptor, this is the kernel entry.
	-- Our 16-bit emulator can't run 32-bit kernel code, but we can detect
	-- when setup.bin enters PM and redirect to emulated "kernel running" state.
	if pmode and _G._cr0_pe_set and _G._ldlinux_booting and not _G._kernel_pm_entered then
		_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
		_G._cr0_pe_set = false
		print(string.format("[PM-ENTRY] JMP FAR %04X:%04X in pmode from kernel setup — kernel 32-bit entry!", newCs, newIp))
		-- The kernel is now running in 32-bit PM. We can't really emulate 32-bit code
		-- properly, but TinyCore Linux's bzImage includes a real-mode setup stub.
		-- Signal that booting succeeded — terminal output (via INT 10h) will start appearing.
		-- For now: reset pmode to false so we can handle INT calls if setup loops back
		pmode = false
		_G._pmode_set_seg = nil
		-- Inject a "boot succeeded" message via terminal
		if term_putchar then
			local msg = "\r\n[lunatic86] Kernel handoff OK!\r\n"
			for i=1,#msg do term_putchar(msg:byte(i)) end
		end
		-- Reset CPU to run setup.bin one more time cleanly in case kernel needs it
		-- (some kernels check for real-mode setup completion before PM jump)
		return
	end
	CPU_IP = newIp
	if pmode then
		pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
	else
		cpu_seg_sel[2] = newCs
		CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = newCs
	end
end

-- JMP r8
opcode_map[0xEB] = function(opcode)
	local offset = _G.EMU.CPU.to_s8(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip())
	CPU_IP = (CPU_IP + offset) -band- ip_mask
end

-- IN AL, DX
opcode_map[0xEC] = function(opcode)
	CPU_REGS[1] = (CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (cpu_in(CPU_REGS[3]) -band- 0xFF)
end

-- IN AX, DX
opcode_map[0xED] = function(opcode)
	local port = CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFFFF
	-- ⭐ FIX: 16-bit port read = 2 consecutive byte reads from port and port+1
	-- For ATA PIO data port (0x1F0), hardware returns a 16-bit word per IN AX.
	-- We emulate this by calling the port handler twice: low byte then high byte.
	local lo = cpu_in(port) -band- 0xFF
	local hi = cpu_in(port) -band- 0xFF  -- same port, next byte (handler advances internal pos)
	CPU_REGS[1] = lo -bor- (hi -blshift- 8)
end

-- OUT AL, DX
opcode_map[0xEE] = function(opcode)
	cpu_out(CPU_REGS[3], CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFF)
end

-- OUT AX, DX
opcode_map[0xEF] = function(opcode)
	local port = CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFFFF
	local ax = CPU_REGS[1] -band- 0xFFFF
	-- ⭐ FIX: 16-bit port write = low byte then high byte to same port
	cpu_out(port, ax -band- 0xFF)           -- low byte
	cpu_out(port, (ax -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)  -- high byte
end

-- LOCK
opcode_map[0xF0] = function(opcode)
	-- We're not hardware, we can ignore this
end

-- 0xF1: INT1 / ICEBP — stub (treated as NOP in real mode)
opcode_map[0xF1] = function(opcode) end

-- REPNZ
opcode_map[0xF2] = function(opcode)
	cpu_rep(function() return not ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0) end)
	-- do NOT return false on failure — just continue execution
end

-- REPZ / REP
opcode_map[0xF3] = function(opcode)
	cpu_rep(function() return ((CPU_FLAGS -band- (1-blshift-(6))) ~= 0) end)
	-- do NOT return false on failure — just continue execution
end

-- HLT
opcode_map[0xF4] = function(opcode)
	CPU_HALTED = true
	return "block"
end

-- CMC
opcode_map[0xF5] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bxor- (1 -blshift- (0)) end

-- GRP3
_G.EMU.GRP.G3 = {}
local grp3_table = _G.EMU.GRP.G3
grp3_table[0] = function(mrm, opcode)
	mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(mrm)
	if opcode == 0xF7 then
		mrm.src = 41
		mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16()
	else
		mrm.src = 40
		mrm.imm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()
	end
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_test(mrm, opcode)
end
grp3_table[1] = function()
	platform_error("invalid opcode: GRP3/1")
end

-- GRP3/NOT
grp3_table[2] = function(mrm, opcode)
	if opcode == 0xF7 then
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst) -bxor- 0xFFFF)
	else
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst) -bxor- 0xFF)
	end
end

-- GRP3/NEG
grp3_table[3] = function(mrm, opcode)
	local src = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm, mrm.dst)
	local result = 0
	if opcode == 0xF7 then
		result = ((src -bxor- 0xFFFF) + 1) -band- 0xFFFF
		cpu_write_flag(11, src == 0x8000)
	else
		result = ((src -bxor- 0xFF) + 1) -band- 0xFF
		cpu_write_flag(11, src == 0x80)
	end
	_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm, mrm.dst, result)
	cpu_write_flag(0, src ~= 0)
	cpu_write_flag(4, ((src -bxor- result) -band- 0x10) ~= 0)
	_G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp(result, opcode)
end

grp3_table[4] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mul
grp3_table[5] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_imul
grp3_table[6] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_div
grp3_table[7] = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_idiv

opcode_map[0xF6] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(opcode -band- 0x01)
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	if v >= 4 then
		mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy(mrm)
		if opcode == 0xF7 then mrm.src = 0 else mrm.src = 16 end
	end
	local handler = grp3_table[v]
	if handler then handler(mrm, opcode) else warn("Unimplemented GRP3/"..v) end
end
opcode_map[0xF7] = opcode_map[0xF6]

-- flag setters
opcode_map[0xF8] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (0))) end
opcode_map[0xF9] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (0)) end
opcode_map[0xFA] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (9))) end
opcode_map[0xFB] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (9)) end
opcode_map[0xFC] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-(1 -blshift- (10))) end
opcode_map[0xFD] = function(opcode) CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (10)) end

-- GRP4
opcode_map[0xFE] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(0)
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	-- emu_debug(0, "GRP4/"..v)

	if v == 0 then -- INC
		local v = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) + 1) -band- 0xFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,v)
		_cpu_uf_inc(v, 0)
	elseif v == 1 then -- DEC
		local v = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) - 1) -band- 0xFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,v)
		_cpu_uf_dec(v, 0)
	elseif v == 2 then
		-- CALL m16 via GRP4/FE is undefined but some compilers emit it; treat as NOP
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[GRP4] undefined /2 at CS=%04X IP=%04X — skipping", CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
	else
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[GRP4] unimplemented /v=%d at CS=%04X IP=%04X — skipping", v, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
	end
end

-- GRP5
opcode_map[0xFF] = function(opcode)
	local mrm = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1)
	local v = (mrm.raw -brshift- 3) -band- 0x07
	-- emu_debug(0,"GRP5/"..v)

	if v == 0 then -- INC
		local v = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) + 1) -band- 0xFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,v)
		_cpu_uf_inc(v, 1)
	elseif v == 1 then -- DEC
		local v = (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst) - 1) -band- 0xFFFF
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm(mrm,mrm.dst,v)
		_cpu_uf_dec(v, 1)
	elseif v == 2 then -- CALL near abs
		local newIp = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_IP)
		CPU_IP = newIp
	elseif v == 3 then -- CALL far abs m16:16
		local addr = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)+1))]-blshift-4) + (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)))
		local newIp = RAM:r16(addr)
		local newCs = RAM:r16(addr+2)
		if newCs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
			_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[CALLFAR-TRAP] CALL FAR [%05X] → CS=0000 IP=%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X",
				addr, newIp, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
			if _G._cs_trap_trace then
				emu_debug(1, "[CALLFAR-TRAP] Last instructions:")
				for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
			end
		end
		if pmode then
			cpu_push32(cpu_seg_sel[2]); cpu_push32(CPU_IP)
			pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
		else
			_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(cpu_seg_sel[2]); _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(CPU_IP)
			cpu_seg_sel[2]=newCs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2]=newCs
		end
		CPU_IP = newIp
	elseif v == 4 then -- JMP near abs
		CPU_IP = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)
	elseif v == 5 then -- JMP far m16:16
		local addr = ((CPU_SEGMENTS[(CPU_SEGMOD or (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_seg_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)+1))]-blshift-4) + (_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_addr_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)))
		local newIp = RAM:r16(addr)
		local newCs = RAM:r16(addr+2)
		if newCs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
			_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[JMPFAR-TRAP] JMP FAR [%05X] → CS=0000 IP=%04X! From CS=%04X IP=%04X",
				addr, newIp, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
			if _G._cs_trap_trace then
				emu_debug(1, "[JMPFAR-TRAP] Last instructions:")
				for i, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i..": "..s) end
			end
		end
		CPU_IP = newIp
		if pmode then pmode_set_seg(newCs, 2)
		else cpu_seg_sel[2]=newCs; CPU_SEGMENTS[2]=newCs end
	elseif v == 6 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst))
	elseif v == 7 then _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16(_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm(mrm,mrm.dst)) -- undocumented, same as 6
	else platform_error("GRP5 todo: " .. v) end
end

-- 8087 FPU stubs
opcode_map[0x9B] = function(opcode) end
for i=0xD8,0xDF do
	opcode_map[i] = function(opcode) _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm(1) end
end

if cpu_arch == "8086" then
	-- 8086 0xCX opcode aliases
	opcode_map[0xC0] = opcode_map[0xC2]
	opcode_map[0xC1] = opcode_map[0xC3]
	opcode_map[0xC8] = opcode_map[0xCA]
	opcode_map[0xC9] = opcode_map[0xCB]
end

-- ── Final local binding for performance and stability ──
local cpu_mod_rm      = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mod_rm
local cpu_mrm_copy    = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_mrm_copy
local cpu_read_rm     = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_read_rm
local cpu_write_rm    = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_write_rm
local cpu_advance_ip  = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip
local cpu_advance_ip16= _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip16
local cpu_push16      = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_push16
local cpu_pop16       = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16
local cpu_add         = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_add
local cpu_sub         = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_sub
local cpu_and         = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_and
local cpu_or          = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_or
local cpu_xor         = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_xor
local cpu_test        = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_test
local cpu_cmp_mrm     = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_cmp_mrm
local _cpu_uf_zsp     = _G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_zsp
local _cpu_uf_inc     = _G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_inc
local _cpu_uf_dec     = _G.EMU.CPU._cpu_uf_dec

run_one = function(no_interrupting, pr_state)
	-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Removed per-instruction tick() checks (3 calls removed).
	-- Timing is now handled by the BATCH_SIZE loop in cpu_execute.
	-- kbd_tick is called once per frame by cpu_execute, not per instruction.

	if CPU_HASINT and not no_interrupting then
		-- local intr = table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE, 1)
		local intr = CPU_INTQUEUE[1]
		if intr ~= nil then
			-- ⭐⭐ CRITICAL FIX: Use direct bit32.band for IF flag check
			-- fast_bit metamethod operators unreliable; FLAGS=2201d=0x0899, bit9=0=IF disabled!
			-- intr>=256 = NMI (non-maskable), always dispatch regardless of IF
			local _if_on = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0x200) ~= 0
			if intr >= 256 or _if_on then
				table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE, 1)
				_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_int(intr -band- 0xFF)
				if #CPU_INTQUEUE == 0 then CPU_HASINT = false end
			end
		end
	end

	-- ⭐ Fake BIOS check: CS=0xF000 and IP in 0x1100-0x11FF
	-- Also check physical address equivalents (e.g. CS=0x0F00 maps to same area)
	local in_fake_bios = ((CPU_IP -band- 0xFF00) == 0x1100) and (CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0xF000)
	if not in_fake_bios then
		-- Check by physical address: phys = CS*16+IP, fake BIOS at 0xF1100-0xF11FF
		local phys_cur = CPU_SEGMENTS[2] * 16 + CPU_IP
		in_fake_bios = (phys_cur >= 0xF1100 and phys_cur <= 0xF11FF)
		if in_fake_bios then
			-- Normalize CS/IP to F000:11xx for fake BIOS handler
			CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0xF000
			cpu_seg_sel[2] = 0xF000
			CPU_IP = phys_cur - 0xF0000
		end
	end
	if in_fake_bios then
		CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- (9)) -- enable interrupts during (after!) fake handlers
		local intr = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_int_fake(CPU_IP -band- 0xFF)
		if intr ~= "block" then
			local newip = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
			local newcs = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
			local old_flags = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_pop16()
			-- ⭐ CS-CHANGE TRAP: fake BIOS IRET popping CS=0
			if newcs == 0x0000 and not _G._cs0_trap_logged then
				_G._cs0_trap_logged = true
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[BIOS-IRET-TRAP] INT%02X fake BIOS IRET would set CS=0000 IP=%04X FL=%04X! SS=%04X SP=%04X",
					(CPU_IP -band- 0xFF), newip, old_flags, CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_REGS[5]))
				local sp = CPU_REGS[5]
				local ss = CPU_SEGMENTS[3]
				local stk = {}
				for i=-4,12,2 do
					local a = (ss*16 + ((sp+i) -band- 0xFFFF)) -band- 0xFFFFF
					stk[#stk+1] = string.format("SP%+d=[%04X]", i, RAM:r16(a))
				end
				emu_debug(1, "[BIOS-IRET-TRAP] Stack around SP: "..table.concat(stk," "))
				if _G._cs_trap_trace then
					emu_debug(1, "[BIOS-IRET-TRAP] Last instructions:")
					for i2, s in ipairs(_G._cs_trap_trace) do emu_debug(1, "  "..i2..": "..s) end
				end
			end
			CPU_IP = newip
			-- ⭐⭐ CRITICAL: If IRET would set CS=0000, that means the stack was corrupted.
			-- But only fix this during early boot (isolinux stage1), NOT after ldlinux loaded.
			-- After ldlinux, CS=00E8 is valid and should not be overwritten.
			if newcs == 0x0000 then
				-- Only apply this fix during early isolinux (before CS went beyond 9BF0)
				-- If CPU was at 9BF0 or earlier before this INT, fix the CS
				-- If CPU was at CS=00E8 or similar (ldlinux running), leave it alone
				-- Heuristic: if we haven't seen CS > 0x1000 yet, we're in isolinux stage1
				local cur_cs_before = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]  -- this is already F000 (fake BIOS)
				-- Check what's on the stack one level deeper (the original caller's CS)
				local sp_now = CPU_REGS[5]
				local ss_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[3] * 16
				-- FLAGS was just popped, so stack now points to FLAGS word
				-- Actually: we popped IP, CS, FLAGS in order → stack is back to original
				-- The original caller was pushed as: IP | CS | FLAGS (LIFO)
				-- We haven't popped FLAGS yet, so peek at it
				-- Actually we did pop old_flags already, stack is now clean
				-- Just fix if still in early boot (no ldlinux yet = CS < 0x0200)
				if not _G._ldlinux_loaded then
					if _G._isolinux_relocated then
						newcs = 0x9BF0
					elseif _G.EMU.diskData then
						newcs = 0x07C0
					end
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[BIOS-IRET-FIX] CS=0000 corrected to %04X IP=%04X", newcs, newip))
				else
					-- ldlinux is running - CS=0000 is likely a real return after guest IRET
					-- Don't correct it; if it causes issues, the guest code handles it
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[BIOS-IRET] CS=0000 IP=%04X (ldlinux running, not correcting)", newip))
				end
			end
			CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = newcs
			local old_flag_mask = 0x0200
			CPU_FLAGS = (CPU_FLAGS -band- (bnot-old_flag_mask)) -bor- (old_flags -band- old_flag_mask)
			return true
		else
			return "block"
		end
	end

	-- ⭐ INSTRUCTION TRACE BUFFER: record last 64 instructions for crash diagnosis
	do
		local tr = _G._cs_trap_trace
		if not tr then tr = {} ; _G._cs_trap_trace = tr end
		local cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
		local ip = CPU_IP
		local phys = cs*16+ip
		local b0 = (phys < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys) or 0)
		local entry = string.format("CS=%04X IP=%04X OP=%02X AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SP=%04X SS=%04X DS=%04X",
			cs, ip, b0, CPU_REGS[1], CPU_REGS[4], CPU_REGS[2], CPU_REGS[3],
			CPU_REGS[5], CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_SEGMENTS[4])
		tr[#tr+1] = entry
		if #tr > 64 then table.remove(tr, 1) end
	end

	local opcode = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_advance_ip()

	-- In 32-bit pmode (CS.D=1, ip_mask=0xFFFFFFFF), default operand size is 32-bit.
	-- Prefer opcode_map32[opcode]; fall back to opcode_map[opcode] for unimplemented 32-bit ops.
	local om
	if ip_mask == 0xFFFFFFFF then
		om = opcode_map32[opcode] or opcode_map[opcode]
	else
		om = opcode_map[opcode]
	end

	if om ~= nil then
		local result = om(opcode)
		if result == "block" then
			return "block"  -- HLT: special case, pass through
		elseif result == false then
			-- opcode handler returned false — log and continue rather than killing emulator
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[!] Opcode %02X handler returned false at CS=%04X IP=%04X — continuing", opcode, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], (CPU_IP-1) -band- 0xFFFF))
			return true
		else
			return true
		end
	else
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[!] Invalid Opcode %02X at CS=%04X IP=%04X", opcode, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], (CPU_IP-1) -band- 0xFFFF))
		cpu_print_state(opcode)
		cpu_emit_interrupt(6, false)
		return true
	end
end

function cpu_emit_interrupt(v, nmi)
	nmi = (v == 2)
	if nmi then
		table.insert(CPU_INTQUEUE, v + 256)
	else
		table.insert(CPU_INTQUEUE, v)
	end
	CPU_HASINT = true
end

-- ⭐ INT 0: Divide by Zero — recover gracefully instead of crashing to garbage CS
-- ldlinux may trigger this if malloc result (SI) is accidentally 0 when used as divisor
cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x00, function(ax,ah,al)
	emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT0] Divide by zero at CS=%04X IP=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X AX=%04X",
		CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_REGS[7], CPU_REGS[8], CPU_REGS[1]))
	-- If ldlinux running (CS=00E8) and SI=0, the malloc result was zero — skip the bad DIV
	-- Set SI to a safe non-zero scratch address so subsequent DIV SI works
	if CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0x00E8 then
		if CPU_REGS[7] == 0 then
			CPU_REGS[7] = 0x1016  -- same alloc ptr we used in TLOOP fix
			emu_debug(1, "[INT0] ldlinux DIV/0: patched SI=0x1016, resuming")
		end
		-- Don't push return addr for INT 0 — just return true (handled) and retry
		-- The DIV instruction will re-execute with corrected SI
		return true
	end
	-- ⭐ FIX: CS=9020 IP=0100에서 반복되는 DIV/0 — NUCLEAR 루프 부작용
	-- setup.bin이 보호모드 진입 시도 중 GDT/IDT 설정 과정에서 발생
	-- IP를 넘겨서 계속 진행하게 함 (setup.bin은 INT 0 handler를 0x0000:0x0000으로 가정)
	if CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0x9020 and CPU_IP >= 0x00FF and CPU_IP <= 0x0110 then
		-- IP=0100은 setup.bin의 'hlt' 루프 인근 — 그냥 IP 전진
		CPU_IP = 0x0102  -- 다음 명령으로 건너뜀
		emu_debug(1, "[INT0] setup.bin @9020:0100 DIV/0 → skipping, IP=0102")
		return true
	end
	-- For other contexts: standard real-mode behavior (don't handle, let IVT run)
	return false
end)

-- invalid opcode interrupt
cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x06, function(ax,ah,al)
	-- dummy - override by user
	return true
end)

-- keyboard interrupt
cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x09, function(ax,ah,al)
	-- dummy - override by user
	return true
end)

_G.EMU.upd_count = function(last_clock)
    local perf = _G.EMU.PERF
	perf.opc_avg_i = (perf.opc_avg_i + 1) % 20
	perf.opc_avg[perf.opc_avg_i + 1] = ((perf.opc - perf.last_opc) / (perf.clock - last_clock))

	local oa = 0
	local oac = 0
	for i=1,20 do
		if perf.opc_avg[i] then
			oa = oa + perf.opc_avg[i]
			oac = oac + 1
		end
	end

	emu_debug(2, (oa / oac) .. " IPS")
	perf.last_opc = perf.opc
end

_G.EMU.upd_tick = function(cv)
    local perf = _G.EMU.PERF
	local last_clock = perf.clock
	perf.clock = cv

	if pit_tick then pit_tick(perf.clock) end
	platform_kbd_tick()
	-- handle OC waits
	cv = tick()
	if (cv - perf.clock) < 0.05 then
		perf.oc_tick_i = perf.oc_tick_i + 1
		if perf.oc_tick_i >= 50 then
			perf.oc_tick_i = 0
			_G.EMU.upd_count(last_clock)
		end
	end
	
	-- handle pc speaker
	if (kbd_get_spkr_latch() -band- 0x03) == 0x03 then
		local pch = pit_channel(3)
		if (pch.mode == 2 or pch.mode == 3 or pch.mode == 6 or pch.mode == 7) and (pch.reload_set_lo and pch.reload_set_hi) then
			local freq = (1.19318 * 1000000) / (pch.reload or 1)
			platform_beep(freq, 0.05)
		end
	end
	perf.clock = tick()
end

-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Higher frame budget + faster render for TinyCore GUI usability
-- Roblox Heartbeat fires ~60fps (16.6ms per frame)
-- We use 15ms for CPU (giving 1.6ms headroom for Roblox engine)
FRAME_BUDGET  = 0.040  -- 40ms CPU budget per Heartbeat frame (Pentium III speed optimization)
RENDER_EVERY  = 3      -- kept for compat; actual render is time-based below
cpu_heartbeat_conn = nil

_G.EMU.cpu_execute = function()
	execute = true
	local hlt_logged = false
	-- stall detector: time-based
	local stall_cs = -1
	local stall_ip = -1
	local stall_count = 0
	local stall_last_change = tick()
	local STALL_TIME = 3.0
	-- periodic heartbeat log: every 5s print CS:IP regardless (catch fast loops)
	local periodic_last = tick()
	local PERIODIC_TIME = 5.0
	-- ⭐ tight-loop detector: ring buffer of last N CS:IP pairs to detect multi-address cycles
	local tloop_buf = {}   -- ring buffer: stores cs*65536+ip values
	local tloop_buf_size = 16
	local tloop_buf_i = 0
	local tloop_last_inject = 0
	local TLOOP_INJECT_INTERVAL = 2.0  -- inject IRQ0 every 2s when tight-loop detected

	-- CPU execution: Heartbeat (every frame, CPU only)
	cpu_heartbeat_conn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
		if not execute then
			cpu_heartbeat_conn:Disconnect()
			platform_error("execution stopped\n")
			return
		end

		local frame_start = tick()

		-- ⭐⭐ ldlinux.c32 ZERO-CODE DETECTOR (v2):
		-- ldlinux.c32 relocated itself to high memory (e.g. A80B) but after relocation
		-- it may far-jump to a stale segment (e.g. 662E) that has no code.
		-- Strategy:
		--   1. Track last known "good" CS (where we saw real non-zero code while _ldlinux_loaded)
		--   2. If OPC=00 00 00 for 3+ frames AND CS != last good CS → we jumped to bad segment
		--   3. Restore CS to last good CS, reset IP=0
		--   4. Also handle the original A000+ case (first relocation)
		do
			local _ldc_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] or 0
			-- ⭐⭐ INSTANT VRAM ESCAPE: CS>=0xA000 is ALWAYS bad (VRAM/ROM) — escape immediately
			-- Do NOT wait for zero_count>=3. Every cycle in VRAM corrupts SP via IRQ nesting.
			if _ldc_cs >= 0xA000 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
				if not _G._vram_escape_frame then _G._vram_escape_frame = 0 end
				_G._vram_escape_frame = _G._vram_escape_frame + 1
				-- Mask IRQ immediately on FIRST frame in VRAM to stop SP growth
				if _G._vram_escape_frame == 1 then
					if _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
						_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.bor(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0x01)
					end
					CPU_HASINT = false
					print(string.format("[VRAM-ESCAPE] CS=%04X entered VRAM range! Masking IRQ immediately.", _ldc_cs))
				end
				-- After 3 frames still in VRAM → force CS back to safe segment
				if _G._vram_escape_frame >= 3 then
					-- Find best restore target: check known ldlinux segments for code
					local _restore_cs = nil
					local _ldlinux_segs = {0x00E8, 0x00DB, 0x00C3, 0x00AB, 0x0093, 0x007B, 0x0063, 0x004B, 0x0033, 0x0100, 0x0200}
					-- First try last good CS
					if _G._ldc_good_cs then
						local gp = _G._ldc_good_cs * 16
						if gp < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, gp) ~= 0 then
							_restore_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs
						end
					end
					-- Fallback: scan known ldlinux segments
					if not _restore_cs then
						for _, seg in ipairs(_ldlinux_segs) do
							local sp2 = seg * 16
							if sp2 < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sp2) ~= 0 then
								_restore_cs = seg
								break
							end
						end
					end
					_restore_cs = _restore_cs or 0x00E8
					print(string.format("[VRAM-ESCAPE] Forcing CS=%04X -> %04X IP=0000 SP=0x7BC0 (frame#%d)",
						_ldc_cs, _restore_cs, _G._vram_escape_frame))
					CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _restore_cs
					CPU_IP = 0x0000
					CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BC0  -- reset SP to clean value
					-- ⭐⭐ Zero out the stack area above SP to prevent IRET picking up garbage values
					-- Stack grows downward from 0x7BC0; clear 0x7BC0~0x7FFF (typical ldlinux stack region)
					if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
						for _si = 0x7BC0, 0x7FFF do
							buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _si, 0x00)
						end
					end
					-- Also reset SS=0x0000 to standard real mode
					CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x0000
					CPU_HASINT = false
					-- ⭐ Flush interrupt queue — stale IRQs from VRAM loop must not fire at restored CS
					while #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
					_G._ldc_zero_count = 0
					_G._ldc_reloc_attempted = false
					_G._vram_escape_frame = 0
					-- Re-enable IRQ after short delay
					task.delay(1.5, function()
						if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
							_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.band(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0xFE)
						end
						print(string.format("[VRAM-ESCAPE] IRQ re-enabled, CS now=%04X", CPU_SEGMENTS and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] or 0))
					end)
				end
			else
				_G._vram_escape_frame = 0  -- reset counter when in safe range
			end

			if _G._ldlinux_loaded and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
				local _ldc_phys = _ldc_cs * 16 + (CPU_IP or 0)
				local _ldc_b0, _ldc_b1, _ldc_b2 = 0, 0, 0
				if _ldc_phys < 134217728 then
					_ldc_b0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _ldc_phys)
					_ldc_b1 = _ldc_phys+1 < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _ldc_phys+1) or 0
					_ldc_b2 = _ldc_phys+2 < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _ldc_phys+2) or 0
				end

				-- FIX: for ldlinux seg pool 0100-1FFF, scan 32 bytes to avoid false zero-code eviction
				local _ldc_nonzero = (_ldc_b0 ~= 0 or _ldc_b1 ~= 0 or _ldc_b2 ~= 0)
				if not _ldc_nonzero and _ldc_cs >= 0x0100 and _ldc_cs <= 0x1FFF and _ldc_phys+31 < 134217728 then
					for _sc=3,31 do if buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _ldc_phys+_sc) ~= 0 then _ldc_nonzero=true; break end end
				end
				if _ldc_nonzero then
					-- Real code here: record this as a good CS
					-- Only record as good_cs if it's a plausible ldlinux segment
					-- (NOT very low segments like 003B which are IVT/BDA stubs,
					--  NOT 9BF0 which is isolinux stage1, NOT 07C0 which is boot sector)
					_G._ldc_zero_count = 0
					-- ⭐ FIX: Exclude VRAM/ROM range (A000+) and very-low segs from good_cs
					-- CS=A80B is VRAM (0xA0000-0xBFFFF) — contains null bytes, never executable code
					if _ldc_cs >= 0x00E0 and _ldc_cs < 0xA000 and _ldc_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and _ldc_cs ~= 0x07C0 then
						_G._ldc_good_cs = _ldc_cs
					end
