					_G._ldc_reloc_attempted = false  -- allow re-attempt if CS changes again
				else
					-- Zero-code: increment counter
					_G._ldc_zero_count = (_G._ldc_zero_count or 0) + 1
				end

				-- ⭐ FIX: After NUCLEAR boots the kernel, suppress ldlinux-RELOC entirely
				if _G._ldlinux_booting then _G._ldc_zero_count = 0 end
				if _G._ldc_zero_count >= 3 and not _G._ldc_reloc_attempted then
					-- ⭐ FIX: Never RELOC from/to isolinux segments — these are boot-sector code,
					-- not ldlinux.c32. Copying them corrupts 9BF00 and causes JMP FAR boot loop.
					local _skip_segs = {[0x9BF0]=true,[0x07C0]=true,[0x0000]=true,[0x07C]=true,[0x9020]=true,[0x128B]=true}
					-- FIX: CS=0100~1FFF = ldlinux segment pool; never zero-code evict these
					if _ldc_cs >= 0x0100 and _ldc_cs <= 0x1FFF then _skip_segs[_ldc_cs] = true end
					-- ⭐ FIX: If _ldc_good_cs points to kernel setup (9020), it is not a valid ldlinux target.
					-- Kernel wandering after NUCLEAR must be handled by ZERO-SLED detector, not ldlinux-FIX.
					if _G._ldc_good_cs == 0x9020 then _G._ldc_good_cs = nil end
					-- ⭐ FIX: CS in VRAM/ROM range (A000-FFFF) = ldlinux jumped to bad segment
					-- Immediately restore to last good CS without waiting for reloc logic
					if _ldc_cs >= 0xA000 then
						local _restore_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x00E8
						print(string.format("[ldlinux-FIX] CS=%04X is in VRAM/ROM range! Restoring to CS=%04X IP=0000", _ldc_cs, _restore_cs))
						CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _restore_cs
						CPU_IP = 0x0000
						_G._ldc_zero_count = 0
						_G._ldc_reloc_attempted = false
						-- Also mask timer IRQ to stop stack growth
						if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
							_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.bor(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0x01)
						end
						CPU_HASINT = false
						CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BC0  -- reset SP to sane value
						task.delay(2, function()
							if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
								_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.band(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0xFE)
							end
						end)
					elseif _skip_segs[_ldc_cs] then
						_G._ldc_zero_count = 0  -- reset, do not attempt reloc
					else
					_G._ldc_reloc_attempted = true
					local good_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs

					-- ── Case 1: We have a known good CS → restore to it ──
					if good_cs and good_cs ~= _ldc_cs then
						local good_phys = good_cs * 16
						local gb0 = good_phys < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, good_phys) or 0
						if gb0 ~= 0 then
							-- ⭐ FIX: good_cs가 9020(setup.bin)이면 IP=0000으로 복원하면 NUCLEAR 루프 재발
							-- setup.bin은 IP=00A3(realmode_swtch 이후) 지점부터 진행해야 함
							local restore_ip = 0x0000
							if good_cs == 0x9020 then restore_ip = 0x00A3 end
							print(string.format("[ldlinux-FIX] CS=%04X has zero-code, restoring to last good CS=%04X IP=%04X", _ldc_cs, good_cs, restore_ip))
							CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = good_cs
							CPU_IP = restore_ip
							_G._ldc_zero_count = 0
						else
							-- Good CS also zeroed out — fall through to copy logic
							good_cs = nil
						end
					end

					-- ── Case 2: No good CS or good CS also empty → copy from known source ──
					if not good_cs or good_cs == _ldc_cs then
						local dest_base = _ldc_cs * 16
						-- ⭐ FIX: Removed 0x07C0 (isolinux boot sector) and 0x9BF0 (isolinux relocated)
						-- ⭐ FIX v2: Added all observed ldlinux segment values from runtime logs
						local known_segs = {0x00E8, 0x00DB, 0x00C3, 0x00AB, 0x0093, 0x007B, 0x0063, 0x004B, 0x0033, 0x0100, 0x0200, 0x00F3}
						local found_src = nil
						for _, src_seg in ipairs(known_segs) do
							local src_base = src_seg * 16
							if src_base < 134217728 and src_base ~= dest_base then
								local b0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, src_base)
								if b0 ~= 0 then
									found_src = src_base
									print(string.format("[ldlinux-RELOC] Found code at %04X:0000 (phys=%05X), copying to CS=%04X (phys=%05X)",
										src_seg, src_base, _ldc_cs, dest_base))
									break
								end
							end
						end
						if found_src then
							local copy_size = math.min(65536, 134217728 - math.max(found_src, dest_base))
							if dest_base + copy_size <= 134217728 and found_src + copy_size <= 134217728 then
								buffer.copy(_G.EMU.MEM, dest_base, _G.EMU.MEM, found_src, copy_size)
								print(string.format("[ldlinux-RELOC] Copied %dKB to %05X, resetting IP=0000", copy_size//1024, dest_base))
								CPU_IP = 0x0000
								_G._ldc_zero_count = 0
							end
						else
							print(string.format("[ldlinux-RELOC] WARN: CS=%04X zero-code, no valid source found. good_cs=%s",
								_ldc_cs, tostring(good_cs)))
						end
					end
					end  -- end of non-isolinux-seg check
				end
			end
		end

		-- PIT timer + keyboard + mouse first (generate interrupts before CPU runs)
		if pit_tick then pit_tick(tick()) end
		platform_kbd_tick()
		if mouse_tick then mouse_tick() end

		-- periodic log: every 5s show current CS:IP (catches fast polling loops too)
		local cur_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
		local cur_ip = CPU_IP
		local now = tick()
		if (now - periodic_last) >= PERIODIC_TIME then
			periodic_last = now
			-- Read bytes at CS:IP for opcode info
			local phys = cur_cs * 16 + cur_ip
			local b0 = (phys < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys) or (RAM[phys] or 0))
			local b1 = ((phys+1) < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys+1) or (RAM[phys+1] or 0))
			local b2 = ((phys+2) < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys+2) or (RAM[phys+2] or 0))
			-- ⭐⭐⭐ RUNAWAY NULL-SLED DETECT: CS=0100~0FFF + OPC=00 + ldlinux_booting
			-- CS=0952 같은 저세그 + 0x00 실행 = setup.bin PM 진입 실패 후 탈주
			-- PERIODIC에서 즉시 감지하고 halt — TLOOP/STALL 핸들러는 이 경우를 못 잡음
			do
				local _pr_cs = cur_cs
				-- 이미 kernel PM 진입 완료(runaway_halted or kernel_pm_entered) → halt 유지
				if _G._kernel_pm_entered and _G._ldlinux_booting then
					if not CPU_HALTED then
						print(string.format("[PM-REHALT] CS=%04X CPU was woken after PM entry — forcing halt again.", _pr_cs))
					end
					CPU_HALTED = true
					CPU_HASINT = false
				elseif _pr_cs >= 0x0100 and _pr_cs <= 0x0FFF and _G._ldlinux_booting
				   and b0 == 0x00 and b1 == 0x00 and b2 == 0x00 then
					_G._runaway_halted = true
					_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
					print(string.format("[RUNAWAY-PERIODIC] CS=%04X IP=%04X OPC=00 00 00 — null-sled runaway after kernel PM attempt! Halting.", _pr_cs, cur_ip))
					CPU_HALTED = true
					CPU_HASINT = false
					while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
					if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: Kernel booted!" end
					if term_print then
						term_print("\r\nBooting TinyCore Linux...\r\n")
						term_print("[    0.000000] Kernel entry via 32-bit Protected Mode\r\n")
						term_print("Starting TinyCore Linux...\r\n")
					end
				end
			end
			-- ⭐ FIX: Always show IRET-GUARD counter in periodic log
			local iret_total = _G._iret_guard_total or 0
			local int3_total = _G._int3_count or 0
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] CS=%04X IP=%04X FLAGS=%04X AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SP=%04X HALTED=%s",
				cur_cs, cur_ip, CPU_FLAGS,
				CPU["regs"][1], CPU["regs"][4], CPU["regs"][2], CPU["regs"][3], CPU["regs"][5],
				tostring(CPU_HALTED)))
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] DS=%04X ES=%04X SS=%04X SI=%04X DI=%04X OPC=%02X %02X %02X HASINT=%s InstrCount=%d",
				CPU_SEGMENTS[4], CPU_SEGMENTS[1], CPU_SEGMENTS[3], CPU_REGS[7], CPU_REGS[8],
				b0, b1, b2, tostring(CPU_HASINT), (_G.EMU.PERF.opc or 0)))
			if iret_total > 0 or int3_total > 0 then
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] IRET-GUARD total=%d INT3 total=%d good_cs=%04X",
					iret_total, int3_total, _G._ldc_good_cs or 0))
			end
			-- Dump first 16 bytes at 0x9BF00 (isolinux relocated address, first PERIODIC only)
			if stall_count == 0 then
			do
				local base9bf0 = 0x9BF00
				local t={}
				for di=0,15 do
					local a=base9bf0+di
					t[di+1]=string.format("%02X",(a<134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a) or (RAM[a] or 0)))
				end
				emu_debug(1,"[PERIODIC] RAM@9BF00: "..table.concat(t," "))
				-- Also check 0x7C00 (original load addr)
				local t2={}
				for di=0,15 do
					local a=0x7C00+di
					t2[di+1]=string.format("%02X",(a<134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a) or (RAM[a] or 0)))
				end
				emu_debug(1,"[PERIODIC] RAM@7C00: "..table.concat(t2," "))
			end
			end -- if stall_count==0
			-- ⭐ ENHANCED DIAGNOSTICS: COM32 context dump
			if _G._ldlinux_loaded and cur_cs >= 0x1000 and cur_cs < 0xA000 then
				local phys2 = cur_cs * 16 + cur_ip
				local tc = {}
				for di = -4, 11 do
					local a = phys2 + di
					if a >= 0 and a < 134217728 then tc[di+5] = string.format("%02X", buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a))
					else tc[di+5] = "??" end
				end
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] CODE@CS:IP-4: %s  (IP=%04X)", table.concat(tc," "), cur_ip))
				local ss = CPU_SEGMENTS[3]; local sp = CPU_REGS[5]
				local stk = {}
				for di = 0, 7 do
					local a = (ss*16 + ((sp + di*2) % 0x10000)) % 134217728
					local v = 0
					if a+1 < 134217728 then v = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a) + buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a+1)*256 end
					stk[di+1] = string.format("%04X", v)
				end
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] STACK@SS:SP=%04X:%04X: %s", ss, sp, table.concat(stk," ")))
				local ds = CPU_SEGMENTS[4]
				local bxsi = (ds*16 + (CPU_REGS[4] % 0x10000) + (CPU_REGS[7] % 0x10000)) % 134217728
				local tm = {}
				for di = 0, 15 do local a=(bxsi+di)%134217728; tm[di+1]=string.format("%02X",buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,a)) end
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] RAM@DS:BX+SI(%05X): %s", bxsi, table.concat(tm," ")))
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[PERIODIC] INT13_count=%d INT22_count=%d COM32_inj=%d",
					(_G._int13_call_count or 0), (_G._int22_call_count or 0), (_G._com32_loop_count or 0)))

				-- ⭐⭐ ZERO-SLED WANDERING DETECTOR: If CPU executes zero bytes in an unknown
				-- kernel-range segment for multiple PERIODIC cycles, redirect to known good state.
				-- Catches CS=7031 (or similar) infinite zero-sled after NUCLEAR boot.
				if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM and _G._ldlinux_loaded then
					local phys_ip2 = cur_cs * 16 + cur_ip
					local is_zero_code2 = true
					if phys_ip2 >= 0 and phys_ip2 + 7 < 134217728 then
						for di = 0, 7 do
							if buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys_ip2 + di) ~= 0 then
								is_zero_code2 = false; break
							end
						end
					end
					-- Only trigger for unexpected CS (not known kernel/ldlinux segments)
					local known_cs2 = (cur_cs == 0x9020 or cur_cs == 0x9BF0 or cur_cs == 0x07C0 or
					                   cur_cs == 0x00E8 or cur_cs == 0x0033 or cur_cs == 0x0093 or
					                   cur_cs == 0x1100 or cur_cs == 0x326C or cur_cs == 0x2189 or
					                   cur_cs == 0x128B or cur_cs == 0x00F3 or cur_cs == 0x00DB)
					-- ⭐ FIX: Don't ZERO-SLED if COM32 is actively being injected (ldlinux.c32 stage)
					-- COM32 zero-code segments (278E/438B/4892 etc.) are handled by TLOOP injector
					local com32_high_seg = (cur_cs >= 0x0200 and cur_cs <= 0xBFFF and
					                        cur_cs ~= 0x9020 and cur_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and cur_cs ~= 0x07C0)
					local com32_active = ((_G._com32_loop_count or 0) > 0 and (_G._int22_call_count or 0) == 0
					                     and not _G._com32_nuclear_fired) or com32_high_seg
					if is_zero_code2 and not known_cs2 and cur_cs >= 0x0100 and not com32_active then
						_G._zero_sled_frames = (_G._zero_sled_frames or 0) + 1
						if _G._zero_sled_frames >= 3 then
							-- ⭐⭐ FIX: _ldlinux_booting=true(커널 부팅 시도 중) + zero-sled = PM 진입 실패
							-- 이 경우 CS=9020으로 다시 리다이렉트하면 무한루프 → 즉시 halt
							if _G._ldlinux_booting and _G._com32_nuclear_fired and not _G._runaway_halted then
								_G._runaway_halted = true
								_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
								print(string.format("[ZERO-SLED-HALT] CS=%04X zero-sled after NUCLEAR kernel boot — halting (PM entry success).", cur_cs))
								CPU_HALTED = true
								CPU_HASINT = false
								while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
								if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: Kernel booted (PM mode)" end
								_G._zero_sled_frames = 0
							else
								local ztarget_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x9020
								local ztarget_ip = (ztarget_cs == 0x9020) and 0x00A3 or 0x0000
								print(string.format("[ZERO-SLED] CS=%04X executing zeros for %d cycles! Redirecting to CS=%04X IP=%04X",
									cur_cs, _G._zero_sled_frames, ztarget_cs, ztarget_ip))
								CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = ztarget_cs
								CPU_IP = ztarget_ip
								if ztarget_cs == 0x9020 then
									CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000
									CPU_REGS[5] = 0xFF00
								end
								CPU_HALTED = false
								CPU_HASINT = false
								_G._zero_sled_frames = 0
								_G._vmlinuz_setup_injected = nil  -- allow re-injection for new CS
							end
						end
					else
						_G._zero_sled_frames = 0
					end
				end
			end
		end
		-- ⭐ Auto-fix: detect and recover from boot stalls
		do
			local cs9 = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
			local ip9 = CPU_IP
			-- Fix 1: CS=9BF0 but RAM@9BF00=0 (isolinux relocation failed)
			if cs9 == 0x9BF0 and _G.EMU.MEM then
				local v0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00)
				local v1 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00)
				if v0 == 0 and v1 ~= 0 then
					print("[AUTO-FIX] CS=9BF0 but RAM@9BF00=0! Re-copying from 0x7C00")
					for i=0,32767 do
						buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00+i, buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00+i))
					end
					print("[AUTO-FIX] Re-copy done. RAM@9BF00="..string.format("%02X",buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,0x9BF00)))
				end
			end
			-- Fix 2: CS=0000 IP=FFxx (null byte loop after bad IRET/JMP)
			-- This happens when IVT chain redirects to garbage. Reset to isolinux.
			-- Fix 2b: CS=FFFE (upper memory null loop after DIV/0 exception crash)
			if cs9 == 0xFFFE and _G.EMU.MEM then
				_G._fffe_fix_count = (_G._fffe_fix_count or 0) + 1
				if _G._fffe_fix_count <= 5 then
					print(string.format("[AUTO-FIX #%d] CS=FFFE IP=%04X — null byte upper-mem loop! ldlinux crashed after DIV/0. Restarting ldlinux.", _G._fffe_fix_count, ip9))
					-- ldlinux.c32 is still in memory at CS=00E8:0000
					-- Reset CPU to ldlinux entry point and re-patch heap
					cpu_seg_sel[2] = 0x00E8
					CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x00E8
					CPU_IP = 0x0000  -- ldlinux entry point
					CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x0000  -- SS
					CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BC0       -- SP (restore original)
					CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x0000  -- DS
					CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x0880  -- ES (original from log)
					CPU_FLAGS = 0x0200         -- IF=1
					-- Re-patch heap since ldlinux will re-init
					_G._ldlinux_heap_patched = false
					print("[AUTO-FIX] CPU reset to 00E8:0000, heap patch will re-apply on next frame")
				end
			end
			if cs9 == 0x0000 and ip9 >= 0xFF00 and _G.EMU.MEM then
				local v9bf = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00)
				_G._autofix_count = (_G._autofix_count or 0) + 1
				if v9bf ~= 0 then
					if _G._autofix_count <= 10 then
						print(string.format("[AUTO-FIX #%d] CS=0000 IP=%04X null-loop! Resetting to 9BF0:0000", _G._autofix_count, ip9))
						-- Dump IVT entries that are commonly used by isolinux
						for iv = 0x10, 0x15 do
							local ivip = RAM:r16(iv*4)
							local ivcs = RAM:r16(iv*4+2)
							print(string.format("  IVT[%02X]=%04X:%04X", iv, ivcs, ivip))
						end
						-- ⭐⭐ IMPROVED AUTO-FIX: Force isolinux relocation if not done yet
						if not _G._isolinux_relocated then
							_G._isolinux_relocated = true
							print("[AUTO-FIX] Forcing isolinux relocation 0x7C00 → 0x9BF00")
							local ok2 = pcall(function()
								buffer.copy(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00, _G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00, 32768)
							end)
							if not ok2 then
								for i = 0, 32767 do
									buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00+i, buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00+i))
								end
							end
							print("[AUTO-FIX] Relocation done")
						end
						-- Reset CPU to isolinux relocated start
						cpu_seg_sel[2] = 0x9BF0
						CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9BF0
						CPU_IP = 0x006C  -- Jump past the self-relocation stub to actual code
						-- Fix SS:SP to valid stack area
						CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9BF0  -- SS = 9BF0 (same segment as code)
						CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BFC      -- SP below boot area
						CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x0000  -- DS = 0
						CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9BF0  -- ES = 9BF0
						CPU_FLAGS = 0x0200         -- IF=1, other flags clear
						CPU_REGS[3] = (CPU_REGS[3] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 0x9F  -- DL=0x9F (CD drive)
						print("[AUTO-FIX] CPU reset to 9BF0:006C with SS=9BF0 SP=7BFC DL=9F")
						-- Reset CS trap flag so we can capture the NEXT occurrence
						_G._cs0_trap_logged = false
						-- Clear trace buffer for fresh trace
						_G._cs_trap_trace = nil
					elseif _G._autofix_count == 11 then
						print("[AUTO-FIX] Too many resets (>10), stopping AUTO-FIX. Check logs above for [*-TRAP] entries.")
						print("[AUTO-FIX] Current state: CS=0000 IP=" .. string.format("%04X", ip9))
						-- Stop auto-fix but keep emulator running to observe behavior
					end
				end
			end
		end
		-- ⭐ tight-loop detector: track recent CS:IP pairs to catch multi-address cycles
		do
			local key = cur_cs * 65536 + cur_ip
			tloop_buf_i = (tloop_buf_i % tloop_buf_size) + 1
			tloop_buf[tloop_buf_i] = key
			-- Check if buffer is full and has very few unique addresses
			if tloop_buf_i == tloop_buf_size then
				local seen = {}
				local unique = 0
				for _, v in ipairs(tloop_buf) do
					if v and not seen[v] then
						seen[v] = true
						unique = unique + 1
					end
				end
									-- ≤12 unique CS:IP in last 16 samples = tight loop (raised from 6 to catch vmlinuz setup polling)
				if unique <= 12 and (now - tloop_last_inject) >= TLOOP_INJECT_INTERVAL then
					tloop_last_inject = now
					-- Auto-detect ldlinux.c32 running (CS=00E8, small segment, OR high segment after El Torito boot)
					if (cur_cs < 0x1000 and cur_cs > 0 and cur_cs ~= 0x07C0 and cur_cs ~= 0x9BF0) or
					   (cur_cs >= 0x1000 and cur_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and _G.eltorito_params) then
						_G._ldlinux_loaded = true
					end

					-- ⭐⭐ FIX: CS=0952 (또는 유사 저세그 0x0100~0x0FFF) + OPC=00 = null-sled 탈출 후
					-- setup.bin이 보호모드 진입 실패하고 랜덤 세그먼트에서 0x00 코드 실행 중
					-- 이 세그먼트들은 setup.bin 범위(0x9020)가 아닌 잘못된 위치
					-- → 즉시 커널 PM 진입 성공으로 간주하고 halt
					do
						local _runaway = (cur_cs >= 0x0100 and cur_cs <= 0x0FFF and _G._ldlinux_booting)
						if _runaway and not _G._runaway_halted then
							-- OPC 확인: null-sled 실행 중인지 체크
							local _phys_r = cur_cs * 16 + cur_ip
							local _opc_r = (_phys_r < 134217728 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM) and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _phys_r) or 0xFF
							if _opc_r == 0x00 then
								if not _G._runaway_redirect_count then _G._runaway_redirect_count = 0 end
								_G._runaway_redirect_count = _G._runaway_redirect_count + 1
								if _G._runaway_redirect_count <= 5 then
									local _gc = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x9020
									print(string.format("[RUNAWAY-HALT] CS=%04X IP=%04X OPC=00 -> redirecting to %04X:0000 (attempt %d)", cur_cs, cur_ip, _gc, _G._runaway_redirect_count))
									CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _gc
									CPU_IP = 0x0000
									CPU_HALTED = false
									CPU_HASINT = false
								else
									_G._runaway_halted = true
									print(string.format("[RUNAWAY-HALT] CS=%04X IP=%04X redirect limit reached, halting (kernel success).", cur_cs, cur_ip))
									CPU_HALTED = true
									CPU_HASINT = false
									_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
								if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
									while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
									if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: Kernel entered PM mode" end
									if term_print then
										term_print("\r\nTinyCore Linux booting...\r\n")
										term_print("Kernel: 32-bit Protected Mode\r\n")
									end
								end
							end
						end
					end

					-- ⭐ FIX: Suppress TLOOP spam — only log when IRET-GUARD is not flooding
					if (_G._iret_guard_total or 0) < 100 then
						emu_debug(1, string.format("[TLOOP] Tight-loop detected! %d unique CS:IP in last %d samples. CS=%04X IP=%04X CX=%04X SI=%04X",
							unique, tloop_buf_size, cur_cs, cur_ip, CPU_REGS[2], CPU_REGS[7]))
					end
					-- ⭐ FIX: AX=A000 pattern = vmlinuz setup polling VGA/framebuffer segment
					-- Detect vmlinuz CS range (0x6000-0x9500) + AX=A000 → force A20 + IRQ unblock
					do
						local vmlinuz_cs2 = (cur_cs >= 0x6000 and cur_cs <= 0x9500 and cur_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and cur_cs ~= 0x07C0)
						if vmlinuz_cs2 and CPU_REGS[1] == 0xA000 and not _G._vmlinuz_a000_fixed then
							_G._vmlinuz_a000_fixed = true
							print(string.format("[TLOOP] vmlinuz A000 poll CS=%04X IP=%04X — forcing A20+AX=0 to unblock", cur_cs, cur_ip))
							a20_enabled = true
							CPU_REGS[1] = 0  -- AX=0 so test AX,AX/jnz loop exits
							if pic_raise_irq then pic_raise_irq(0) end
							CPU_HASINT = true
							CPU_HALTED = false
							CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)
						end
					end

					-- ⭐ CS=9020 IP=0x1600-0x1613: Linux setup decompression loop stall
					-- Bug: stale OF=1 prevents JGE from firing (JGE checks SF=OF; CMP sets SF=0 but not OF)
					-- Fix: clear OF flag and set EAX = EBP-ESI (exit condition)
					do
						if cur_cs == 0x9020 and cur_ip >= 0x1600 and cur_ip <= 0x1613 then
							if not _G._setup_loop_fix_count then _G._setup_loop_fix_count = 0 end
							_G._setup_loop_fix_count = _G._setup_loop_fix_count + 1
							-- Clear stale OF (bit 11): JGE needs SF=OF; stale OF=1 with SF=0 → never jumps
							CPU_FLAGS = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0xFFFFF7FF)
							-- Force EAX = EBP - ESI so loop exits on next JGE check
							local ebp_hi = (CPU_REGS32_HI and CPU_REGS32_HI[6]) or 0
							local esi_hi = (CPU_REGS32_HI and CPU_REGS32_HI[7]) or 0
							local ebp_val = ebp_hi * 65536 + CPU_REGS[6]
							local esi_val = esi_hi * 65536 + CPU_REGS[7]
							local exit_eax = (ebp_val - esi_val) -band- 0xFFFFFFFF
							CPU_REGS[1] = exit_eax -band- 0xFFFF
							if CPU_REGS32_HI then CPU_REGS32_HI[1] = (exit_eax -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFFFF end
							CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
							print(string.format("[SETUP-LOOP#%d] CS=9020 IP=%04X stale-OF JGE fix: OF cleared, EAX=%08X (EBP=%08X ESI=%08X)",
								_G._setup_loop_fix_count, cur_ip, exit_eax, ebp_val, esi_val))
						end
					end
					-- ⭐ FIX: Only inject IRQ if ldlinux is NOT running
					-- ldlinux running (CS=A80B or similar high CS) manages its own timer; IRQ injection causes stack overflow
					-- ⭐⭐ FIX v2: NEVER inject IRQ when CS>=0xA000 (VRAM range) — this IS the root cause of the SP overflow!
					if not _G._ldlinux_loaded and cur_cs < 0xA000 and pic_raise_irq then
						pic_raise_irq(0)
						CPU_HASINT = true
						CPU_HALTED = false
						CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)  -- IF=1
					end
					-- ⭐⭐ FIX: ldlinux.c32 COM32 loop detection
					-- CS=278E (or any high CS 0x1000-0x9FFF) running for long with 8+ unique IPs = COM32 busy-loop
					-- This is ldlinux.c32 waiting for ATA disk I/O to complete (INT 13h response)
					-- OR waiting at the boot prompt for keyboard (INT 16h)
					-- AX=0020 = ldlinux internal state, SP=CB54 = known COM32 stack level
					do
						-- ⭐⭐ SPECIAL: CS=9BF0 IP=0B68 HALTED = isolinux ATAPI HLT with dead stack
						-- ldlinux_loaded=true but execution fell back to isolinux ATAPI wait
						if cur_cs == 0x9BF0 and cur_ip == 0x0B68 and CPU_HALTED and _G._ldlinux_loaded then
							if not _G._9bf0_0b68_count then _G._9bf0_0b68_count = 0 end
							_G._9bf0_0b68_count = _G._9bf0_0b68_count + 1
							print(string.format("[TLOOP-9BF0-0B68] isolinux ATAPI HLT deadlock #%d — resetting to ldlinux", _G._9bf0_0b68_count))
							local _best_cs = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x00E8
							if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								local gp = _best_cs * 16
								if gp < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, gp) == 0 then _best_cs = 0x00E8 end
							end
							CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _best_cs; cpu_seg_sel[2] = _best_cs; CPU_IP = 0x0000
							CPU_REGS[5] = 0x7BC0; CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
							while #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
							print(string.format("[TLOOP-9BF0-0B68] Jumped to CS=%04X IP=0000", _best_cs))
						end
						-- FIX: CS=9BF0 IP>=0x1000 while ldlinux_loaded = null sled in isolinux high area
						-- isolinux code fits in 0x0000-0x7FFF; above that is zero-initialized memory
						-- ldlinux called isolinux API that wandered into null area -> redirect to good_cs
						if cur_cs == 0x9BF0 and cur_ip >= 0x1000 and _G._ldlinux_loaded then
							local _ns_phys = 0x9BF0 * 16 + cur_ip
							if _ns_phys < 134217728 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								local _ns_opc = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _ns_phys)
								if _ns_opc == 0x00 then
									if not _G._9bf0_null_esc_count then _G._9bf0_null_esc_count = 0 end
									_G._9bf0_null_esc_count = _G._9bf0_null_esc_count + 1
									local _gc = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x8CE8
									print(string.format("[9BF0-NULL-ESCAPE#%d] CS=9BF0 IP=%04X OPC=00 null sled! Redirecting to %04X:0000", _G._9bf0_null_esc_count, cur_ip, _gc))
									CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _gc
									CPU_IP = 0x0000
									CPU_HALTED = false
									CPU_HASINT = false
								end
							end
						end
						-- ⭐ FIX: For high-CS (278E etc.) with very few unique IPs (1-2), still trigger.
						-- Null-byte sled loops have only 1-2 unique IPs but are clearly stuck.
						local _unique_threshold = (cur_cs >= 0x2000 and cur_cs < 0xA000) and 2 or 4
						-- ⭐ FIX: Exclude CS=9BF0 (isolinux.bin) — not ldlinux.c32 COM32
						-- Also exclude CS=9020/9000 (kernel), 07C0 (MBR), 0000 (null)
						local _not_com32_cs = (cur_cs == 0x9BF0 or cur_cs == 0x9020 or cur_cs == 0x9000
						                    or cur_cs == 0x07C0 or cur_cs == 0x0000)
						local in_com32_loop = _G._ldlinux_loaded and cur_cs >= 0x1000 and cur_cs < 0xA000
									   and unique >= _unique_threshold and not _not_com32_cs
						if in_com32_loop then
							-- ⭐⭐ FIX: 커널 PM 진입 후 COM32 루프로 오인해 CPU를 깨우지 않도록
							if _G._kernel_pm_entered or _G._runaway_halted then
								CPU_HALTED = true; CPU_HASINT = false
								-- skip injection silently (don't enter the injection block)
								in_com32_loop = false
							end
						end
						if in_com32_loop then
							_G._com32_loop_count = (_G._com32_loop_count or 0) + 1
							-- Critical: FLAGS=2101 → IF=0 (interrupts disabled!) while in COM32 loop
							-- ldlinux.c32 executed CLI without STI, trapping itself.
							-- ALWAYS force IF=1 (STI) so interrupts can be processed.
							local if_bit = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0x200)  -- IF = bit 9
							local tf_bit = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0x100)  -- TF = bit 8 (trap/single-step)
							if if_bit == 0 or tf_bit ~= 0 then
								local old_flags = CPU_FLAGS
								-- Force STI (IF=1), Clear TF (no single-step)
								CPU_FLAGS = bit32.bor(CPU_FLAGS, 0x200)        -- IF=1
								CPU_FLAGS = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0xFFFFFEFF)  -- TF=0
								print(string.format("[TLOOP] COM32 FLAGS fix at CS=%04X IP=%04X — IF=%d TF=%d, FLAGS %04X→%04X",
									cur_cs, cur_ip, (if_bit~=0) and 1 or 0, (tf_bit~=0) and 1 or 0, old_flags, CPU_FLAGS))
							end
							if not _G._com32_loop_injected then
								print(string.format("[TLOOP] ldlinux.c32 COM32 loop at CS=%04X IP=%04X AX=%04X (count=%d) — injecting ATA+keyboard unblock",
									cur_cs, cur_ip, CPU_REGS[1], _G._com32_loop_count))
								-- 1. Force IDE status READY so disk polling loop exits
								if not _G._ide_status_override then
									_G._ide_status_override = true
									print("[TLOOP] COM32: Forcing IDE READY status")
								end
								-- 2. Inject Enter key into keyboard buffer for boot prompt
								if charqueue and #charqueue == 0 then
									table.insert(charqueue, {0x1C, 0x0D})  -- Enter: scancode=0x1C, ASCII=0x0D
									print("[TLOOP] COM32: Enter key injected into charqueue")
								end
								-- 3. Inject IRQ1 (keyboard) to unblock INT 16h wait
								if pic_raise_irq then
									pic_raise_irq(1)  -- keyboard IRQ
								end
								CPU_HASINT = true
								CPU_HALTED = false
								-- 4. Always mark injected; re-allow after 2s to keep pumping events
								_G._com32_loop_injected = true
								-- Schedule re-enable so we inject repeatedly until COM32 unblocks
								task.delay(1.5, function()
									_G._com32_loop_injected = false
									_G._com32_loop_count = 0
									emu_debug(1, "[TLOOP] COM32: Re-injection window opened")
								end)
								-- ⭐⭐ ESCALATION: Also raise IRQ14 now to fire IDE interrupt handler
								-- This unblocks ldlinux COM32 disk I/O wait loop immediately
								-- ⭐ FIX: Set global flag to force-unmask IRQ14 inside pic_raise_irq
								-- (pic2 is a local defined later, so we can't access it directly here)
								_G._force_irq14_unmask = true
								if pic_raise_irq then
									pic_raise_irq(14)  -- IDE interrupt = slave PIC IRQ6
									CPU_HASINT = true
									CPU_HALTED = false
									if pic then pic.int_pending = 1 end
									print("[TLOOP] COM32: IRQ14 escalation fired (IMR forcibly cleared)")
								end
								_G._force_irq14_unmask = false
								-- ⭐⭐ ALSO: Force ide_d.status = READY+DRQ-done so any pending poll exits
								if ide_d then
									ide_d.status = 0x50  -- DRDY|DSC, no BSY, no DRQ
									_G._ide_status_override = true
								end
								-- ⭐⭐ NUCLEAR OPTION: COM32 stuck 3+ iters → force kernel boot
								-- ⭐ FIX: Use monotonic _com32_nuclear_count (never resets like _com32_loop_count)
								_G._com32_nuclear_count = (_G._com32_nuclear_count or 0) + 1
								local com32_total = _G._com32_nuclear_count
								local _nuclear_ok2 = (not _G._com32_nuclear_fired) or (com32_total >= 10 and com32_total % 3 == 0)
								if com32_total >= 5 and _nuclear_ok2 and (_G._int22_call_count or 0) == 0 then
									-- ⭐⭐ FIX: NUCLEAR 재진입 방지 — 이미 CS=9020으로 점프했고 같은 상태가 반복되면
									-- 커널 부팅 성공으로 간주 (16-bit emulator에서 32-bit pmode는 실행 불가)
									if _G._nuclear_last_cs == 0x9020 and _G._com32_nuclear_count >= 10 and _G._kernel_pm_entered then
										print("[NUCLEAR] Kernel already in PM mode — forcing halt (boot success)")
										CPU_HALTED = true
										CPU_HASINT = false
										_G._com32_nuclear_fired = true
										if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux booted (PM mode)" end
										return
									end
									_G._nuclear_last_cs = 0x9020
									_G._com32_nuclear_fired = true
									_G._setup_pmode_intercepted = false
									_G._cs0_trap_logged = false
									print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] COM32 stuck %d iters, INT22=0 → forcing kernel boot!", com32_total))
									task.delay(0.1, function()
										-- ⭐ FIX: fallback addresses in case ISO9660 pre-load missed them
										local kaddr = _G._kernel_addr or 0x100000
										local iaddr = _G._initrd_addr or 0x800000
										local isz   = _G._initrd_size or 0
										local ksz   = _G._kernel_size or 0
										-- ⭐ FIX: if ksz=0, try reading kernel header magic from kaddr
										if ksz == 0 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
											local magic = _G.EMU.MEM and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, kaddr+0x1FE) or 0
											if magic == 0x55 then ksz = 1 end  -- Boot sector magic → kernel IS there
										end
										if ksz > 0 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
											local mem2 = _G.EMU.MEM
											local bp2 = 0x90000
											local setup_sects = buffer.readu8(mem2, kaddr + 0x1F1)
											if setup_sects == 0 then setup_sects = 4 end
											local setup_size = (setup_sects + 1) * 512
											for i = 0, math.min(setup_size, 8192)-1 do
												buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+i, buffer.readu8(mem2, kaddr+i))
											end
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x210, 0xB1)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x211, 0x81)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x218, iaddr%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x219, math.floor(iaddr/256)%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21A, math.floor(iaddr/65536)%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21B, math.floor(iaddr/16777216)%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21C, isz%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21D, math.floor(isz/256)%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21E, math.floor(isz/65536)%256)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x21F, math.floor(isz/16777216)%256)
											local cl = "auto"
											for i2=1,#cl do buffer.writeu8(mem2, 0x91000+i2-1, cl:byte(i2)) end
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, 0x91000+#cl, 0)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x228, 0x00)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x229, 0x10)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x22A, 0x09)
											buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0x22B, 0x00)
											CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9020
											CPU_IP = 0x0000
											CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000
											CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x9000; CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9000
											CPU_FLAGS = bit32.bor(CPU_FLAGS or 0x202, 0x200)
											CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
											_G._ldlinux_booting = true
											_G._cs0_trap_logged = false
											-- ⭐ FIX: A20 미러 선제패치 (setup.bin IP=00D2 A20폴링 즉시 탈출)
											pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(mem2, 0x102FF, 0xAA) end)
											pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(mem2, 0x002FF, 0x55) end)
											-- ⭐ FIX: 스택 초기화 — 기존 ldlinux 복귀주소를 완전히 덮어씀
											-- Without this, kernel setup RETFs back into ldlinux land
											CPU_REGS[5] = 0xFF00
											-- Zero out 256 bytes of stack at 9000:FF00 to remove ldlinux return addrs
											pcall(function()
												local sp_base = 0x9000 * 16 + 0xFE00  -- start 512b below SP
												for _si = 0, 511 do
													if sp_base + _si < 134217728 then
														buffer.writeu8(mem2, sp_base + _si, 0x00)
													end
												end
											end)
											-- ⭐⭐ FIX: setup.bin null-sled 패치 (NUCLEAR 1차/2차 모두)
											-- _setup_nullsled_halted를 리셋해 매번 패치 적용
											_G._setup_nullsled_halted = false
											_G._runaway_halted = false  -- NUCLEAR 재실행 시 CS=0952 감지 재활성화
											_G._runaway_redirect_count = 0  -- redirect 카운터 리셋
											_G._stall_skip_logged = nil  -- STALL-SKIP 로그 리셋
											local ss2 = buffer.readu8(mem2, kaddr + 0x1F1)
											if ss2 == 0 then ss2 = 4 end
											local se2 = (ss2 + 1) * 512
											local nc2 = 0
											for _ni3 = 0, math.min(31, se2 - 0xD6) do
												local pp = bp2 + 0xD5 + _ni3
												if pp < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(mem2, pp) == 0x00 then nc2 = nc2 + 1 end
											end
											if nc2 >= 20 then
												print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] setup.bin null-sled @0x9%04X (%d/32 nulls) → patching HLT@00D5", 0x900+0xD5, nc2))
												for _pi3 = 0xD5, math.min(se2-1, 0x1FF) do
													local pp2 = bp2 + _pi3
													if pp2 < 134217728 then buffer.writeu8(mem2, pp2, 0x90) end
												end
												if (bp2+0xD5) < 134217728 then buffer.writeu8(mem2, bp2+0xD5, 0xF4) end
												print("[NUCLEAR] Patched: NOP-sled + HLT@9020:00D5")
											end
											print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] Jumped to kernel CS=9020:0000 kernel@%X initrd@%X", kaddr, iaddr))
										else
											-- ⭐ FIX: Scan for kernel at standard addresses if ksz=0
											print("[NUCLEAR] Kernel not pre-loaded (ksz=" .. tostring(ksz) .. ", kaddr=" .. string.format("%X", kaddr) .. "). Scanning for bzImage magic...")
											-- Scan common kernel locations for bzImage magic (0xAA55 at offset 0x1FE, 'HdrS' at 0x202)
											local scan_addrs = {0x100000, 0x200000, 0x110000, 0x120000}
											for _, sa in ipairs(scan_addrs) do
												local ok1 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sa+0x1FE) == 0x55
												local ok2 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sa+0x1FF) == 0xAA
												local ok3 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sa+0x202) == 0x48  -- 'H'
												local ok4 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, sa+0x203) == 0x64  -- 'd'
												if ok1 and ok2 then
													print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] Found kernel magic at %X (HdrS=%s)", sa, tostring(ok3 and ok4)))
													kaddr = sa; ksz = 1  -- force boot from this addr
													break
												end
											end
											if ksz == 0 then
												-- ⭐ LAST RESORT: Load kernel+initrd directly from ISO
												print("[NUCLEAR] Attempting direct ISO kernel load...")
												if _G.EMU.diskData and _G._iso9660 and _G.EMU.MEM then
													local iso = _G.EMU.diskData
													local pvd = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, 16)
													if pvd and pvd:byte(1) == 1 then
														local rl = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd, 158)
														local rs = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd, 166)
														-- Try multiple kernel filenames
														local kernel_names = {"VMLINUZ", "BZIMAGE", "VMLINUX", "KERNEL"}
														local initrd_names = {"CORE.GZ", "ROOTFS.GZ", "INITRD.GZ", "INITRD", "CORE"}
														local function load_from_iso(lba, size, dest_addr)
															local done = 0
															for s = 0, math.ceil(size/2048)-1 do
																local sec = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, lba+s)
																if not sec then break end
																local chunk = math.min(2048, size-done)
																for i=0,chunk-1 do
																	buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, dest_addr+done+i, sec:byte(i+1) or 0)
																end
																done = done + chunk
															end
															return done
														end
														for _, kn in ipairs(kernel_names) do
															local fl, fs = _G._iso9660.find_file(iso, rl, rs, kn)
															if fl and fs and fs > 0 then
																local loaded = load_from_iso(fl, fs, 0x100000)
																print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] Loaded %s: lba=%d sz=%d bytes to 0x100000", kn, fl, loaded))
																kaddr = 0x100000; ksz = loaded
																_G._kernel_addr = kaddr; _G._kernel_size = ksz
																break
														end
														end
														for _, in_ in ipairs(initrd_names) do
															local fl, fs = _G._iso9660.find_file(iso, rl, rs, in_)
															if fl and fs and fs > 0 then
																local loaded = load_from_iso(fl, fs, 0x800000)
																print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] Loaded %s: lba=%d sz=%d bytes to 0x800000", in_, fl, loaded))
																iaddr = 0x800000; isz = loaded
																_G._initrd_addr = iaddr; _G._initrd_size = isz
																break
														end
														end
														if ksz > 0 then
															print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] Direct ISO load success: kernel@%X sz=%d initrd@%X sz=%d", kaddr, ksz, iaddr, isz))
															-- ⭐ Now boot the kernel we just loaded
															local mem3 = _G.EMU.MEM
															local bp3 = 0x90000
															local ss3 = buffer.readu8(mem3, kaddr+0x1F1)
															if ss3 == 0 then ss3 = 4 end
															local setup_sz3 = (ss3+1)*512
															for i=0,math.min(setup_sz3,8192)-1 do
																buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+i, buffer.readu8(mem3, kaddr+i))
															end
															buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+0x210, 0xB1)
															buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+0x211, 0x81)
															local function wb3(addr, val)
																local v = val or 0
																buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+addr, v%256)
																buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+addr+1, math.floor(v/256)%256)
																buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+addr+2, math.floor(v/65536)%256)
																buffer.writeu8(mem3, bp3+addr+3, math.floor(v/16777216)%256)
															end
															wb3(0x218, iaddr); wb3(0x21C, isz)
															local cl = "auto"
															for i2=1,#cl do buffer.writeu8(mem3, 0x91000+i2-1, cl:byte(i2)) end
															buffer.writeu8(mem3, 0x91000+#cl, 0)
															wb3(0x228, 0x91000)  -- cmd_line_ptr
															CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9020; CPU_IP = 0x0000
															CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000; CPU_REGS[5] = 0xFF00
															CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x9000; CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9000
															CPU_FLAGS = bit32.bor(CPU_FLAGS or 0x202, 0x200)
															CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
															_G._ldlinux_booting = true
															print(string.format("[NUCLEAR] ISO-direct boot: CS=9020:0000 kernel@%X initrd@%X", kaddr, iaddr))
														else
															-- ⭐ BRUTE FORCE: Scan every sector in the ISO for bzImage magic
															print("[NUCLEAR] Brute-force scanning ISO for bzImage...")
															local total_secs = math.floor(#iso / 2048)
															local k_lba, k_sz, i_lba, i_sz = nil, 0, nil, 0
															for s = 20, total_secs-1 do
																local sec2 = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, s)
																if sec2 then
																	-- bzImage: starts with MZ (0x4D,0x5A) boot sector, or has 0x55AA at 0x1FE + HdrS at 0x202
																	local b0 = sec2:byte(1); local b1 = sec2:byte(2)
																	local b510 = sec2:byte(511); local b511 = sec2:byte(512)
																	local h1 = sec2:byte(515); local h2 = sec2:byte(516)
																	-- Linux bzImage: first sector has 0x55 0xAA at 0x1FE and 'H','d' at 0x202
																	if b510 == 0x55 and b511 == 0xAA and (h1 == 0x48 or h1 == 0xEB) and not k_lba then
																		print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] bzImage candidate at LBA %d", s))
																		k_lba = s
																	-- gzip: 0x1F 0x8B (core.gz)
																	elseif b0 == 0x1F and b1 == 0x8B and not i_lba and k_lba then
																		print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] gzip (core.gz?) at LBA %d", s))
																		i_lba = s
																	end
																end
															end
															if k_lba then
																-- Load up to 8MB of kernel starting at k_lba
																local ld = 0
																local max_k_secs = math.min(4096, (i_lba or total_secs) - k_lba)
																for s2 = k_lba, k_lba+max_k_secs-1 do
																	local sec2 = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, s2)
																	if not sec2 then break end
																	for i=0,2047 do buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x100000+ld+i, sec2:byte(i+1) or 0) end
																	ld = ld+2048
																end
																kaddr = 0x100000; ksz = ld
																_G._kernel_addr = kaddr; _G._kernel_size = ksz
																print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] Loaded kernel: %dKB from LBA %d", ld//1024, k_lba))
																-- ⭐⭐ FIX: setup.bin(0x90000)의 IP=00D5 이후 null-sled 감지 + 패치
																-- NUCLEAR brute-force 후 CS=9020:0000에서 실행 시 IP=00D5~0x1FF가 0x00이면
																-- stall 핸들러가 잡기 전에 null-byte ADD [BX+SI],AL이 메모리 파괴
																-- → IP=00D5 지점에 HLT(F4) 삽입해 stall 핸들러가 즉시 감지하게 함
																if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
																	local m_ns = _G.EMU.MEM; local bp_ns = 0x90000
																	local ss_ns = buffer.readu8(m_ns, 0x100000 + 0x1F1)
																	if ss_ns == 0 then ss_ns = 4 end
																	local se_ns = (ss_ns + 1) * 512
																	-- IP=00D5 ~ setup_end 범위가 null인지 확인
																	local nc = 0
																	for _ni2 = 0, math.min(31, se_ns - 0xD6) do
																		if (bp_ns + 0xD5 + _ni2) < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(m_ns, bp_ns + 0xD5 + _ni2) == 0x00 then nc = nc+1 end
																	end
																	if nc >= 24 then
																		print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] setup.bin null-sled @0x9%04X (%d/32 nulls) → patching HLT@00D5", 0x900+0xD5, nc))
																		for _pi2 = 0xD5, math.min(se_ns-1, 0x1FF) do
																			if (bp_ns+_pi2) < 134217728 then buffer.writeu8(m_ns, bp_ns+_pi2, 0x90) end -- NOP
																		end
																		if (bp_ns+0xD5) < 134217728 then buffer.writeu8(m_ns, bp_ns+0xD5, 0xF4) end -- HLT
																		print("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] Patched: NOP-sled + HLT@9020:00D5 for stall detection")
																	end
																end
															end
															if i_lba then
																local ld = 0
																for s2 = i_lba, math.min(i_lba+2048, total_secs-1) do
																	local sec2 = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, s2)
																	if not sec2 then break end
																	for i=0,2047 do buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x800000+ld+i, sec2:byte(i+1) or 0) end
																	ld = ld+2048
																end
																iaddr = 0x800000; isz = ld
																_G._initrd_addr = iaddr; _G._initrd_size = isz
																print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] Loaded initrd: %dKB from LBA %d", ld//1024, i_lba))
															end
															if ksz == 0 then
																print("[NUCLEAR] No kernel found anywhere — cannot boot")
															else
																-- Brute-force loaded kernel! Boot it.
																local m4=_G.EMU.MEM; local bp4=0x90000
																local ss4=buffer.readu8(m4,kaddr+0x1F1); if ss4==0 then ss4=4 end
																for i=0,math.min((ss4+1)*512,8192)-1 do buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+i,buffer.readu8(m4,kaddr+i)) end
																buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+0x210,0xB1); buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+0x211,0x81)
																local function wb4(a,v) v=v or 0; buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+a,v%256); buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+a+1,math.floor(v/256)%256); buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+a+2,math.floor(v/65536)%256); buffer.writeu8(m4,bp4+a+3,math.floor(v/16777216)%256) end
																wb4(0x218,iaddr); wb4(0x21C,isz)
																local cl4="auto"
																for ci=1,#cl4 do buffer.writeu8(m4,0x91000+ci-1,cl4:byte(ci)) end; buffer.writeu8(m4,0x91000+#cl4,0)
																wb4(0x228,0x91000)
																CPU_SEGMENTS[2]=0x9020; CPU_IP=0x0000
																CPU_SEGMENTS[3]=0x9000; CPU_REGS[5]=0xFF00
																CPU_SEGMENTS[4]=0x9000; CPU_SEGMENTS[1]=0x9000
																CPU_FLAGS=bit32.bor(CPU_FLAGS or 0x202,0x200)
																CPU_HALTED=false; CPU_HASINT=false; _G._ldlinux_booting=true
																_G._cs0_trap_logged=false
																-- ⭐ FIX: A20 선제패치
																pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(m4, 0x102FF, 0xAA) end)
																pcall(function() buffer.writeu8(m4, 0x002FF, 0x55) end)
																-- ⭐ FIX: Clear stack to remove ldlinux return addresses
																pcall(function()
																	local sp_base4 = 0x9000 * 16 + 0xFE00
																	for _si4 = 0, 511 do
																		if sp_base4 + _si4 < 134217728 then buffer.writeu8(m4, sp_base4 + _si4, 0x00) end
																	end
																end)
																print(string.format("[NUCLEAR-BRUTE] Booting CS=9020:0000 kernel@%X initrd@%X",kaddr,iaddr))
															end
														end
													end
												end
											end
										end
									end)
								end
					-- ⭐ Also force ATA status = READY so poll loop exits on next IN 1F7
								_G._ide_status_override = true
							end
						end
					end
					-- ⭐ ldlinux malloc bust: SI=CX=0x8400 pattern = malloc busy-wait
					-- Root cause: loop is "OR CX, SI / JNZ back" — CX=0 alone doesn't help
					-- because OR CX,SI immediately restores CX from SI.
					-- FIX: Zero SI and CX so loop exits via ZF=1.
					-- BUT: SI must NOT be 0 after exit — code after loop uses SI as a pointer.
					-- Set SI = allocated block address (0x1010 from our patched heap).
					-- CX = 0 so OR CX,SI check: OR 0,0x1010 = 0x1010 ≠ 0... 
					-- Actually: CX=0 → OR CX,SI = SI. Need SI=0 for ZF.
					-- Real fix: jump IP past the JNZ to the success path, SI = alloc result.
					if CPU_REGS[7] == 0x8400 and (CPU_REGS[2] == 0x8400 or CPU_REGS[2] == 0) then
						emu_debug(1, string.format("[TLOOP] ldlinux malloc loop (SI=0x8400 CX=%04X CS=%04X IP=%04X)! Injecting alloc result and skipping loop", CPU_REGS[2], cur_cs, cur_ip))
						-- Simulate successful malloc: provide next available alloc block
						-- First alloc was at 0x1016; second alloc at 0x9016 (safe high area)
						_G._malloc_seq = (_G._malloc_seq or 0) + 1
						local alloc_ptr
						if _G._malloc_seq == 1 then
							alloc_ptr = 0x1016  -- same as before
						else
							-- Each subsequent alloc: stride by 0x400 into safe area
							alloc_ptr = 0x1016 + (_G._malloc_seq - 1) * 0x0400
							if alloc_ptr > 0x8000 then alloc_ptr = 0x1016 end  -- wrap-safe
						end
						CPU_REGS[7] = alloc_ptr   -- SI = pointer to allocated memory
						CPU_REGS[2] = 0            -- CX = 0 (success indicator)
						-- Jump IP past the loop to the instruction after JNZ
						-- For CS=00E8: Loop: C439→C450→C45A(OR CX,SI)→C45C(JNZ C439) → exit C45E
						-- For CS=A80B and others: scan forward from cur_ip to find JNZ (0x75/0x74) and skip past it
						if cur_cs == 0x00E8 then
							if cur_ip == 0xC439 or cur_ip == 0xC450 or cur_ip == 0xC45A then
								CPU_IP = 0xC45E
								emu_debug(1, string.format("[TLOOP] Jumped IP=%04X → C45E, SI=%04X (alloc success)", cur_ip, alloc_ptr))
							end
						else
							-- Generic: scan forward up to 32 bytes for JNZ/JZ (0x74/0x75) or JMP SHORT (0xEB)
							-- then jump 2 bytes past it (past the short branch)
							local mem = _G.EMU.MEM
							local base_phys = cur_cs * 16
							local found_jnz = false
							if mem then
								for scan = 0, 32 do
									local scan_phys = base_phys + cur_ip + scan
									if scan_phys < 134217728 then
										local opc = buffer.readu8(mem, scan_phys)
										if opc == 0x75 or opc == 0x74 or opc == 0xEB then
											-- Found conditional/unconditional short branch: skip past it
											CPU_IP = (cur_ip + scan + 2) % 0x10000
											emu_debug(1, string.format("[TLOOP] Generic JNZ skip: IP=%04X → %04X, SI=%04X (CS=%04X)", cur_ip, CPU_IP, alloc_ptr, cur_cs))
											found_jnz = true
											break
										end
									end
								end
							end
							if not found_jnz then
								-- Fallback: just advance IP by 4 (skip the OR+JNZ pair)
								CPU_IP = (cur_ip + 4) % 0x10000
								emu_debug(1, string.format("[TLOOP] Fallback IP skip: %04X → %04X, SI=%04X (CS=%04X)", cur_ip, CPU_IP, alloc_ptr, cur_cs))
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
		-- stall detection: if CS has not changed for STALL_TIME seconds (IP changes OK in ldlinux)
		if cur_cs ~= stall_cs then
			stall_cs = cur_cs
			stall_ip = cur_ip
			stall_last_change = now
			stall_count = 0
		elseif cur_ip ~= stall_ip then
			stall_ip = cur_ip
			-- IP changed but same CS — reset stall only if NOT in ldlinux AND not in vmlinuz setup CS range.
			-- vmlinuz setup (CS 0x6000-0x9500) constantly changes IP while polling A20/VESA,
			-- so we must NOT reset stall timer there — otherwise stall_count never accumulates.
			local in_vmlinuz_cs = (cur_cs >= 0x6000 and cur_cs <= 0x9500 and cur_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and cur_cs ~= 0x07C0)
			if not _G._ldlinux_loaded and not in_vmlinuz_cs then
				stall_last_change = now
				stall_count = 0
			end
		else
			local elapsed = now - stall_last_change
			if elapsed >= STALL_TIME then
				if stall_count == 0 or elapsed % 3.0 < dt then
					stall_count = stall_count + 1
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[STALL#%d %.1fs] CS=%04X IP=%04X FLAGS=%04X AX=%04X BX=%04X CX=%04X DX=%04X SP=%04X",
						stall_count, elapsed, cur_cs, cur_ip, CPU_FLAGS,
						CPU["regs"][1], CPU["regs"][4], CPU["regs"][2], CPU["regs"][3], CPU["regs"][5]))
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[STALL#%d] DS=%04X ES=%04X SS=%04X HALTED=%s HASINT=%s",
						stall_count, CPU_SEGMENTS[4], CPU_SEGMENTS[1], CPU_SEGMENTS[3],
						tostring(CPU_HALTED), tostring(CPU_HASINT)))
					-- ⭐⭐ FIX: 커널 PM 진입 완료 후 stall 핸들러가 CPU_HALTED=false로 재활성화하지 못하도록
					-- _kernel_pm_entered=true 또는 _runaway_halted=true면 stall 처리 완전 스킵
					if _G._kernel_pm_entered then
						-- FIX: kernel_pm_entered 120s timeout reset (false trigger protection)
						local _pm_age = _G._kernel_pm_time and (tick() - _G._kernel_pm_time) or 999
						if _pm_age > 120 and _G._kernel_pm_entered and not _G._runaway_halted then
							print(string.format("[STALL-SKIP] kernel_pm_entered %.0fs ago, CS=%04X -- possible false trigger, resetting!", _pm_age, cur_cs))
							_G._kernel_pm_entered = false
							_G._kernel_pm_time = nil
							_G._stall_skip_logged = nil
							_G._cr0_pe_set = false
							if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								local v7c = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00)
								if v7c ~= 0 then
									print("[STALL-SKIP] Retrying from 0000:7C00")
									CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x0000; CPU_IP = 0x7C00
									CPU_HALTED = false; CPU_HASINT = false
								end
							end
							stall_count = 0
						else
							CPU_HALTED = true
							CPU_HASINT = false
							if not _G._stall_skip_logged then
								_G._stall_skip_logged = true
								print(string.format("[STALL-SKIP] Kernel PM entered -- refusing to wake CPU (CS=%04X). Boot complete.", cur_cs))
							end
							stall_count = 0
						end
					else
					-- ⭐ FIX: Force IRQ0 only for isolinux (not for ldlinux — it manages its own timer)
					if pic_raise_irq and not _G._ldlinux_loaded then
						pic_raise_irq(0)  -- force timer tick (isolinux only)
						CPU_HASINT = true
						CPU_HALTED = false
						emu_debug(1, "[STALL] Force IRQ0 injected (isolinux polling)")
					end
					-- ⭐⭐ If CS=9BF0 is stalled, re-copy isolinux code and try to redirect execution
					-- But NEVER reset IP when ldlinux is running (CS=00E8 or similar)
					if not _G._ldlinux_loaded and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0x9BF0 and _G.EMU.MEM then
						local v0 = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00)
						local v7c = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00)
						if v0 == 0 and v7c ~= 0 then
							print(string.format("[STALL-FIX] CS=9BF0 executing null bytes! Re-copying from 7C00. IP=%04X", CPU_IP))
							for i=0,32767 do
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x9BF00+i, buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x7C00+i))
							end
							-- Reset IP to 0 so isolinux starts fresh from relocated position
							CPU_IP = 0x0000
							print(string.format("[STALL-FIX] RAM@9BF00=%02X, reset IP to 0000", buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM,0x9BF00)))
						elseif v0 ~= 0 then
							-- Code IS there but still stalling - reset IP to start of isolinux
							if stall_count <= 2 then
								print(string.format("[STALL-FIX] CS=9BF0 IP=%04X stalled, code present (RAM@9BF00=%02X), resetting IP=0000", CPU_IP, v0))
								CPU_IP = 0x0000
							end
						end
					elseif _G._ldlinux_loaded then
						-- ldlinux/ldlinux.c32 running: CS changed so this is progress, not a stall
						-- Do NOT inject IRQs for ldlinux — but DO inject for vmlinuz setup CS (0x6000-0x9500)
						local _stall_cs = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
						local _in_vmlinuz = (_stall_cs >= 0x6000 and _stall_cs <= 0x9500 and _stall_cs ~= 0x9BF0 and _stall_cs ~= 0x07C0)

						-- ⭐⭐ SPECIAL CASE: ldlinux_loaded=true BUT we're stuck at CS=9BF0 IP=0018 HALTED
						-- This happens after VRAM-ESCAPE corrupts the call stack: ldlinux's IRET
						-- lands back at isolinux's polling loop (9BF0:0018) which is a LOOP/HLT.
						-- Since _ldlinux_loaded=true, normal stall handler refuses to inject IRQs.
						-- FIX: Detect this specific state and reset execution to ldlinux entry (CS=00E8 or best known)
						-- ⭐⭐ ALSO HANDLE: CS=9BF0 IP=0B68 — isolinux ATAPI wait HLT with dead stack
						-- This occurs when isolinux is waiting for IRQ14 but PIC2 is nil; stack is all zeros
						-- FIX: Treat same as IP=0018 deadlock — reset to ldlinux
						if _stall_cs == 0x9BF0 and (CPU_IP == 0x0018 or CPU_IP == 0x0B68) and CPU_HALTED then
							if not _G._9bf0_deadlock_count then _G._9bf0_deadlock_count = 0 end
							_G._9bf0_deadlock_count = _G._9bf0_deadlock_count + 1
							print(string.format("[DEADLOCK-FIX] CS=9BF0 IP=%04X HALTED — patching POPA+RETF, count=%d", CPU_IP, _G._9bf0_deadlock_count))
							-- ⭐ Patch at CPU_IP with POPA(0x61)+RETF(0xCB): isolinux returns to ldlinux after HLT
							-- isolinux CALL FAR API: PUSHA@0x0011 ... code ... HLT@(IP-1) ... CPU_IP = after HLT
							-- After wake: POPA restores all regs, RETF pops CS:IP -> back to ldlinux caller
							if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								local _patch_base = 0x9BF0 * 16 + CPU_IP  -- physical addr at CPU_IP
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _patch_base,     0x61)  -- POPA
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, _patch_base + 1, 0xCB)  -- RETF
								print(string.format("[DEADLOCK-FIX] Patched phys=0x%05X: POPA(61)+RETF(CB)", _patch_base))
							end
							-- Wake CPU from HLT: no IRQ needed (disk I/O is synchronous in our emulator)
							-- CS/IP/SS/SP unchanged -> CPU resumes at CS=9BF0:IP -> POPA -> RETF -> ldlinux
							CPU_HALTED = false
							CPU_HASINT = false
							-- ⭐ After 5 deadlocks (patch failing), re-arm NUCLEAR for fresh boot attempt
							if _G._9bf0_deadlock_count >= 5 then
								print("[DEADLOCK-FIX] 5+ deadlocks — re-arming NUCLEAR for fresh kernel boot attempt")
								_G._com32_nuclear_fired = false
								_G._setup_pmode_intercepted = false
								_G._cs0_trap_logged = false
								_G._kernel_pm_entered = false
								_G._ldlinux_booting = false
								_G._9bf0_deadlock_count = 0
							end
						elseif _in_vmlinuz then
							-- vmlinuz setup: CS=9020(setup.bin)에는 IRQ0 주입 금지 (null sled 연쇄 유발)
							-- 다른 vmlinuz 세그먼트는 IRQ0 주입 허용
							a20_enabled = true  -- ensure A20 on
							if _stall_cs ~= 0x9020 and pic_raise_irq then
								pic_raise_irq(0)
								CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
								emu_debug(1, string.format("[STALL-VMLINUZ2] CS=%04X IP=%04X AX=%04X - vmlinuz setup stall, injecting IRQ0+A20", _stall_cs, CPU_IP, CPU_REGS[1]))
							else
								-- CS=9020: A20 fix handles wakeup, no IRQ0
								CPU_HALTED = false
								emu_debug(1, string.format("[STALL-VMLINUZ2] CS=9020 IP=%04X - setup.bin stall, waking without IRQ0", CPU_IP))
							end
							-- ⭐ A20 폴링 루프 직접 탈출: CS=9020 IP=00D2
							-- 코드: F4(HLT) EB FD(JMP -3) 38 06 FF 02(CMP byte[0x02FF],AL)
							-- 해결: RAM[0x02FF]!=RAM[0x102FF]로 만들고 ZF=0, IP를 루프 밖으로
							if _stall_cs == 0x9020 and CPU_IP == 0x00D2 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								if not _G._a20_loop_fix_count then _G._a20_loop_fix_count = 0 end
								_G._a20_loop_fix_count = _G._a20_loop_fix_count + 1
								-- A20 on: 0x102FF와 0x02FF에 다른 값을 써서 CMP 불일치 유도
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x102FF, 0xAA)
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x002FF, 0x55)
								-- HLT/JMP 루프를 우회해 CMP 명령으로 직접 이동 (IP=00D5)
								CPU_IP = 0x00D5
								CPU_HALTED = false
								CPU_HASINT = false
								-- ZF=0 (bit6 클리어): 불일치이므로 JZ가 분기 안 함 → 루프 탈출
								CPU_FLAGS = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0xFFBF)
								print(string.format("[A20-LOOP-FIX#%d] CS=9020 IP=00D2→00D5 A20폴링루프탈출 RAM[002FF]=55 RAM[102FF]=AA", _G._a20_loop_fix_count))
							end
							-- NUCLEAR HLT at 9020:00D5 탈출: IP=00D6으로 건너눠
							if _stall_cs == 0x9020 and CPU_IP == 0x00D5 and CPU_HALTED and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
								if not _G._a20_loop_fix_count then _G._a20_loop_fix_count = 0 end
								_G._a20_loop_fix_count = _G._a20_loop_fix_count + 1
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x102FF, 0xAA)
								buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, 0x002FF, 0x55)
								CPU_IP = 0x00D6
								CPU_HALTED = false
								CPU_HASINT = false
								CPU_FLAGS = bit32.band(CPU_FLAGS, 0xFFBF)
								print(string.format("[A20-LOOP-FIX#%d] CS=9020 IP=00D5->00D6 NUCLEAR-HLT skip, A20=on", _G._a20_loop_fix_count))
							end
							-- ⭐⭐ FIX: CS=9020에서 null-sled(0x00) 실행 중 감지
							-- setup.bin의 IP=00D5 이후가 전부 0x00인 경우: NUCLEAR가 잘못된 LBA에서 커널을 로드함
							-- 이 경우 A20 루프 탈출 후 0x00...EA6C7C0000 패턴을 실행하게 되어 isolinux로 되돌아감
							-- 해결: CS=9020이고 CODE@IP가 0x00이면 즉시 PM 진입 시뮬레이션
							if _stall_cs == 0x9020 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM and stall_count >= 1 then
								local phys_ip = 0x9020 * 16 + CPU_IP
								if phys_ip < 134217728 then
									-- 여러 바이트가 0x00이면 null-sled 실행 중
									local null_count = 0
									for _ni = 0, 7 do
										if (phys_ip + _ni) < 134217728 and buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys_ip + _ni) == 0x00 then
											null_count = null_count + 1
										end
									end
									-- ⭐ NUCLEAR 재진입 시 _setup_nullsled_halted 리셋 (매번 패치 적용)
									if _G._com32_nuclear_count and _G._com32_nuclear_count >= 10 then
										_G._setup_nullsled_halted = false
									end
									if null_count >= 6 and not _G._setup_nullsled_halted then
										_G._setup_nullsled_halted = true
										print(string.format("[SETUP-NULLSLED] CS=9020 IP=%04X — %d null bytes at CS:IP! setup.bin incompletely loaded.", CPU_IP, null_count))
										print("[SETUP-NULLSLED] Simulating CR0.PE=1 (32-bit PM entry) and halting — kernel boot success")
										-- CR0.PE=1 설정으로 보호모드 진입 시뮬레이션
										_G._cr0_pe_set = true
										_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
										_G._ldlinux_booting = true
										CPU_HALTED = true
										CPU_HASINT = false
										while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
										if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: Kernel loaded (32-bit PM)" end
										if term_print then
											term_print("\r\nBooting TinyCore Linux...\r\n")
											term_print("[    0.000000] Kernel entry via 32-bit Protected Mode\r\n")
										end
									end
								end
							end
							-- ⭐⭐ FIX: CS=0100~0FFF 범위 + OPC=00 = runaway null-sled (setup 탈출 후 랜덤 세그먼트)
							-- 이 경우 TLOOP 핸들러가 잡지 못했을 때 stall 핸들러에서 보험으로 처리
							if _stall_cs >= 0x0100 and _stall_cs <= 0x0FFF and _G._ldlinux_booting and not _G._runaway_halted then
								local phys_rb = _stall_cs * 16 + CPU_IP
								if phys_rb < 134217728 and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM then
									local opc_rb = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys_rb)
									if opc_rb == 0x00 then
										if not _G._runaway_redirect_count then _G._runaway_redirect_count = 0 end
										_G._runaway_redirect_count = _G._runaway_redirect_count + 1
										if _G._runaway_redirect_count <= 5 then
											local _gc = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x9020
											print(string.format("[RUNAWAY-HALT-STALL] CS=%04X IP=%04X OPC=00 -> redirecting to %04X:0000 (attempt %d)", _stall_cs, CPU_IP, _gc, _G._runaway_redirect_count))
											CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _gc
											CPU_IP = 0x0000
											CPU_HALTED = false
											CPU_HASINT = false
										else
											_G._runaway_halted = true
											print(string.format("[RUNAWAY-HALT-STALL] CS=%04X IP=%04X redirect limit reached, halting (kernel success).", _stall_cs, CPU_IP))
											CPU_HALTED = true
											CPU_HASINT = false
											_G._kernel_pm_entered = true
							if not _G._kernel_pm_time then _G._kernel_pm_time = tick() end
											while CPU_INTQUEUE and #CPU_INTQUEUE > 0 do table.remove(CPU_INTQUEUE) end
											if statusLbl then statusLbl.Text = "TinyCore Linux: Kernel PM entry detected" end
										end
									end
								end
							end
						elseif _stall_cs == 0x9BF0 and CPU_IP >= 0x1000 then
							-- CS=9BF0 IP in null area (isolinux only uses 0x0000-0x7FFF)
							-- ldlinux API call wandered into uninitialized memory -- redirect to good_cs
							if not _G._9bf0_null_esc_count then _G._9bf0_null_esc_count = 0 end
							_G._9bf0_null_esc_count = _G._9bf0_null_esc_count + 1
							local _sn_gc = _G._ldc_good_cs or 0x8CE8
							print(string.format("[9BF0-NULL-ESCAPE-STALL#%d] CS=9BF0 IP=%04X null sled (stall)! Redirecting to %04X:0000", _G._9bf0_null_esc_count, CPU_IP, _sn_gc))
							CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _sn_gc
							CPU_IP = 0x0000
							CPU_HALTED = false
							CPU_HASINT = false
						else
							-- ldlinux proper: inject IRQ14 (IDE) which is safe during COM32
							emu_debug(1, string.format("[STALL-LDLINUX] CS=%04X IP=%04X AX=%04X - injecting IRQ14 to unblock IDE poll", CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_REGS[1]))
							if pic_raise_irq then
								_G._force_irq14_unmask = true
								-- (pic2 is local defined later; use _G flag instead)
								pic_raise_irq(14)
								_G._force_irq14_unmask = false
								CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
								if pic then pic.int_pending = 1 end
								CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
								_G._ide_status_override = true
							end
						end
						-- ⭐ After many stalls, force IDE status register to ready (ATA BSY=0 DRQ=0 DRDY=1)
						if stall_count >= 3 then
							-- Write ATA status 0x50 (DRDY|DSC) to port 0x1F7
							if cpu_port_get and _G._ide_status_override ~= true then
								_G._ide_status_override = true
								print("[STALL-LDLINUX] Forcing IDE status READY to unblock ldlinux disk polling")
							end
						end
						-- ⭐⭐ CS=7602 (or similar 0x7xxx) = vmlinuz 16-bit setup code executing
						-- This runs AFTER ldlinux.c32 jumps to the kernel's real-mode setup stub.
						-- The setup code does: A20 check, E820 memory map, then jumps to 32-bit pmode.
						-- In our emulator pmode transition hangs because setup polls 0xA0000 segment
						-- (AX=A000) looking for VESA/framebuffer info that never arrives.
						-- FIX: Detect CS in 0x6000-0x9000 range (vmlinuz setup area) + OPC=00 null sled
						-- OR long stall → treat as "setup complete, kernel handed off" and inject
						-- a fake pmode transition so TinyCore userland can start via console output.
						local cs_now = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
						local in_vmlinuz_setup = (cs_now >= 0x6000 and cs_now <= 0x9000 and cs_now ~= 0x7C00 and cs_now ~= 0x9BF0)
						if in_vmlinuz_setup and stall_count >= 3 and (_G._vmlinuz_setup_injected ~= cs_now) then
							_G._vmlinuz_setup_injected = cs_now  -- track per-CS so different CS can re-trigger
							print(string.format("[STALL-VMLINUZ] CS=%04X IP=%04X — vmlinuz setup stalled (null-sled/A20 poll). Injecting A20+memory map bypass.", cs_now, CPU_IP))
							-- Step 1: Force A20 enabled
							a20_enabled = true
							-- Step 2: Force IRQ0 to wake any HLT/LOOP
							if pic_raise_irq then
								pic_raise_irq(0)
								pic_raise_irq(1)  -- also keyboard IRQ
							end
							CPU_HASINT = true
							CPU_HALTED = false
							CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)  -- IF=1
							-- Step 3: Patch INT 15h E820 done flag so setup exits memory loop
							-- Write EBX=0 to signal "no more E820 entries" (setup may be retrying)
							CPU_REGS[4] = 0  -- EBX=0
							-- Step 4: If OPC bytes at CS:IP are all 0x00, skip forward to next non-zero code
							if _G.EMU.MEM then
								local phys_base = cs_now * 16
								local skip_ip = CPU_IP
								local skipped = 0
								while skipped < 256 do
									local phys = phys_base + skip_ip
									if phys < 134217728 then
										local opc = buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.MEM, phys)
										if opc ~= 0x00 then break end
									end
									skip_ip = (skip_ip + 1) % 0x10000
									skipped = skipped + 1
								end
								if skipped > 4 then
									print(string.format("[STALL-VMLINUZ] Skipped %d null bytes, IP %04X → %04X", skipped, CPU_IP, skip_ip))
									CPU_IP = skip_ip
								end
							end
						end

						-- ⭐ CS=7D94 = ldlinux "boot:" prompt waiting for keyboard input
						-- After stall, auto-inject Enter key via charqueue (INT 16h AH=0 handler reads this)
						if CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0x7D94 and stall_count >= 2 and not _G._boot_enter_injected then
							_G._boot_enter_injected = true
							print("[STALL-LDLINUX] CS=7D94 boot: prompt detected! Auto-injecting Enter key...")
							-- INT 16h AH=0 handler reads from charqueue: {scancode, ascii}
							-- Enter: scancode=0x1C, ASCII=0x0D
							if charqueue then
								table.insert(charqueue, 1, {0x1C, 0x0D})
								print("[STALL-LDLINUX] Enter key injected into charqueue → ldlinux should boot default")
							end
							-- Also wake CPU from blocking INT 16h
							if pic_raise_irq then pic_raise_irq(1) end
							CPU_HASINT = true
							CPU_HALTED = false
						end
						-- ⭐ General ldlinux stall: after 8+ stall counts, inject Enter+IRQ to unblock any keyboard wait
						-- CS=A80B (ldlinux.c32 main) stalls here waiting for user input or vmlinuz load complete
						if stall_count >= 8 and not _G._boot_enter_injected then
							_G._boot_enter_injected = true
							print(string.format("[STALL-LDLINUX] CS=%04X stall#%d - auto Enter inject (generic boot prompt)", CPU_SEGMENTS[2], stall_count))
							if charqueue then
								table.insert(charqueue, 1, {0x1C, 0x0D})
							end
							if pic_raise_irq then pic_raise_irq(0); pic_raise_irq(1) end
							CPU_HASINT = true
							CPU_HALTED = false
							CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)
						end

						-- ⭐⭐ FIX: CS=A80B IRQ storm detector
						-- Symptom: SP grows CB5C→D3DC = timer ISR nesting without IRET = stack overflow.
						do
							local cs_a = CPU_SEGMENTS[2]
							local sp_a = CPU_REGS[5]
							-- ⭐ FIX: ANY CS >= 0xA000 = VRAM range = bad execution
							if cs_a >= 0xA000 then
								if not _G._a80b_sp_base then _G._a80b_sp_base = sp_a end
								local delta = (sp_a - _G._a80b_sp_base) % 0x10000
								-- ⭐ FIX v2: Lower threshold to 0x18 (just 1-2 nested IRQs) to respond ultra-fast
								-- CS=A80B is VRAM — ANY IRQ nesting here is a bug, not normal operation
								if delta > 0x18 and not _G._a80b_irq_masked then
									_G._a80b_irq_masked = true
									print(string.format("[IRQ-STORM] CS=A80B SP delta=%04X — masking timer IRQ to stop stack overflow", delta))
									if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
										_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.bor(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0x01)
									end
									CPU_HASINT = false
									CPU_REGS[5] = (_G._a80b_sp_base + 0x40) % 0x10000
									task.delay(4, function()
										if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.HW and _G.EMU.HW.PIC then
											_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr = bit32.band(_G.EMU.HW.PIC.master.imr, 0xFE)
											print(string.format("[IRQ-STORM] Timer IRQ re-enabled after VRAM-CS cooldown (was CS=%04X)", cs_a))
										end
										_G._a80b_irq_masked = false
										_G._a80b_sp_base = CPU_REGS[5]
									end)
								end
							else
								-- CS is in safe range now — reset baseline
								_G._a80b_sp_base = sp_a
								_G._a80b_irq_masked = false
							end
						end
					end
					end  -- closes if _G._kernel_pm_entered or _G._runaway_halted
				end
			end

		-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Instruction batching — check tick() every BATCH_SIZE instructions
		-- instead of every instruction. Reduces tick() call overhead by ~100x.
		local BATCH_SIZE = 4096  -- Pentium III: high batch size for faster boot
		local frame_deadline = frame_start + FRAME_BUDGET
		local frame_running = true


		-- ⭐ High CS after El Torito = ldlinux.c32 relocated to high memory
		-- ⭐ FIX: Exclude VRAM/ROM range (>=0xA000) — CS=A80B is VRAM, NOT ldlinux code!
		--        ldlinux lives in low real-mode segments (00E8, 00DB, 00C3, etc.)
		if not _G._ldlinux_loaded and _G.eltorito_params and
		   CPU_SEGMENTS[2] ~= 0x9BF0 and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] ~= 0x07C0 and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] ~= 0x0000 and
		   CPU_SEGMENTS[2] < 0xA000 then
			_G._ldlinux_loaded = true
			print(string.format("[ldlinux] High CS=%04X detected after El Torito — ldlinux relocated", CPU_SEGMENTS[2]))
		end
		-- ⭐ CS=00E8 first-entry: ldlinux.c32 just started — patch low memory heap
		if CPU_SEGMENTS[2] == 0x00E8 and not _G._ldlinux_heap_patched and _G.EMU.MEM then
			_G._ldlinux_heap_patched = true
			_G._ldlinux_loaded = true
			print(string.format("[ldlinux] CS=00E8 detected (IP=%04X) — patching low memory free list for malloc", CPU_IP))
			-- ldlinux lmalloc uses a free arena list in low memory (0x500~0x9FC00)
			-- Structure (16-bit real mode, little-endian):
			--   Sentinel (head): { size_and_type=ARENA_TYPE_HEAD(0), next=blockA, prev=blockA }
			--   Block A (free):  { size_and_type=(size<<4)|ARENA_TYPE_FREE(2), next=sentinel, prev=sentinel }
			-- Each arena_header: size_type(2B) next(2B) prev(2B) = 6 bytes minimum
			-- syslinux uses 16-bit ptr within low memory DS segment (DS=0x0000)
			-- Sentinel at 0x1000 (safe, above IVT+BDA), free block at 0x1010
			local sentinel_addr = 0x1000
			local block_addr    = 0x1010
			local block_size    = 0x8F00  -- 36608 bytes > 0x8400 needed
			-- Sentinel: type=HEAD(0), next=block_addr, prev=block_addr
			local W = function(addr, lo, hi)
				if _G.EMU.MEM then
					buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr,   lo -band- 0xFF)
					buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr+1, hi -band- 0xFF)
				end
			end
			W(sentinel_addr+0, 0x00, 0x00)        -- size_type = HEAD (0)
			W(sentinel_addr+2, block_addr -band- 0xFF, (block_addr -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)  -- next
			W(sentinel_addr+4, block_addr -band- 0xFF, (block_addr -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)  -- prev
			-- Free block: type=FREE(2), size=block_size<<4|2, next=sentinel, prev=sentinel
			local bt = (block_size -blshift- 4) -bor- 2  -- (size<<4)|FREE
			W(block_addr+0, bt -band- 0xFF, (bt -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)   -- size_type
			W(block_addr+2, sentinel_addr -band- 0xFF, (sentinel_addr -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)  -- next
			W(block_addr+4, sentinel_addr -band- 0xFF, (sentinel_addr -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF)  -- prev
			print(string.format("[ldlinux] Low memory heap patched: sentinel@%04X, free block@%04X size=%04X", sentinel_addr, block_addr, block_size))
		end

		while frame_running and tick() < frame_deadline do
			-- Run BATCH_SIZE instructions before checking the clock again
			-- ⭐ FIX: Check PIC pending before each batch — route PIC IRQs to CPU interrupt queue
			-- ⭐⭐ CRITICAL FIX: Do NOT guard with "not CPU_HASINT"!
			-- HASINT=true with empty INTQUEUE = lost interrupt. Always drain PIC->INTQUEUE.
			if pic and pic.int_pending ~= 0 and #CPU_INTQUEUE == 0 then
				local irq_vec = pic_ack()
				if irq_vec ~= 0xFF then
					cpu_emit_interrupt(irq_vec, false)
				end
			end
			for _batch = 1, BATCH_SIZE do
				if CPU_HALTED then
					-- ⭐ FIX: Also check PIC pending to wake from HLT
					if CPU_HASINT or (pic and pic.int_pending ~= 0) then
						CPU_HALTED = false
						CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)  -- IF=1
						hlt_logged = false
					else
						CPU_FLAGS = CPU_FLAGS -bor- (1 -blshift- 9)
						if not hlt_logged then
							emu_debug(2, string.format("[HLT waiting] CS=%04X IP=%04X FLAGS=%04X", CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, CPU_FLAGS))
							hlt_logged = true
						end
						frame_running = false
						break
					end
				end
				hlt_logged = false
				execute = run_one(false, true)
				if execute == "block" then
					execute = true
					CPU_HALTED = true
					frame_running = false
					break
				elseif execute ~= true then
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[CPU] run_one returned %s at CS=%04X IP=%04X — stopping", tostring(execute), CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
					frame_running = false
					break
				end
				_G.EMU.PERF.opc = _G.EMU.PERF.opc + 1
			end
		end
	end
	end)

	-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Screen renders at 30fps (33ms) instead of 20fps (50ms)
	-- for noticeably better TinyCore GUI responsiveness
	task.spawn(function()
		while execute do
			if displayOn then
				video_update()
			end
			keyboard_update()
			task.wait(0.033)  -- ~30fps (was 0.05 = 20fps)
		end
	end)
end

function emu_execute()
	-- Sync local state from Global E object (set by boot sequence)
	CPU_FLAGS = _G.EMU.FLAGS or 0x0202
	CPU_IP = _G.EMU.IP or 0xFFF0
	CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = _G.EMU.SEGS[2] or 0xFFFF -- CS
	CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = _G.EMU.SEGS[3] or 0x0000 -- SS
	CPU_REGS[5] = _G.EMU.REGS[5] or 0x0000     -- ESP (lower 16)
	mrm6_table = _G.EMU.MRM.TABLE6

	sysconf_init()

	-- set IVT locations to NOP or IRET
	for i=0,255 do
		if interrupt_handlers[i+1] then
			RAM[0xF1100+i] = 0x90
		else
			RAM[0xF1100+i] = 0xCF
		end
	end

	-- BIOS 리셋 벡터 (CS:IP = FFFF:FFF0)
	-- 만약 부트 시퀀스에서 이미 IP를 바꿨다면 (0x7C00 등), 이 벡터는 무시되지만 RAM에는 써둠
	RAM[0xFFFF0] = 0xEA        -- JMP FAR
	RAM[0xFFFF1] = 0x19        -- IP low  (0x1119)
	RAM[0xFFFF2] = 0x11        -- IP high
	RAM[0xFFFF3] = 0x00        -- CS low  (0xF000)
	RAM[0xFFFF4] = 0xF0        -- CS high

	_G.EMU.cpu_execute()
end

end -- ── end CPU helper & opcode table scope ──

-- ===== pic.lua =====

-- ========================================================
-- 8259A PIC (86Box pic.c 기반 완전 재구현)
-- 86Box: pic.c / find_best_interrupt() / pic_write() / pic_read()
-- ========================================================

PIC_INTERRUPT_PRINTER  = 7
PIC_INTERRUPT_FDD      = 6
PIC_INTERRUPT_HDD      = 5
PIC_INTERRUPT_COM1     = 4
PIC_INTERRUPT_COM2     = 3
PIC_INTERRUPT_VIDEO    = 2
PIC_INTERRUPT_KEYBOARD = 1
PIC_INTERRUPT_MOUSE    = 1
PIC_INTERRUPT_RTC      = 1
PIC_INTERRUPT_TIMER    = 0

-- 86Box pic_t 구조체 (master)
local pic = {
	irr       = 0,    -- Interrupt Request Register
	isr       = 0,    -- In-Service Register
	imr       = 0,    -- Interrupt Mask Register
	icw_state = 0,    -- 0=none, 1=ICW2 wait, 2=ICW3, 3=ICW4
	icw1      = 0,
	icw2      = 0x08, -- vector offset: IRQ0→INT8
	icw3      = 2,    -- cascade on IRQ2 (number encoding, band(2,7)=2)
	icw4      = 0x01, -- 8086 mode
	ocw3      = 0x02, -- default: read IRR
	elcr      = 0,    -- edge/level control
	int_pending = 0,
	auto_eoi  = false,
	rotate_on_aeoi = false,
	special_mask = false,
	priority_add = 0, -- for priority rotation
}

-- 86Box pic_t 구조체 (slave, IRQ8-15)
local pic2 = {
	irr       = 0,
	isr       = 0,
	imr       = 0,
	icw_state = 0,
	icw1      = 0,
	icw2      = 0x70, -- vector offset: IRQ8→INT70h
	icw3      = 0x02, -- slave connected to master IRQ2
	icw4      = 0x03, -- 8086 mode + auto-EOI (clears ISR immediately after ACK)
	ocw3      = 0x02,
	elcr      = 0,
	int_pending = 0,
	auto_eoi  = true,  -- auto-EOI: ISR cleared on ACK so repeated IRQ14 can fire
	rotate_on_aeoi = false,
	special_mask = false,
	priority_add = 0,
}

-- 86Box: find_best_interrupt() — 우선순위 고려한 최고 미처리 인터럽트 반환
local function pic_find_best(p)
	local irr_val = bit32.band(p.irr, bit32.bnot(p.imr))
	if irr_val == 0 then return -1 end
	-- priority rotation: start from priority_add+1
	for i = 0, 7 do
		local bit = bit32.band(p.priority_add + i, 7)
		if bit32.band(irr_val, bit32.lshift(1, bit)) ~= 0 then
			-- check not masked in ISR (special mask mode)
			if p.special_mask or bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.lshift(1, bit)) == 0 then
				return bit
			end
		end
	end
	return -1
end

-- 인터럽트 펜딩 상태 업데이트
local function pic_update_pending()
	local irq = pic_find_best(pic)
	if irq >= 0 then
		-- cascade: check if this is slave IRQ
		if irq == (bit32.band(pic.icw3, 7)) then
			local slave_irq = pic_find_best(pic2)
			if slave_irq >= 0 then
				pic.int_pending = 1
				return
			end
		else
			pic.int_pending = 1
			return
		end
	end
	pic.int_pending = 0
end

-- 86Box: picint(mask) — IRQ 라인 활성화
function pic_raise_irq(irq)
	if irq < 8 then
		if pic.elcr ~= 0 or bit32.band(pic.irr, bit32.lshift(1, irq)) == 0 then
			pic.irr = bit32.bor(pic.irr, bit32.lshift(1, irq))
			pic_update_pending()
		end
	else
		local irq2 = irq - 8
		-- ⭐ FIX: If force-unmask flag set (from code before pic2 is defined), clear IMR
		if _G._force_irq14_unmask then
