			pic2.imr = bit32.band(pic2.imr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq2)))  -- unmask this IRQ
			pic.imr  = bit32.band(pic.imr,  0xFB)  -- unmask cascade IRQ2
		end
		-- ⭐ FIX: If ISR bit is stuck (no EOI came), clear it so IRQ can re-fire
		-- This happens when ldlinux COM32 loop swallows the interrupt without EOI
		if bit32.band(pic2.isr, bit32.lshift(1, irq2)) ~= 0 then
			pic2.isr = bit32.band(pic2.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq2)))
		end
		if pic2.elcr ~= 0 or bit32.band(pic2.irr, bit32.lshift(1, irq2)) == 0 then
			pic2.irr = bit32.bor(pic2.irr, bit32.lshift(1, irq2))
			-- cascade into master IRQ2
			local cas = bit32.band(pic.icw3, 7)  -- slave cascade line
			-- ⭐ FIX: Also clear master ISR cascade bit if stuck
			if bit32.band(pic.isr, bit32.lshift(1, cas)) ~= 0 then
				pic.isr = bit32.band(pic.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, cas)))
			end
			pic.irr = bit32.bor(pic.irr, bit32.lshift(1, cas))
			pic_update_pending()
		end
	end
end

function pic_lower_irq(irq)
    if irq < 8 then
        pic.irr = bit32.band(pic.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq)))
    else
        local irq2 = irq - 8
        pic2.irr = bit32.band(pic2.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq2)))
        if pic2.irr == 0 then
            local cas = bit32.band(pic.icw3, 7)
            pic.irr = bit32.band(pic.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, cas)))
        end
    end
    pic_update_pending()
end

function pic_set_level(irq, level)
    if level then pic_raise_irq(irq) else pic_lower_irq(irq) end
end

-- 86Box: pic_inta() — 인터럽트 ACK, 벡터 번호 반환
function pic_ack()
	local irq = pic_find_best(pic)
	if irq < 0 then return 0xFF end

	local cas = bit32.band(pic.icw3, 7)
	local is_slave = (irq == cas) and pic_find_best(pic2) >= 0

	if is_slave then
		local irq2 = pic_find_best(pic2)
		-- set ISR, clear IRR in slave
		pic2.isr = bit32.bor(pic2.isr, bit32.lshift(1, irq2))
		pic2.irr = bit32.band(pic2.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq2)))
		if pic2.auto_eoi then
			pic2.isr = bit32.band(pic2.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq2)))
			if pic2.rotate_on_aeoi then
				pic2.priority_add = bit32.band(irq2 + 1, 7)
			end
		end
		-- set ISR, clear IRR in master for cascade
		pic.isr = bit32.bor(pic.isr, bit32.lshift(1, cas))
		pic.irr = bit32.band(pic.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, cas)))
		if pic.auto_eoi then
			pic.isr = bit32.band(pic.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, cas)))
		end
		pic_update_pending()
		return pic2.icw2 + irq2
	else
		-- master IRQ
		pic.isr = bit32.bor(pic.isr, bit32.lshift(1, irq))
		pic.irr = bit32.band(pic.irr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq)))
		if pic.auto_eoi then
			pic.isr = bit32.band(pic.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq)))
			if pic.rotate_on_aeoi then
				pic.priority_add = bit32.band(irq + 1, 7)
			end
		end
		pic_update_pending()
		return pic.icw2 + irq
	end
end

-- 86Box: pic_interrupt_enabled — 인터럽트 마스크 확인
function pic_interrupt_enabled(i)
	if i < 8 then
		return bit32.band(pic.imr, bit32.lshift(1, i)) == 0
	else
		return bit32.band(pic2.imr, bit32.lshift(1, i - 8)) == 0
	end
end

-- 86Box: pic_write() — 포트 쓰기 (ICW1-4, OCW2-3)
local function pic_write_handler(p, is_cmd_port, val)
	if is_cmd_port then
		-- 포트 0x20/0xA0
		if bit32.band(val, 0x10) ~= 0 then
			-- ICW1
			p.icw1 = val
			p.icw_state = 1  -- next: ICW2
			p.irr = 0; p.isr = 0; p.imr = 0
			p.priority_add = 0
			p.auto_eoi = false
			p.special_mask = false
			p.ocw3 = 0x02
		elseif bit32.band(val, 0x08) == 0 then
			-- OCW2 (D3=0)
			local cmd = bit32.rshift(val, 5)
			local irq = bit32.band(val, 7)
			if cmd == 1 then
				-- Non-specific EOI
				for i = 0, 7 do
					local bit_i = bit32.band(p.priority_add + i, 7)
					if bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.lshift(1, bit_i)) ~= 0 then
						p.isr = bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, bit_i)))
						break
					end
				end
			elseif cmd == 3 then
				-- Specific EOI
				p.isr = bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq)))
			elseif cmd == 5 then
				-- Rotate on non-specific EOI
				for i = 0, 7 do
					local bit_i = bit32.band(p.priority_add + i, 7)
					if bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.lshift(1, bit_i)) ~= 0 then
						p.isr = bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, bit_i)))
						p.priority_add = bit32.band(bit_i + 1, 7)
						break
					end
				end
			elseif cmd == 7 then
				-- Rotate + specific EOI
				p.isr = bit32.band(p.isr, bit32.bnot(bit32.lshift(1, irq)))
				p.priority_add = bit32.band(irq + 1, 7)
			elseif cmd == 6 then
				-- Set priority
				p.priority_add = bit32.band(irq + 1, 7)
			elseif cmd == 0 then
				-- Rotate in AEOI clear
				p.rotate_on_aeoi = false
			elseif cmd == 4 then
				-- Rotate in AEOI set
				p.rotate_on_aeoi = true
			end
			pic_update_pending()
		else
			-- OCW3 (D3=1)
			p.ocw3 = val
			if bit32.band(val, 0x40) ~= 0 then
				p.special_mask = (bit32.band(val, 0x20) ~= 0)
			end
		end
	else
		-- 포트 0x21/0xA1 (ICW2/3/4 or IMR)
		if p.icw_state == 1 then
			-- ICW2: vector offset
			p.icw2 = bit32.band(val, 0xF8)
			if bit32.band(p.icw1, 0x02) ~= 0 then
				p.icw_state = 0  -- single mode: skip ICW3
				if bit32.band(p.icw1, 0x01) ~= 0 then
					p.icw_state = 3  -- need ICW4
				end
			else
				p.icw_state = 2  -- cascade: need ICW3
			end
		elseif p.icw_state == 2 then
			-- ICW3
			p.icw3 = val
			if bit32.band(p.icw1, 0x01) ~= 0 then
				p.icw_state = 3  -- need ICW4
			else
				p.icw_state = 0
			end
		elseif p.icw_state == 3 then
			-- ICW4
			p.icw4 = val
			p.auto_eoi = (bit32.band(val, 0x02) ~= 0)
			p.icw_state = 0
		else
			-- OCW1: IMR
			p.imr = val
			pic_update_pending()
		end
	end
end

-- 86Box: pic_read() — 포트 읽기
local function pic_read_handler(p, is_cmd_port)
	if is_cmd_port then
		if bit32.band(p.ocw3, 0x03) == 0x03 then
			return p.isr
		else
			return p.irr
		end
	else
		return p.imr
	end
end

-- 포트 등록: Master PIC (0x20/0x21)
cpu_port_set(0x20, function(cond, val)
	if val then
		pic_write_handler(pic, true, val)
	else
		return pic_read_handler(pic, true)
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x21, function(cond, val)
	if val then
		pic_write_handler(pic, false, val)
	else
		return pic_read_handler(pic, false)
	end
end)

-- 포트 등록: Slave PIC (0xA0/0xA1)
cpu_port_set(0xA0, function(cond, val)
	if val then
		pic_write_handler(pic2, true, val)
	else
		return pic_read_handler(pic2, true)
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0xA1, function(cond, val)
	if val then
		pic_write_handler(pic2, false, val)
	else
		return pic_read_handler(pic2, false)
	end
end)

-- ELCR 포트 (0x4D0/0x4D1)
cpu_port_set(0x4D0, function(cond, val)
	if val then pic.elcr = val else return pic.elcr end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x4D1, function(cond, val)
	if val then pic2.elcr = val else return pic2.elcr end
end)

-- 포트 0x22/0x23 (APIC ID 등, stub)
local p22 = 0
local p23 = 0
cpu_port_set(0x22, function(cond, val) if val then p22=val else return p22 end end)
cpu_port_set(0x23, function(cond, val) if val then p23=val else return p23 end end)

-- ========================================================
-- 8253/8254 PIT (86Box pit.c 기반 완전 재구현)
-- 86Box: pit.c / ctr_tick() / ctr_load_count() / pit_write()
-- ========================================================

-- ⭐ FIX: forward-declared here so pit_tick (below) can call them
-- (actual definitions with identical body also appear later in timer.lua section)
local function get_timer_ticks()
	return RAM:r32(0x46c)
end
local function set_timer_ticks(v)
	return RAM:w32(0x46c, v)
end

pit_osc_freq = 1.193182  -- MHz

-- 86Box ctr_t 구조체 (채널당)
local function pit_new_channel()
	return {
		count    = 0,     -- current counter value
		l        = 0,     -- latched reload value (lo/hi split)
		l_lo     = 0,     -- reload lo byte
		l_hi     = 0,     -- reload hi byte
		reload   = 0x10000, -- reload value (loaded from l on trigger)
		mode     = 3,     -- mode 0-5 (86Box: m field)
		rl       = 3,     -- read/load mode: 0=latch, 1=lo, 2=hi, 3=lo+hi
		gate     = true,  -- gate input
		out      = false, -- output state
		bcd      = false, -- BCD mode
		latched  = false, -- output latch
		latch_val= 0,     -- latched count value
		rw_state = 0,     -- 0=lo next, 1=hi next (for rl=3)
		rd_state = 0,     -- 0=lo next, 1=hi next (for read)
		running  = false, -- counter is loaded and running
		null_count=false, -- waiting for new count to be loaded
	}
end

local pit_channels = {pit_new_channel(), pit_new_channel(), pit_new_channel()}

function pit_channel(c)
	return pit_channels[c]
end

-- 86Box: ctr_load_count() — count=l, wraps 0→0x10000
local function pit_load_count(ch)
	local l = ch.l_lo + bit32.lshift(ch.l_hi, 8)
	if l == 0 then l = 0x10000 end
	ch.reload  = l
	ch.count   = l
	ch.running = true
	ch.null_count = false
end

local pit_last_tick = -1
local pit_ticks_acc = {0, 0, 0}  -- fractional tick accumulator

-- 86Box: ctr_tick() — 모든 6개 모드 구현
local function pit_ctr_tick(n, ticks)
	local ch = pit_channels[n]
	if not ch.running then return 0 end

	local firings = 0
	local mode = ch.mode

	if mode == 0 then
		-- Mode 0: interrupt on terminal count
		-- OUT goes low when loaded, high when count reaches 0
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks
		if ch.count <= 0 then
			ch.out = true
			ch.count = 0
			ch.running = false
			firings = 1
		end
	elseif mode == 1 then
		-- Mode 1: hardware retriggerable one-shot
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks
		if ch.count <= 0 then
			ch.out = true
			ch.running = false
			firings = 1
		end
	elseif mode == 2 or mode == 6 then
		-- Mode 2: rate generator (like 86Box mode 2/6)
		-- OUT low for 1 tick, high for (reload-1) ticks
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks
		while ch.count <= 0 do
			ch.count = ch.count + ch.reload
			firings = firings + 1
		end
	elseif mode == 3 or mode == 7 then
		-- Mode 3: square wave
		-- Count by 2 each tick, fire every reload/2
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks * 2
		while ch.count <= 0 do
			ch.count = ch.count + ch.reload
			firings = firings + 1
		end
	elseif mode == 4 then
		-- Mode 4: software triggered strobe
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks
		if ch.count <= 0 then
			ch.out = true
			ch.running = false
			firings = 1
		end
	elseif mode == 5 then
		-- Mode 5: hardware triggered strobe (gate-triggered)
		ch.count = ch.count - ticks
		if ch.count <= 0 then
			ch.out = true
			ch.running = false
			firings = 1
		end
	end
	return firings
end

function pit_tick(curr_t)
	if pit_last_tick < 0 then
		pit_last_tick = curr_t
		return
	end
	local elapsed = curr_t - pit_last_tick
	pit_last_tick = curr_t

	-- 86Box: osc_count = elapsed * freq_hz
	local osc_float = elapsed * pit_osc_freq * 1000000
	local osc_count = math.floor(osc_float)
	if osc_count <= 0 then return end

	-- Channel 0: timer interrupt (IRQ0 → INT 08h)
	local fires = pit_ctr_tick(1, osc_count)
	if fires > 0 then
		-- ⭐ FIX: Directly increment BIOS timer ticks (0x46C) so INT 1Ah timeout works
		-- This replaces cpu_emit_interrupt(0x08) which caused stack overflow
		local cur_ticks = get_timer_ticks()
		set_timer_ticks(cur_ticks + fires)
		-- ⭐⭐ FIX: When ldlinux is executing in high CS (A80B+), DO NOT raise IRQ0.
		-- ldlinux.c32 manages its own scheduler; injecting IRQ0 causes unbounded
		-- stack growth because each timer interrupt pushes FLAGS/CS/IP but the
		-- ldlinux INT 08h handler never does a proper EOI+IRET back to our code.
		-- Only raise IRQ0 during pre-ldlinux boot (isolinux stage1, CS=9BF0/07C0)
		-- or when CS is in the low real-mode range (<0x1000, excludes A80B+).
		local _cur_cs_pit = CPU_SEGMENTS and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] or 0
		-- ⭐ FIX: Suppress IRQ0 when:
		--   a) ldlinux loaded + CS >= 0x0100 (ldlinux manages own timer)
		--   b) CS >= 0xA000 (VRAM/ROM range — executing null bytes, IRQ makes stack overflow worse)
		local _ldlinux_high_cs = _G._ldlinux_loaded and (_cur_cs_pit >= 0x0100)
		local _in_vram_cs = (_cur_cs_pit >= 0xA000)
		if not _ldlinux_high_cs and not _in_vram_cs then
			-- Raise IRQ0 via PIC (processed by batch loop PIC bridge, not directly)
			pic_raise_irq(0)
		end
	end

	-- Channel 1: DRAM refresh (not emulated, just tick)
	pit_ctr_tick(2, osc_count)

	-- Channel 2: PC speaker
	pit_ctr_tick(3, osc_count)
end

-- 86Box: pit_write() — 포트 0x43 컨트롤 워드 디코딩
-- Control byte: SC[7:6] | RL[5:4] | M[3:1] | BCD[0]
cpu_port_set(0x43, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return 0xFF end
	local sc = bit32.rshift(val, 6)         -- channel select (0-2, 3=readback)
	local rl = bit32.band(bit32.rshift(val, 4), 3) -- read/load mode
	local m  = bit32.band(bit32.rshift(val, 1), 7) -- mode
	local bcd = bit32.band(val, 1) ~= 0    -- BCD mode

	if sc == 3 then
		-- Read-back command (82C54 only) — stub
		return
	end

	local ch = pit_channels[sc + 1]
	if rl == 0 then
		-- Latch count
		ch.latch_val = ch.count
		ch.latched   = true
		return
	end

	-- Normal: set mode
	ch.rl = rl
	ch.mode = bit32.band(m, 5)  -- 86Box: masks to 0,1,2,3,4,5
	ch.bcd  = bcd
	ch.rw_state = 0
	ch.rd_state = 0
	ch.running = false
	ch.null_count = true
	ch.l_lo = 0
	ch.l_hi = 0
	if ch.mode == 0 then
		ch.out = false
	else
		ch.out = true
	end
end)

-- PIT 채널 데이터 포트 (0x40-0x42) — 86Box pit_write_data()
local function pit_write_data(n)
	return function(cond, val)
		if not val then
			-- Read count
			local ch = pit_channels[n]
			local count
			if ch.latched then
				count = ch.latch_val
			else
				count = ch.count < 0 and 0 or ch.count
			end
			count = bit32.band(count, 0xFFFF)

			if ch.rl == 1 then
				-- lo only
				ch.latched = false
				return bit32.band(count, 0xFF)
			elseif ch.rl == 2 then
				-- hi only
				ch.latched = false
				return bit32.rshift(count, 8)
			else
				-- lo+hi
				if ch.rd_state == 0 then
					ch.rd_state = 1
					return bit32.band(count, 0xFF)
				else
					ch.rd_state = 0
					ch.latched = false
					return bit32.rshift(count, 8)
				end
			end
		else
			-- Write count
			local ch = pit_channels[n]
			if ch.rl == 1 then
				-- lo only
				ch.l_lo = val
				ch.l_hi = 0
				pit_load_count(ch)
			elseif ch.rl == 2 then
				-- hi only
				ch.l_lo = 0
				ch.l_hi = val
				pit_load_count(ch)
			else
				-- lo+hi (two writes)
				if ch.rw_state == 0 then
					ch.l_lo = val
					ch.rw_state = 1
				else
					ch.l_hi = val
					ch.rw_state = 0
					pit_load_count(ch)
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

cpu_port_set(0x40, pit_write_data(1))
cpu_port_set(0x41, pit_write_data(2))
cpu_port_set(0x42, pit_write_data(3))

-- 채널 0 초기화: 86Box 기본값 (mode 3, reload=0x10000)
do
	local ch = pit_channels[1]
	ch.mode = 3; ch.rl = 3; ch.running = true
	ch.reload = 0x10000; ch.count = 0x10000
end

-- ===== timer.lua =====

-- (get_timer_ticks / set_timer_ticks are defined before the PIT section above)

local timer_last_midnight = 0
local timer_midnight = 24*60*60*20

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x08, function(ax,ah,al)
	set_timer_ticks(get_timer_ticks()+1)
	-- ⭐⭐ FIX: Do NOT chain INT 1Ch when ldlinux is running in high CS.
	-- ldlinux installs its own INT 08h/1Ch handlers; chaining into them via
	-- cpu_emit_interrupt causes a recursive stack that grows unboundedly.
	-- When ldlinux is active (high CS), only update the BIOS tick counter.
	local _cur_cs_int8 = CPU_SEGMENTS and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] or 0
	if not (_G._ldlinux_loaded and _cur_cs_int8 >= 0x0100) then
		cpu_emit_interrupt(0x1C,false)
	end
	-- ⭐ FIX: Send EOI to PIC master so ISR bit is cleared (allows next IRQ0)
	-- Without EOI, PIC.isr has IRQ0 bit set permanently → PIC blocks same-priority IRQs
	if pic and not pic.auto_eoi then
		pic.isr = bit32.band(pic.isr, bit32.bnot(1))  -- clear IRQ0 (bit 0) in ISR
		pic_update_pending()
	end
	return true
end)

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x1C, function(ax,ah,al)
	-- dummy - override by user
	return true
end)

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x1A, function(ax,ah,al)
	if (ah == 0x00) then
		local midnight = 0
		local timer_ticks = get_timer_ticks()
		while (timer_ticks - timer_midnight) >= timer_last_midnight do
			midnight = 1
			timer_last_midnight = timer_last_midnight + timer_midnight
		end
		CPU["regs"][1] = (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- midnight
		CPU["regs"][2] = (timer_ticks -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFFFF
		CPU["regs"][3] = (timer_ticks -band- 0xFFFF)
		return true
	elseif (ah == 0x01) then
		local timer_ticks = CPU["regs"][3] -bor- (CPU["regs"][2] -blshift- 16)
		set_timer_ticks(timer_ticks)
		-- reset midnight flag
		timer_last_midnight = 0
		while (timer_ticks - timer_midnight) >= timer_last_midnight do
			timer_last_midnight = timer_last_midnight + timer_midnight
		end
		return true
	elseif (ah == 0x03) or (ah == 0x05) then
		-- TODO
		return true
	elseif (ah == 0x02) or (ah == 0x04) then
		-- TODO
		cpu_clear_flag(0) -- clear carry
		CPU["regs"][2] = 0x0000
		CPU["regs"][3] = 0x0000
		return true
	else
		cpu_set_flag(0)
	end
end)

set_timer_ticks(0)

-- ===== video.lua =====

-- SUPPORTED MODES:
-- CGA: 00h, 01h, 02h, 03h, 04h, 05h, 06h
-- PCjr: 08h, 09h
-- VGA: 12h (pretend; just runs 13h code, used to not upset certain MCGA software)
-- MCGA: 13h (shaky; 0x3D** ports only supported for palette)

local video_mode = 3

pc_16_colors = {
	0x000000, 0x0000AA, 0x00AA00, 0x00AAAA,
	0xAA0000, 0xAA00AA, 0xAA5500, 0xAAAAAA,
	0x555555, 0x5555FF, 0x55FF55, 0x55FFFF,
	0xFF5555, 0xFF55FF, 0xFFFF55, 0xFFFFFF
}

RAM[0x450] = 0 -- cursor pos
RAM[0x451] = 0 
RAM[0x462] = 0 -- current page
RAM:w16(0x463, 0x3D4) -- base IO port for video

local vram = {}
local dirty_lines = {}

function video_pop_dirty_lines()
	local d = dirty_lines
	dirty_lines = {}
	return d
end

function video_vram_read(addr)
	local offset = addr - 0xA0000
	if offset >= 0 and offset < 4194304 then
		return buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.VRAM, offset)
	end
	return 0
end

function video_vram_write(addr, val)
	local offset = addr - 0xA0000
	if offset < 0 or offset >= 4194304 then return end
	
	if buffer.readu8(_G.EMU.VRAM, offset) == val then return end
	buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.VRAM, offset, bit32.band(val, 0xFF))

	local l = nil
	local lx = nil

	if (video_mode >= 0 and video_mode <= 3) or video_mode == 7 then
		if addr >= 0xB8000 and addr < (0xB8000 + (25 * 160)) then
			l = math.floor((addr - 0xB8000) / 160)
			lx = math.floor((addr - 0xB8000) % 160) -brshift- 1
		end
	elseif ((video_mode >= 4 and video_mode <= 6) and (addr >= 0xB8000 and addr < 0xBC000))
		or (video_mode == 8 and (addr >= 0xB0000 and addr < 0xB4000)) then

		if ((addr -band- 0x1FFF) < 8000) then
			-- two banks, 100 lines each, so 80 bytes per line
			l = (math.floor((addr -band- 0x1FFF) / 80)) -brshift- 1 -- 0..99 div 2
			lx = math.floor((addr -band- 0x1FFF) % 80)
		end
	elseif video_mode == 9 and (addr >= 0xB0000 and addr < 0xB8000) then

		if ((addr -band- 0x1FFF) < 8000) then
			-- four banks! 50 lines each, so 160 bytes per line
			l = (math.floor((addr -band- 0x1FFF) / 160))
			lx = math.floor((addr -band- 0x1FFF) % 160)
		end
	elseif video_mode >= 0x12 and video_mode <= 0x13 then
		if (addr >= 0xA0000 and addr < (0xA0000 + 64000)) then
			-- woo, no interleaving on this one
			lx = math.floor(((addr - 0xA0000) -brshift- 1) % 160) -- 0..159
			l = math.floor((addr - 0xA0000) / 1280) -- 0..49
		end
	end

	if l then
		if not dirty_lines[l] then
			dirty_lines[l] = {lx, lx}
		else
			local ld = dirty_lines[l]
			if lx < ld[1] then ld[1] = lx
			elseif lx > ld[2] then ld[2] = lx end
		end
	end
end

function video_text_addr(x, y)
	return 0xB8000 + (y * 160) + (x * 2)
end

function video_scroll_up(lines, empty_attr, y1, x1, y2, x2)
	if lines == 0 then
		for y=y1,y2 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y), empty_attr -blshift- 8)
			end
		end
	else
		for y=y1+lines,y2 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y-lines), RAM:r16(video_text_addr(x,y)))
			end
		end
		for y=y2-lines+1,y2 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y), empty_attr -blshift- 8)
			end
		end
	end
end

function video_scroll_down(lines, empty_attr, y1, x1, y2, x2)
	if lines == 0 then
		for y=y1,y2 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y), empty_attr -blshift- 8)
			end
		end
	else
		for y=y2-lines,y1,-1 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y+lines), RAM:r16(video_text_addr(x,y)))
			end
		end
		for y=y1,y1+lines-1 do
			for x=x1,x2 do
				RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y), empty_attr -blshift- 8)
			end
		end
	end
end

local cga_mode = 0x08
local cga_palette = 0x30
local cga_status = 0x09

function cga_get_palette()
	return cga_palette
end

--local herc_status = 0
local herc_status = 0xFF

function video_update()

	-- ===== DEBUG =====
	if video_mode == 0x13 then
		print("MODE13H ENTERED")
	end

	-- ===== GLOBAL SAFETY =====
	if not _G.EMU then return end
	if not _G.EMU.VRAM then return end

	local vram = _G.EMU.VRAM
	local mode = video_mode

	-- ===== TEXT MODE =====
	if mode == 0 or mode == 1 then
		if _G.EMU.VGA_TEXT_MODE ~= false and platform_render_text then
			platform_render_text(vram, 0xB8000, 40, 25, 160)
		end
		return
	end

	if mode == 2 or mode == 3 or mode == 7 then
		if _G.EMU.VGA_TEXT_MODE ~= false and platform_render_text then
			platform_render_text(vram, 0xB8000, 80, 25, 160)
		end
		return
	end

	-- ===== CGA =====
	if mode >= 4 and mode <= 6 then
		if mode < 6 and platform_render_cga_color then
			platform_render_cga_color(vram, 0xB8000, mode)
		elseif platform_render_cga_mono then
			platform_render_cga_mono(vram, 0xB8000)
		end
		return
	end

	-- ===== PCJR =====
	if mode == 0x08 then
		if platform_render_pcjr_160 then
			platform_render_pcjr_160(vram, 0xB0000)
		end
		return
	end

	if mode == 0x09 then
		if platform_render_pcjr_320 then
			platform_render_pcjr_320(vram, 0xB0000)
		end
		return
	end

	if mode == 0x0A then
		if platform_render_pcjr_640 then
			platform_render_pcjr_640(vram, 0xB0000)
		end
		return
	end

	-- ===== VGA / MCGA =====
	if mode == 0x13 or mode == 0x12 then
		if platform_render_mcga_13h then
			platform_render_mcga_13h(vram, 0xA0000)
		end
		return
	end

	-- ===== UNKNOWN MODE =====
	-- Linux probing 등 → 그냥 무시
end
local cga_mode_mask = 0x17 -- 0b10111
local cga_reg_to_mode = {}
cga_reg_to_mode[0] = 0x04 -- 40x25 mono
cga_reg_to_mode[1] = 0x00 -- 40x25 color
cga_reg_to_mode[2] = 0x05 -- 80x25 mono
cga_reg_to_mode[3] = 0x01 -- 80x25 color
cga_reg_to_mode[4] = 0x02 -- 320x200 graphics
cga_reg_to_mode[5] = 0x06 -- 320x200 alt graphics
cga_reg_to_mode[6] = 0x16 -- 640x200 graphics

-- Hercules ports
cpu_port_set(0x3BA, function(cond, val)
	if not val then
		emu_debug(2, "polling hercules status")
		return herc_status
	end
end)

-- CGA ports
cpu_port_set(0x3D8, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return cga_mode else
		cga_mode = val -band- 0x3F
		for i=0,6 do
			if cga_reg_to_mode[i] == (cga_mode -band- cga_mode_mask) then
				-- TODO: set mode from here
			end
		end
		RAM[0x465] = cga_mode
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x3D9, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return cga_palette else
		cga_palette = val -band- 0x3F
		RAM[0x466] = cga_palette
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x3DA, function(cond, val)
	if not val then
		cga_status = bit32.bxor(cga_status, 0x09)
		return cga_status
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x3DF, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return 0 end
end)

function video_set_mode(vmode, clr)
        print("SET MODE:", vmode)
	local mode_supported = false
	if (vmode >= 4 and vmode <= 6) and platform_render_cga_mono then
		mode_supported = true
	elseif vmode == 0x08 and platform_render_pcjr_160 then
		mode_supported = true
	elseif vmode == 0x09 and platform_render_pcjr_320 then
		mode_supported = true
	elseif vmode == 0x0A and platform_render_pcjr_640 then
		mode_supported = true
	elseif (vmode == 0x13 or vmode == 0x12) and platform_render_mcga_13h then
		mode_supported = true
	elseif vmode >= 0 and vmode <= 3 then
		mode_supported = true
	end
	if not mode_supported then
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[video] unsupported mode %02X — ignored, continuing", vmode))
		return true  -- do NOT stop execution, just skip unsupported mode
	end

	video_mode = vmode

	-- Show/hide VGA framebuffer layer when switching between text and graphics modes
	if vga_fb_show then
		vga_fb_show(vmode == 0x12 or vmode == 0x13)
	end

	cga_mode = 0x08
	if vmode >= 0 and vmode <= 6 then
		cga_mode = cga_mode -bor- cga_reg_to_mode[vmode]
	end
	cga_status = 0x09

	-- 0x449 - byte, video mode
	RAM[0x449] = video_mode

	-- 0x44A - word, text width
	if video_mode == 7 or (cga_mode -band- 1) == 1 then
		RAM[0x44A] = 80
	else
		RAM[0x44A] = 40
	end
	RAM[0x44B] = 0
	RAM[0x465] = cga_mode
	RAM[0x466] = cga_palette

	if clr then
		if (vmode >= 0 and vmode <= 3) or vmode == 7 then
			for y=0,24 do
				for x=0,RAM[0x44A]-1 do
					RAM:w16(video_text_addr(x,y), 0x0700)
				end
			end
		else
			for i=0,7999 do
				RAM[0xB8000 + i] = 0
				RAM[0xBA000 + i] = 0
			end
		end
	end

	return true
end

video_set_mode(3, true)

function video_get_cursor(page)
	if page == nil then
		page = (RAM[0x462] -band- 7) -blshift- 1
	end
	return RAM[0x450+page], RAM[0x451+page]
end

function video_set_cursor(x, y, page)
	if page == nil then
		page = (RAM[0x462] -band- 7) -blshift- 1
	end
	RAM[0x450+page] = x
	RAM[0x451+page] = y
end

local vgapal={}
_G.vgapal = vgapal  -- expose for platform_render_mcga_13h (defined earlier)

function video_vga_get_palette(i)
	return vgapal[1+i] or 0xFF00FF
end

function video_vga_get_palette_orig(i)
	-- just wing it this time, should be good enough
	return (video_vga_get_palette(i) -brshift- 2) -band- 0x3F3F3F
end

function video_vga_set_palette(i,r,g,b)
	local rs = math.floor(r * 255 / 63.0) -band- 0xFF
	local gs = math.floor(g * 255 / 63.0) -band- 0xFF
	local bs = math.floor(b * 255 / 63.0) -band- 0xFF
	vgapal[1+i] = (rs-blshift-16)-bor-(gs-blshift-8)-bor-bs
	-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Update Color3 cache in-place (avoid full rebuild each call)
	if _G.EMU.vga_pal_c3 then
		_G.EMU.vga_pal_c3[1+i] = Color3.fromRGB(rs, gs, bs)
	end
	-- ⭐ Invalidate VRAM dirty hash so next render is forced
	if _G then _G._vram_dirty_forced = true end

	if video_mode >= 0x10 then
		for i=0,49 do dirty_lines[i] = {0,159} end
	end
end

for i=1,16 do
	vgapal[i] = pc_16_colors[i]
end

-- VGA DAC
local dac_pal_idx = 0
local dac_write = true

cpu_port_set(0x3C7, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return 0 else
		dac_pal_idx = (val -band- 0xFF) * 3
		dac_write = false
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x3C8, function(cond, val)
	if not val then return 0 else
		dac_pal_idx = (val -band- 0xFF) * 3
		dac_write = true
	end
end)
cpu_port_set(0x3C9, function(cond, val)
	local shift = (8*(2 - math.floor(dac_pal_idx % 3)))
	local idx = math.floor(dac_pal_idx / 3)
	local mask = 0xFF -blshift- shift
	if not val and not dac_write then
		dac_pal_idx = math.floor((dac_pal_idx + 1) % 768)
		return (video_vga_get_palette_orig(idx) -brshift- (shift)) -band- 0xFF
	elseif val and dac_write then
		dac_pal_idx = math.floor((dac_pal_idx + 1) % 768)
		local pal = video_vga_get_palette_orig(idx) -band- bit32.bxor(mask, 0xFFFFFF)
		pal = pal -bor- ((val -band- 0xFF) -blshift- shift)
		video_vga_set_palette(idx, (pal -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFF, (pal -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF, pal -band- 0xFF)
	elseif not val then return 0 end
end)

-- interrupt	
cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x10, function(ax,ah,al)
	if ah == 0x00 then
		-- set video mode
		local mode = al -band- 0xFF7F
		emu_debug(1, "setting mode to " .. mode)
		video_set_mode(mode, (al -band- 0x80) == 0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x01 then
		-- set cursor shape, TODO
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x02 then
		-- set cursor pos
		video_set_cursor(CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF, CPU["regs"][3] -brshift- 8, CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x03 then
		-- get cursor_pos
		local cursor_x, cursor_y = video_get_cursor(CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8)
		CPU["regs"][3] = (cursor_y -blshift- 8) -bor- (cursor_x)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x04 then
		-- query light pen
		CPU["regs"][1] = al -- AH=0, not triggered
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x05 then
		-- select video page
		RAM[0x462] = al -band- 0x07
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x06 then
		-- scroll up
		video_scroll_up(al, (CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8),
			(CPU["regs"][2] -brshift- 8), (CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0xFF), 
			(CPU["regs"][3] -brshift- 8), (CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF));
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x07 then
		-- scroll down
		video_scroll_down(al, (CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8),
			(CPU["regs"][2] -brshift- 8), (CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0xFF), 
			(CPU["regs"][3] -brshift- 8), (CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF));
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x08 then
		-- read character
		local cursor_x, cursor_y = video_get_cursor(CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8)
		local addr = video_text_addr(cursor_x, cursor_y)
		CPU["regs"][1] = 0x0800 -bor- RAM[addr]
		CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (RAM[addr + 1] -blshift- 8)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x09 or ah == 0x0A then
		-- write character/attribute (0x09) or char (0x0A)
		local cursor_x, cursor_y = video_get_cursor(CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8)
		local addr = video_text_addr(cursor_x, cursor_y)
		local bl = CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF
		for i=1,CPU["regs"][2] do
			if addr < (160*25) then
				RAM[addr] = al
				if ah == 0x09 then
					RAM[addr + 1] = bl
				end
				addr = addr + 2
			end
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0B then
		-- configure video
		local p = cga_palette
		local bh = CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8
		local bl = CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF
		if bh == 0x00 then
			-- TODO: set border color
		elseif bh == 0x01 then
			-- set palette
			p = (p -band- 0xDF) -bor- ((bl -band- 0x01) -blshift- 5)
		end
		cga_palette = p
		RAM[0x466] = p
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0E then
		-- put char like a tty
		local cursor_x, cursor_y = video_get_cursor()
		local addr = video_text_addr(cursor_x, cursor_y)
		local cursor_width = RAM[0x44A]
		local cursor_height = 25
		if al == 0x0D then
			cursor_x = 0
		elseif al == 0x0A then
			if cursor_y < (cursor_height - 1) then
				cursor_y = cursor_y + 1
			else
				video_scroll_up(1, 0x07, 0, 0, cursor_height - 1, cursor_width - 1)
			end
		elseif al == 0x08 then
			if cursor_x > 0 then
				cursor_x = cursor_x - 1
			end
			RAM[video_text_addr(cursor_x, cursor_y)] = 0
		elseif al == 0x07 then
			-- bell
		else
			RAM[addr] = al
			cursor_x = cursor_x + 1
			if cursor_x >= cursor_width then
				cursor_x = 0
				if cursor_y < (cursor_height - 1) then
					cursor_y = cursor_y + 1
				else
					video_scroll_up(1, 0x07, 0, 0, cursor_height - 1, cursor_width - 1)
				end
			end
		end
		video_set_cursor(cursor_x, cursor_y)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0F then
		-- read video mode
		local ah = RAM[0x44A]
		local al = video_mode
		local bh = RAM[0x462]
		CPU["regs"][1] = (ah -blshift- 8) -bor- (al)
		CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (bh -blshift- 8)
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1010 then
		-- set single palette register
		-- BX=i, CH=g, CL=b, DH=r
		video_vga_set_palette(CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF, CPU["regs"][3]-brshift-8, CPU["regs"][2]-brshift-8, CPU["regs"][2]-band-0xFF)
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1012 then
		-- set palette block, BX = start, CX = count, ES:DX = offset
		local addrIn = seg(SEG_ES,CPU["regs"][3])
		local addrOut = CPU["regs"][4] - 1
		for i=1,CPU["regs"][2] do
			video_vga_set_palette((addrOut + i) -band- 0xFF, RAM[addrIn], RAM[addrIn + 1], RAM[addrIn + 2])
			addrIn = addrIn + 3
		end
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1015 then
		-- read single palette register
		local col = video_vga_get_palette_orig(CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF)
		CPU["regs"][2] = col -band- 0xFFFF
		CPU["regs"][3] = ((col -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF)
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1017 then
		-- read palette block
		local addrIn = seg(SEG_ES,CPU["regs"][3])
		local addrOut = CPU["regs"][4] - 1
		for i=1,CPU["regs"][2] do
			local col = video_vga_get_palette_orig((addrOut + i) -band- 0xFF)
			RAM[addrIn] = (col -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFF
			RAM[addrIn + 1] = (col -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF
			RAM[addrIn + 2] = col -band- 0xFF
			addrIn = addrIn + 3
		end
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1130 then
		-- get font information
		local bh = CPU["regs"][4] -brshift- 8
		if bh == 0 then
			-- set ES:BP
			CPU["regs"][6] = RAM:r16(0x1F * 4)
			CPU["segments"][1] = RAM:r16(0x1F * 4 + 2)
		elseif bh == 1 then
			CPU["regs"][6] = RAM:r16(0x43 * 4)
			CPU["segments"][1] = RAM:r16(0x43 * 4 + 2)
		else
			CPU["regs"][6] = 0x0800
			CPU["segments"][1] = 0xF000
		end
		CPU["regs"][2] = 0x08
		CPU["regs"][3] = (CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- RAM[0x484]
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x1A00 then
		-- get display combination code
		CPU["regs"][1] = 0x1A1A
		CPU["regs"][4] = 0x020A
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x12 then
		-- INT 10h AX=12xx: VGA/EGA alternate select subfunction
		-- BL=10: video subsystem config  BL=30: select vertical res
		-- BL=31: palette loading  BL=32: video addr enable
		-- BL=33: gray scale sum   BL=34: cursor emulation
		-- BL=36: video refresh    etc.
		-- 대부분 stub으로 성공 반환 (FreeDOS/UDRVD2 등 드라이버용)
		local bl = CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF
		if bl == 0x10 then
			-- return video subsystem info: BH=0 (color), BL=03 (64K EGA)
			CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 0x03
			CPU["regs"][1] = (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF)  -- BH=0
		else
			-- other 12xx subfunctions: silently succeed
			CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AL=0 (not used)
		end
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x4F then
		-- VESA VBE 2.0 implementation
		-- Supported modes: 0x101=640x480x8, 0x103=800x600x8, 0x105=1024x768x8, 0x111=640x480x16, 0x118=1024x768x24
		local vbe_al = ax -band- 0xFF
		local vbe_fn = (ax -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF  -- subfn from AH (but we check AL too since AX check)
		-- Actually AH=0x4F, AL=subfn
		vbe_fn = al  -- AL = VBE subfunction
		if vbe_fn == 0x00 then
			-- GET CONTROLLER INFO: write VbeInfoBlock at ES:DI
			local di = CPU["regs"][8]
			local es_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] -blshift- 4
			local buf = es_base + di
			-- VBE2.0 signature "VESA"
			RAM[buf+0]=0x56; RAM[buf+1]=0x45; RAM[buf+2]=0x53; RAM[buf+3]=0x41
			RAM[buf+4]=0x02; RAM[buf+5]=0x00  -- VBE version 2.0
			-- OEM String pointer (far ptr) — point to just after block
			RAM[buf+6]=(buf+256)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+7]=((buf+256)-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
			RAM[buf+8]=0; RAM[buf+9]=0  -- segment 0 (linear addr)
			-- Capabilities: [bit0]=DAC width switchable
			RAM[buf+10]=1; RAM[buf+11]=0; RAM[buf+12]=0; RAM[buf+13]=0
			-- Video Mode List ptr (far ptr at buf+14) → buf+32
			local mlist = buf+32
			RAM[buf+14]=(mlist)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+15]=((mlist)-brshift-8)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+16]=0; RAM[buf+17]=0
			-- Total memory in 64KB blocks (128MB = 2048)
			RAM[buf+18]=0; RAM[buf+19]=8
			-- Mode list: 0x101, 0x103, 0x105, 0x111, 0x118, 0xFFFF (end)
			local ml = {0x101, 0x103, 0x105, 0x111, 0x118, 0xFFFF}
			for i,m in ipairs(ml) do RAM[mlist+(i-1)*2]=m-band-0xFF; RAM[mlist+(i-1)*2+1]=(m-brshift-8)-band-0xFF end
			-- OEM string
			local oem = "RBLX VBE 2.0\0"
			for i=1,#oem do RAM[buf+256+i-1]=oem:byte(i) end
			CPU["regs"][1] = 0x004F  -- AX=004Fh (success)
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			emu_debug(1, "[VBE] GET CONTROLLER INFO")
		elseif vbe_fn == 0x01 then
			-- GET MODE INFO: CX=mode, write VbeModeInfoBlock at ES:DI
			local mode = CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0xFFFF
			local di = CPU["regs"][8]
			local es_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] -blshift- 4
			local buf = es_base + di
			-- Clear 256 bytes
			for i=0,255 do RAM[buf+i]=0 end
			-- Supported modes table
			local modes = {
				[0x101]={w=640,h=480,bpp=8,rm=4},
				[0x103]={w=800,h=600,bpp=8,rm=4},
				[0x105]={w=1024,h=768,bpp=8,rm=4},
				[0x111]={w=640,h=480,bpp=16,rm=6},
				[0x113]={w=800,h=600,bpp=16,rm=6},
				[0x118]={w=1024,h=768,bpp=24,rm=5},
			}
			local m = modes[mode]
			if m then
				-- ModeAttributes: supported|color|graphics|linear FB available
				RAM[buf+0] = 0xBB; RAM[buf+1] = 0x00
				-- WinA/B attributes
				RAM[buf+2]=7; RAM[buf+3]=0; RAM[buf+4]=64; RAM[buf+5]=0
				-- WinGranularity=64KB, WinSize=64KB
				RAM[buf+6]=64; RAM[buf+7]=0; RAM[buf+8]=64; RAM[buf+9]=0
				-- WinASegment
				RAM[buf+10]=0; RAM[buf+11]=0xA0
				-- BytesPerScanLine
				local bpsl = m.w * math.ceil(m.bpp/8)
				RAM[buf+16]=bpsl-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+17]=(bpsl-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
				-- Width, Height
				RAM[buf+18]=m.w-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+19]=(m.w-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
				RAM[buf+20]=m.h-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+21]=(m.h-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
				-- CharWidth, CharHeight
				RAM[buf+22]=8; RAM[buf+23]=16
				-- NumberOfPlanes, BitsPerPixel, NumberOfBanks, MemoryModel, BankSize, NumImagePages
				RAM[buf+24]=1; RAM[buf+25]=m.bpp; RAM[buf+26]=1; RAM[buf+27]=m.rm; RAM[buf+28]=64; RAM[buf+29]=0
				-- Linear framebuffer address: 0xE0000000
				local lfb = 0xE0000000
				RAM[buf+40]=(lfb-band-0xFF); RAM[buf+41]=((lfb-brshift-8)-band-0xFF)
				RAM[buf+42]=((lfb-brshift-16)-band-0xFF); RAM[buf+43]=((lfb-brshift-24)-band-0xFF)
				CPU["regs"][1] = 0x004F
				cpu_clear_flag(0)
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[VBE] MODE INFO mode=%04X %dx%dx%d", mode, m.w, m.h, m.bpp))
			else
				CPU["regs"][1] = 0x014F  -- AH=1 failed
				cpu_set_flag(0)
			end
		elseif vbe_fn == 0x02 then
			-- SET VBE MODE: BX=mode
			local mode = CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0x1FF  -- strip linear bit
			local use_lfb = (CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0x4000) ~= 0
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[VBE] SET MODE %04X lfb=%s", mode, tostring(use_lfb)))
			-- Map to video_set_mode equivalent
			if mode == 0x101 or mode == 0x103 or mode == 0x105 then
				video_set_mode(0x13, false)  -- treat as MCGA 256-color for now
			elseif mode == 0x111 or mode == 0x113 then
				video_set_mode(0x13, false)
			elseif mode == 0x118 then
				video_set_mode(0x12, false)
			elseif mode == 0x03 then
				video_set_mode(3, false)     -- text mode
			end
			CPU["regs"][1] = 0x004F
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
		else
			CPU["regs"][1] = 0x014F  -- AH=1 unsupported subfn
			cpu_set_flag(0)
		end
		return true
	else
		-- unknown INT 0x10 AX — set CF, log, continue (do NOT stop execution)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT10] UNKNOWN AX=%04X -> CF=1", ax))
		cpu_set_flag(0)
		return true
	end
end)

-- CRTC ports

local crtc_index = 0

cpu_port_set(0x3D4, function(cond, val)

	if not val then
		return crtc_index
	end

	if val >= 0 and val <= 0x11 then
		crtc_index = val
	end

	-- ⭐ VGA MODE HEURISTIC (Tiny Core boot 필수)
	if not _G.EMU then _G.EMU = {} end

	if val == 0x01 or val == 0x03 then
		_G.EMU.VGA_TEXT_MODE = true
	else
		_G.EMU.VGA_TEXT_MODE = false
	end
end)

local cga_cursor = 0
cpu_port_set(0x3D5, function(cond, val)
	if val then -- writes
		if crtc_index == 0x0E then
			cga_cursor = (cga_cursor -band- 0xFF) -bor- (val -band- 0xFF)
		elseif crtc_index == 0x0F then
			cga_cursor = (cga_cursor -band- 0xFF00) -bor- (val -band- 0xFF)
		end
	else -- reads
		if crtc_index == 0x0E then
			return (cga_cursor -brshift- 8)
		elseif crtc_index == 0x0F then
			return (cga_cursor -band- 0xFF)
		else
			return 0
		end
	end
end)

-- mirroring
for i=0,6,2 do
	cpu_port_set(0x3B0 + i, cpu_port_get(0x3D4))
	cpu_port_set(0x3D0 + i, cpu_port_get(0x3D4))
	cpu_port_set(0x3B1 + i, cpu_port_get(0x3D5))
	cpu_port_set(0x3D1 + i, cpu_port_get(0x3D5))
end

-- ===== disks.lua =====

local drives = {}

RAM[0x475] = 0

local function disk_init_data(fptr, d)
	local fsize = 0
	if fptr ~= nil then
		fsize = fptr:seek("end")
		fptr:seek("set", 0)
	end

	-- print only once on first call
	print(string.format("[disk_init_data] drive=%02X fsize=%d", d.id, fsize))
	d.inserted = true
	if fsize == 0 then
		d.inserted = false
		d.sector_size = 0
		d.sectors = 0
		d.heads = 0
		d.cylinders = 0
	elseif d.floppy then
		d.sector_size = 512
		if fsize == 2949120 then
			d.sectors = 36
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 80
		elseif fsize == 1761280 then
			d.sectors = 21
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 82
		elseif fsize == 1720320 then
			d.sectors = 21
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 80
		elseif fsize == 1474560 then
			d.sectors = 18
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 80
		elseif fsize == 1228800 then
			d.sectors = 15
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 80
		elseif fsize == 737280 then
			d.sectors = 9
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 80
		elseif fsize == (360*1024) then
			d.sectors = 9
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 40
		elseif fsize == (320*1024) then
			d.sectors = 8
			d.heads = 2
			d.cylinders = 40
		elseif fsize == (180*1024) then
			d.sectors = 9
			d.heads = 1
			d.cylinders = 40
		elseif fsize == (160*1024) then
			d.sectors = 8
			d.heads = 1
			d.cylinders = 40
		elseif fsize > 2 * 1024 * 1024 then
			-- Exception for Large ISO/Images (e.g. Tiny Core 20MB)
			-- Force HDD-style geometry even if marked as floppy
			d.sectors = 63
			d.heads = 16
			d.cylinders = math.floor(fsize / (d.sector_size * d.sectors * d.heads))
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[Disk] Large image detected on floppy port, forcing HDD geometry: %d cyls", d.cylinders))
		else
			error("unknown fsize: " .. fsize)
		end
	else
		d.sector_size = 512
		d.sectors = 63
		d.heads = 16
		d.cylinders = math.floor(fsize / (d.sector_size*d.sectors*d.heads))
		if d.cylinders <= 0 then
			-- Fallback for small custom images
			d.cylinders = 1
			if fsize < 512 then d.inserted = false end
		end
	end
	emu_debug(2, string.format("disks: added %d x %d x %d x %d @ %02X", d.cylinders, d.heads, d.sectors, d.sector_size, d.id))

	-- configure table
	local tba = 0xF2000 + d.id*16
	if d.id == 0x80 then
		RAM:w16(0x0104, tba -band- 0xFFFF)
		RAM:w16(0x0106, 0xF000)
	elseif d.id == 0x81 then
		RAM:w16(0x0118, tba -band- 0xFFFF)
		RAM:w16(0x011A, 0xF000)
	elseif d.id == 0x00 then
		RAM:w16(0x0078, tba -band- 0xFFFF)
		RAM:w16(0x007A, 0xF000)
	end
	if d.floppy then
		RAM[tba] = 0xF0
		RAM[tba + 1] = 0x00
		RAM[tba + 2] = 0x00
		RAM[tba + 3] = math.ceil(d.sector_size / 128) - 1
		RAM[tba + 4] = d.sectors
		RAM[tba + 5] = 0
		RAM[tba + 6] = 0
		RAM[tba + 7] = 0
		RAM[tba + 8] = 0xF6
		RAM[tba + 9] = 0
		RAM[tba + 10] = 0
	else
		RAM:w16(tba, d.cylinders)
		RAM[tba + 2] = d.heads
		RAM:w16(tba + 3, 0)
		RAM:w16(tba + 5, 0)
		RAM[tba + 7] = 0
		RAM[tba + 8] = 0xC0
		if d.heads > 8 then
			RAM[tba + 8] = RAM[tba + 8] -bor- 0x08
		end
		RAM[tba + 9] = 0
		RAM[tba + 10] = 0
		RAM[tba + 11] = 0
		RAM:w16(tba + 12, 0)
		RAM[tba + 14] = d.sectors
	end
end

function disk_init(fn, id)
	local d = {}
	d.id = id
	local is_floppy = id < 0x80
	d.floppy = is_floppy

	if type(fn) == "function" then
		d.ptr = fn
	else
		local ptrmode = nil
		local f = nil
		local data_initialized = false
		d.ptr = function(a, mode)
			if ptrmode ~= mode then
				if f ~= nil then f:close() end
				f = io_seek.open(fn, mode)
				if f == nil then return nil end
				-- disk_init_data called only once (initialize drive parameters)
				if not data_initialized then
					disk_init_data(f, a)
					data_initialized = true
				end
				f:seek("set", 0)
				ptrmode = mode
			end
			return f
		end
	end

	drives[id] = d
	if d.id >= 0x80 then
		RAM[0x475] = RAM[0x475] + 1
	end
end

function disk_has(id)
	return drives[id] ~= nil
end

local last_status = 0x00

local function ret_status(v)
	if v ~= nil then
		last_status = v -band- 0xFF
	end
	CPU["regs"][1] = (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (last_status -blshift- 8)
	cpu_write_flag(0, last_status ~= 0)
end

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x13, function(ax,ah,al)
	_G._int13_call_count = (_G._int13_call_count or 0) + 1
	-- Drive aliasing: normalize unknown drive numbers to known CD/HDD drives
	do
		local dx = CPU["regs"][3]
		local dl = bit32.band(dx, 0xFF)
		-- ⭐ FIX: DX=0xFFFF (DH=FF DL=FF) is common from isolinux — normalize BOTH bytes
		-- DH=FF is invalid head number; reset DH=0 for CD-ROM drives
		if dl == 0xFF or dx >= 0xFF00 then
			-- 0xFF = "any CD-ROM" → map to 0x9F (our virtual CD drive)
			local mapped = drives[0x9F] and 0x9F or (drives[0x80] and 0x80 or 0x9F)
			-- ⭐ FIX: Also clear DH (head byte) — DH=0xFF is garbage for CD-ROM
			CPU["regs"][3] = mapped  -- DX = 0x00XX (DH=0, DL=mapped)
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] DL=%02X alias → %02X (DX was %04X)", dl, mapped, dx))
			-- ⭐ Register drives[0xFF] alias so AH=42 lookups work before re-read of DL
			if not drives[0xFF] then drives[0xFF] = drives[mapped] end
		elseif dl >= 0x80 and not drives[dl] then
			-- Unknown HDD/CD drive → try 0x9F first, then 0x80
			local mapped = drives[0x9F] and 0x9F or (drives[0x80] and 0x80 or dl)
			CPU["regs"][3] = bit32.bor(bit32.band(CPU["regs"][3], 0xFF00), mapped)
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] DL=%02X (no drive) alias → %02X", dl, mapped))
		elseif dl < 0x80 and not drives[dl] and drives[0x80] then
			-- Unknown floppy → map to HDD as fallback (El Torito floppy emulation)
			CPU["regs"][3] = bit32.bor(bit32.band(CPU["regs"][3], 0xFF00), 0x80)
		end
	end
	-- 디스크 인터럽트 로깅: 헤더는 레벨2(READ성공), 에러/특수만 레벨1
	emu_debug(2, string.format("[INT13] AH=%02X AL=%02X DX=%04X CX=%04X BX=%04X CS=%04X IP=%04X",
		ah, al, CPU["regs"][3], CPU["regs"][2], CPU["regs"][4], CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
	if ah == 0x00 then
		emu_debug(2, "[INT13] disk reset -> OK")
		ret_status(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x01 then
		emu_debug(2, string.format("[INT13] get status -> %02X", last_status))
		ret_status(nil)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x02 then
		local cx = CPU["regs"][2]
		local dx = CPU["regs"][3]
		local bx = CPU["regs"][4]
		local sector   = bit32.band(cx, 0x3F)
		local cylinder = bit32.rshift(cx, 8)
		local head     = bit32.rshift(dx, 8)
		local drive    = bit32.band(dx, 0xFF)
		if drive >= 0x80 then
			cylinder = bit32.bor(cylinder, bit32.lshift(bit32.band(cx, 0xC0), 2))
		end
		emu_debug(2, string.format("[INT13] READ drv=%02X c=%d h=%d s=%d cnt=%d", drive, cylinder, head, sector, al))
		local d = drives[drive]
		if not d or d:ptr("rb") == nil then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] READ drv=%02X -> NO DRIVE", drive))
			ret_status(1)
			return true
		else
			d:ptr("rb")
			if sector == 0 or sector > d.sectors or head >= d.heads or cylinder >= d.cylinders then
				ret_status(4)
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] READ OUT OF BOUNDS drv=%02X c=%d h=%d s=%d (max c=%d h=%d s=%d)", drive, cylinder, head, sector, d.cylinders-1, d.heads-1, d.sectors))
				return true
			end
		end
		local pos = cylinder
		pos = pos * d.heads + head
		pos = pos * d.sectors + (sector - 1)
		pos = pos * d.sector_size + (d._iso_base or 0)
		emu_debug(2, string.format("[INT13] READ pos=%d bytes=%d -> ES:BX=%04X:%04X", pos, al*d.sector_size, CPU_SEGMENTS[1], bx))
		CPU["regs"][1] = al -- AH = 0 (OK), AL = sectors transferred
		-- ⭐ CRITICAL FIX: use ONE handle for both seek+read
		local fh = d:ptr("rb")
		fh:seek("set", pos)
		local count = al * d.sector_size
		local data = fh:read(count)
		local base = seg(SEG_ES, bx)
		-- process in 512-byte chunks (prevent string.byte stack overflow)
		local RAM_BUF_local = _G.EMU.MEM
		for chunk=0, count-1, 512 do
			local cend = math.min(chunk+511, count-1)
			local bytes = table.pack(string.byte(data, chunk+1, cend+1))
			if RAM_BUF_local and (base + cend) < 134217728 then
				for i=0, cend-chunk do
					buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF_local, base + chunk + i, bytes[i+1] or 0)
				end
			else
				for i=0, cend-chunk do
					RAM[base + chunk + i] = bytes[i+1]
				end
			end
		end
		ret_status(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x03 then
		local cx = CPU["regs"][2]
		local dx = CPU["regs"][3]
		local bx = CPU["regs"][4]
		local sector   = bit32.band(cx, 0x3F)
		local cylinder = bit32.rshift(cx, 8)
		local head     = bit32.rshift(dx, 8)
		local drive    = bit32.band(dx, 0xFF)
		if drive >= 0x80 then
			cylinder = bit32.bor(cylinder, bit32.lshift(bit32.band(cx, 0xC0), 2))
		end
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] WRITE drv=%02X c=%d h=%d s=%d cnt=%d", drive, cylinder, head, sector, al))
		local d = drives[drive]
		if not d or d:ptr("ab") == nil then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] WRITE drv=%02X -> NO DRIVE", drive))
			ret_status(1)
			return true
		else
			d:ptr("ab")
			if sector == 0 or sector > d.sectors or head >= d.heads or cylinder >= d.cylinders then
				ret_status(4)
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] WRITE OUT OF BOUNDS drv=%02X c=%d h=%d s=%d (max c=%d h=%d s=%d)", drive, cylinder, head, sector, d.cylinders-1, d.heads-1, d.sectors))
				return true
			end
		end
		local pos = cylinder
		pos = pos * d.heads + head
		pos = pos * d.sectors + (sector - 1)
		pos = pos * d.sector_size
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] WRITE pos=%d bytes=%d <- ES:BX=%04X:%04X", pos, al*d.sector_size, CPU_SEGMENTS[1], bx))
		CPU["regs"][1] = al -- AH = 0 (OK), AL = sectors transferred
		d:ptr("ab"):seek("set", pos)
		local count = al * d.sector_size
		for i=0,count-1 do
			d:ptr("ab"):write(string.char(RAM[seg(SEG_ES, bx + i)]))
		end
		ret_status(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x04 then -- verify
		emu_debug(1, "[INT13] VERIFY -> OK")
		ret_status(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x08 then -- get drive parameters
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local d = drives[drive]
		if not d or d:ptr("rb") == nil then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] GET PARAMS drv=%02X -> NO DRIVE", drive))
			ret_status(1)
		else
			d:ptr("rb") -- init disk data
			-- ⭐ FIX: CD-ROM (sector_size=2048) returns special values per ATAPI spec
			if (d.sector_size or 512) == 2048 then
				-- CD-ROM: CX=0, DX=DH(max_head)=0 DL(num_drives), AH=0, CF=0
				CPU["regs"][2] = 0  -- CX = 0 (no CHS for CD)
				CPU["regs"][3] = (CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF) -bor- 0x0000  -- DH=0
				CPU["regs"][4] = CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF00  -- BL=0
				CPU["segments"][SEG_ES+1] = 0  -- ES:DI = 0:0
				CPU["regs"][8] = 0  -- DI = 0
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] GET PARAMS drv=%02X CD-ROM -> CX=0 DX=%04X",
					drive, CPU["regs"][3]))
				emu_debug(1, "[INT13] GET PARAMS CD-ROM: returning AH=0 CF=0")
				CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF  -- AH=0
				cpu_clear_flag(0)
			else
				local maxc = d.cylinders - 1
				local numDrives = RAM[0x475]
				if d.floppy then numDrives = ((RAM[0x410] -brshift- 6) -band- 3) + 1 end
				CPU["regs"][2] = ((maxc -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8) -bor- (d.sectors -band- 0x3F) -bor- ((maxc -band- 0x300) -brshift- 2) -- CX = cylinder number -bor- sector number
				CPU["regs"][3] = ((d.heads - 1) -blshift- 8) -bor- numDrives
				CPU["regs"][8] = 2000 + (drive*16)
				CPU["segments"][SEG_ES+1] = 0xF000 -- ES:DI - hdpt ptr
				if d.floppy then
					if d.sectors == 18 then
						CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 4
					else
						CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 3
					end
				else
					CPU["regs"][4] = (CPU["regs"][4] -band- 0xFF00)
				end
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] GET PARAMS drv=%02X c=%d h=%d s=%d floppy=%s -> CX=%04X DX=%04X",
					drive, d.cylinders, d.heads, d.sectors, tostring(d.floppy or false),
					CPU["regs"][2], CPU["regs"][3]))
				emu_debug(1, "[INT13] GET PARAMS HDD: returning AH=0 CF=0")
				ret_status(0)
			end
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x15 then -- get disk type
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local d = drives[drive]
		local code = 0
		if d and d:ptr("rb") ~= nil then
			if d.floppy then code = 1
			else code = 3 end
		end
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] GET TYPE drv=%02X -> AH=%02X (%s)", drive, code,
			code==0 and "no drive" or code==1 and "floppy" or code==3 and "HDD" or "?"))
		cpu_clear_flag(0) -- clear carry
		CPU["regs"][1] = (code -blshift- 8) -bor- (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x18 then -- set media type for format
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local code = 0x80
		if drives[drive] then code = 0 end
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] SET MEDIA TYPE drv=%02X -> %02X", drive, code))
		cpu_clear_flag(0) -- clear carry
		CPU["regs"][1] = (code -blshift- 8) -bor- (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x41 then -- check extensions present (IBM/MS Extensions v1.x)
		print("[emu] [INT13-AH41] LBA CHECK called DX="..string.format("%04X", CPU["regs"][3]).." CS="..string.format("%04X", CPU_SEGMENTS[2]).." IP="..string.format("%04X", CPU_IP))
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local bx = CPU["regs"][4]
		-- ⭐ FIX: isolinux sometimes calls AH=41 with BX already set to other values.
		-- Only require drives[drive] to exist — if so, report LBA support regardless of BX magic
		if drives[drive] then
			-- Extensions present: LBA supported (subset 1)
			CPU["regs"][4] = 0xAA55
			CPU["regs"][2] = (CPU["regs"][2] -band- 0xFF00) -bor- 0x21  -- version 2.1
			CPU["regs"][1] = (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- 0x0100  -- no error AH=0
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] CHECK EXT drv=%02X bx=%04X -> present (v2.1 LBA+EDD)", drive, bx))
		else
			ret_status(1)
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x42 then -- extended read sectors (LBA)
		print("[emu] [INT13-AH42] EXT READ called AX="..string.format("%04X", CPU["regs"][1]).." DX="..string.format("%04X", CPU["regs"][3]).." CS="..string.format("%04X", CPU_SEGMENTS[2]).." IP="..string.format("%04X", CPU_IP))
		local drive = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][3], 0xFF)
		-- ⭐ FIX: Secondary drive remap in case aliasing missed it (e.g. drive still 0xFF)
		if not drives[drive] then
			drive = drives[0x9F] and 0x9F or (drives[0x80] and 0x80 or drive)
			CPU["regs"][3] = bit32.bor(bit32.band(CPU["regs"][3], 0xFF00), drive)
		end
		local si = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][7], 0xFFFF)  -- DS:SI → DAP
		-- ⭐ FIX: isolinux may use DS=0 with absolute SI, or SS:SI.
		-- Try DS:SI first; if DAP size byte is garbage, try SS:SI
		local ds_base = bit32.lshift(CPU["segments"][SEG_DS+1], 4)
		local ss_base = bit32.lshift(CPU["segments"][SEG_SS+1], 4)
		local dap_base = ds_base + si
		-- Validate DAP: first byte must be 0x10 or 0x18 (DAP size)
		local dap_size_byte = RAM[dap_base] or 0
		if dap_size_byte ~= 0x10 and dap_size_byte ~= 0x18 and dap_size_byte ~= 0x13 then
			-- Try SS:SI
			dap_base = ss_base + si
			dap_size_byte = RAM[dap_base] or 0
			if dap_size_byte ~= 0x10 and dap_size_byte ~= 0x18 and dap_size_byte ~= 0x13 then
				-- Try raw SI as absolute address (DS=0 case)
				dap_base = si
				dap_size_byte = RAM[dap_base] or 0
			end
		end
		-- DAP: [0]=size(1), [1]=reserved(1), [2-3]=count(2), [4-7]=buf_off+seg(4), [8-15]=lba(8)
		local count   = bit32.bor(RAM[dap_base+2], bit32.lshift(RAM[dap_base+3], 8))
		local buf_off = bit32.bor(RAM[dap_base+4], bit32.lshift(RAM[dap_base+5], 8))
		local buf_seg = bit32.bor(RAM[dap_base+6], bit32.lshift(RAM[dap_base+7], 8))
		local lba     = bit32.bor(bit32.bor(bit32.bor(
		                  (RAM[dap_base+8]  or 0),
		                  bit32.lshift((RAM[dap_base+9]  or 0), 8)),
		                  bit32.lshift((RAM[dap_base+10] or 0), 16)),
		                  (RAM[dap_base+11] or 0) * 0x1000000)
		-- Guard: count and lba must be sane
		-- For CD-ROM (sector_size=2048), max LBA = total_bytes / 2048
		-- For HDD (sector_size=512), max LBA = total_bytes / 512
		local d_for_maxlba = drives[drive]
		local max_lba
		if d_for_maxlba then
			local ss = d_for_maxlba.sector_size or 2048
			max_lba = d_for_maxlba.cylinders and (d_for_maxlba.cylinders + 64) or 1000000
		else
			max_lba = 1000000
		end
		-- Allow up to 4096 sectors per read (CD-ROM: isolinux may request large counts)
		-- isolinux may request large counts for ldlinux.c32/ldlinux.sys
		if count > 4096 or lba > max_lba then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] EXT READ bad DAP drv=%02X dap_base=%05X size_byte=%02X count=%d lba=%d max=%d — CF=1", drive, dap_base, dap_size_byte, count, lba, max_lba))
			ret_status(1); return true
		end
		if count == 0 then
			-- count=0: isolinux probe — report success with 0 bytes transferred
			CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF  -- AH=0
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true
		end
		local d = drives[drive]
		if not d or d:ptr("rb") == nil then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] EXT READ drv=%02X NO DRIVE", drive))
			ret_status(1); return true
		end
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] EXT READ drv=%02X lba=%d cnt=%d buf=%04X:%04X dap@%05X", drive, lba, count, buf_seg, buf_off, dap_base))
		-- FIX: For CD-ROM (sector_size=2048), LBA and count are BOTH in 2048-byte sectors.
		-- isolinux no-emulation El Torito uses 2048-byte units for count — NOT 512.
		-- For HDD (sector_size=512), LBA and count are in 512-byte sectors.
		local d_ss = d.sector_size or 512
		local byte_off, total
		if d_ss == 2048 then
			-- CD-ROM: both LBA and count in 2048-byte CD sectors
			byte_off = (d._iso_base or 0) + lba * 2048
			total    = count * 2048
		else
			byte_off = (d._iso_base or 0) + lba * d_ss
			total    = count * d_ss
		end
		-- ⭐ CRITICAL FIX: use ONE handle for both seek+read (ptr() creates fresh handle each call)
		local fh = d:ptr("rb")
		fh:seek("set", byte_off)
		local data  = fh:read(total)
		if not data or #data == 0 then
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] EXT READ drv=%02X lba=%d read returned empty!", drive, lba))
			ret_status(1); return true
		end
		local base  = bit32.lshift(buf_seg, 4) + buf_off
		-- Write data to RAM: ALWAYS use MEM buffer directly (bypasses VRAM routing).
		-- ldlinux.c32 may request writes to 0xA0000-0xBFFFF (VRAM range segs like A80B),
		-- but those are real memory allocations, not VRAM. Writing via RAM metatable
		-- routes them through video_vram_write which doesn't persist for code execution.
		local data_len = #data
		local RAM_BUF_local = _G.EMU.MEM
		if RAM_BUF_local and base + data_len <= 134217728 then
			-- Direct buffer write — bypasses VRAM/ROM routing (correct for disk loads)
			for i = 0, data_len - 1 do
				buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF_local, base + i, data:byte(i+1) or 0)
			end
		else
			for i = 0, data_len - 1 do
				RAM[base + i] = data:byte(i+1) or 0
			end
		end
		-- update DAP transfer count
		RAM[dap_base+2] = bit32.band(count, 0xFF); RAM[dap_base+3] = bit32.band(bit32.rshift(count, 8), 0xFF)
		CPU["regs"][1] = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][1], 0xFF)  -- AH=0
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		-- FIX: Raise IRQ14 after EXT READ to unblock HLT-waiting isolinux/ldlinux
		if pic_raise_irq then
			_G._force_irq14_unmask = true
			pic_raise_irq(14)
			_G._force_irq14_unmask = false
			CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
			if pic then pic.int_pending = 1 end
		end
		_G._int13_call_count = (_G._int13_call_count or 0) + 1
		-- ⭐ Mark ldlinux as loaded once we've done a significant disk read from guest code
		-- (CS != 9BF0 means we're past isolinux stage1)
		if CPU_SEGMENTS[2] ~= 0x9BF0 and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] ~= 0x07C0 and not _G._ldlinux_loaded then
			_G._ldlinux_loaded = true
			print(string.format("[boot] ldlinux active - CS=%04X, disabling BIOS-IRET CS fix", CPU_SEGMENTS[2]))
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x43 then -- extended write sectors (LBA)
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local si = CPU["regs"][7] -band- 0xFFFF
		local dap_base = (CPU["segments"][SEG_DS+1] -blshift- 4) + si
		local count   = RAM[dap_base+2] -bor- (RAM[dap_base+3] -blshift- 8)
		local buf_off = RAM[dap_base+4] -bor- (RAM[dap_base+5] -blshift- 8)
		local buf_seg = RAM[dap_base+6] -bor- (RAM[dap_base+7] -blshift- 8)
		local lba     = (RAM[dap_base+8] or 0) -bor- ((RAM[dap_base+9] or 0) -blshift- 8)
		              -bor- ((RAM[dap_base+10] or 0) -blshift- 16) -bor- ((RAM[dap_base+11] or 0) * 0x1000000)
		local d = drives[drive]
		if not d or d:ptr("ab") == nil then ret_status(1); return true end
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] EXT WRITE drv=%02X lba=%d cnt=%d", drive, lba, count))
		d:ptr("ab"):seek("set", lba * d.sector_size)
		local base = (buf_seg -blshift- 4) + buf_off
		local total = count * d.sector_size
		for i=0,total-1 do d:ptr("ab"):write(string.char(RAM[base+i] or 0)) end
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF; cpu_clear_flag(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x48 then -- get extended drive parameters
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		local d = drives[drive]
		local si = CPU["regs"][7] -band- 0xFFFF
		local buf = (CPU["segments"][SEG_DS+1] -blshift- 4) + si
		if d and d:ptr("rb") then
			local total = d.cylinders * d.heads * d.sectors
			-- write 0x1A byte EDD parameter block
			RAM[buf+0]=0x1A; RAM[buf+1]=0
			RAM[buf+2]=0x03; RAM[buf+3]=0  -- info flags: LBA+CHS
			-- cylinders
			RAM[buf+4]=d.cylinders-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+5]=(d.cylinders-brshift-8)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+6]=0; RAM[buf+7]=0
			-- heads
			RAM[buf+8]=d.heads-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+9]=(d.heads-brshift-8)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+10]=0; RAM[buf+11]=0
			-- sectors/track
			RAM[buf+12]=d.sectors-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+13]=(d.sectors-brshift-8)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+14]=0; RAM[buf+15]=0
			-- total sectors (64-bit LE)
			RAM[buf+16]=total-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+17]=(total-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
			RAM[buf+18]=(total-brshift-16)-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+19]=(total-brshift-24)-band-0xFF
			RAM[buf+20]=0; RAM[buf+21]=0; RAM[buf+22]=0; RAM[buf+23]=0
			-- sector size
			RAM[buf+24]=d.sector_size-band-0xFF; RAM[buf+25]=(d.sector_size-brshift-8)-band-0xFF
			CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF; cpu_clear_flag(0)
		else
			ret_status(1)
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x4B then -- El Torito: terminate/query disk emulation
		local al_func = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		if al_func == 0x00 then -- terminate disk emulation
			-- No-emulation mode: nothing to terminate, just succeed
			CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF  -- AH=0
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			emu_debug(1, "[INT13] El Torito terminate emulation -> OK")
		elseif al_func == 0x01 then -- query emulation status
			local si  = CPU["regs"][7] -band- 0xFFFF
			local buf = (CPU["segments"][SEG_DS+1] -blshift- 4) + si
			-- Fill 19-byte specification packet
			local ep = _G.eltorito_params or {}
			RAM[buf+0]  = 19          -- size
			RAM[buf+1]  = ep.media_type or 0  -- media type (0=no emulation)
			RAM[buf+2]  = ep.dl or 0x9F       -- drive number used
			RAM[buf+3]  = 0           -- controller index
			local lba = ep.img_lba or 0
			RAM[buf+4]  = lba -band- 0xFF;        RAM[buf+5]  = (lba -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF
			RAM[buf+6]  = (lba -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFF; RAM[buf+7]  = (lba -brshift- 24) -band- 0xFF
			RAM[buf+8]  = (ep.dl or 0x9F); RAM[buf+9] = 0  -- device spec
			local sc = ep.sec_count or 1
			RAM[buf+10] = sc -band- 0xFF; RAM[buf+11] = (sc -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF
			RAM[buf+12] = 0; RAM[buf+13] = 0; RAM[buf+14] = 0; RAM[buf+15] = 0
			RAM[buf+16] = 0; RAM[buf+17] = 0; RAM[buf+18] = 0
			CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			emu_debug(1, "[INT13] El Torito query emulation -> OK")
		else
			cpu_clear_flag(0)  -- unknown subfunction, succeed silently
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0C then -- seek to cylinder (CD-ROM: always OK)
		cpu_clear_flag(0); CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x10 then -- check if drive is ready
		local drive = CPU["regs"][3] -band- 0xFF
		if drives[drive] then
			cpu_clear_flag(0); CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF  -- AH=0 ready
		else
			ret_status(0xAA)  -- drive not ready
		end
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x11 then -- recalibrate drive
		cpu_clear_flag(0); CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0D then -- reset fixed disk controller
		cpu_clear_flag(0); CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x0E or ah == 0x0F then -- XT buffer read/write (obsolete, stub)
		cpu_clear_flag(0); CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		return true
	else
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT13] UNKNOWN AH=%02X -> CF=1", ah))
		cpu_set_flag(0)
		return true  -- unknown but do NOT stop execution
	end
end)

function disk_boot(id)
	local f = drives[id]:ptr("rb")
	local boot_dl = id
	local boot_cs = 0x0000
	local boot_ip = 0x7C00
	local loaded = false

	-- Try El Torito boot: check Boot Record Volume Descriptor at sector 17
	f:seek("set", 34816)  -- sector 17 × 2048
	local brvd = f:read(2048)
	if brvd and #brvd >= 74 and brvd:byte(1) == 0 and brvd:sub(2,6) == "CD001"
	   and brvd:sub(8,30):find("EL TORITO SPECIFICATION", 1, true) then
		-- Parse boot catalog LBA (bytes 71-74, 1-indexed = offsets 70-73)
		local cat_lba = brvd:byte(72) + brvd:byte(73)*256 + brvd:byte(74)*65536 + brvd:byte(75)*16777216
		f:seek("set", cat_lba * 2048)
		local catalog = f:read(64)  -- validation entry (32) + default entry (32)
		if catalog and #catalog >= 64 then
			local bootable    = catalog:byte(33)  -- 0x88 = bootable
			local media_type  = catalog:byte(34)  -- 0=no-emulation, 1-3=floppy
			local load_seg    = catalog:byte(35) + catalog:byte(36)*256  -- load segment (0=0x07C0)
			local sec_count   = catalog:byte(39) + catalog:byte(40)*256  -- 512-byte sectors to load
			local img_lba     = catalog:byte(41) + catalog:byte(42)*256
			                  + catalog:byte(43)*65536 + catalog:byte(44)*16777216
			if load_seg == 0 then load_seg = 0x07C0 end
			if sec_count == 0 then sec_count = 1 end
			local load_base   = load_seg * 16  -- physical address
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[El Torito] catalog_lba=%d bootable=%02X media=%d img_lba=%d sec=%d seg=%04X",
				cat_lba, bootable, media_type, img_lba, sec_count, load_seg))
			if bootable == 0x88 then
				-- CRITICAL FIX: El Torito sec_count=4 only loads 2KB,
				-- but isolinux.bin is ~20-30KB. Get real size from ISO9660.
				local actual_size = 0
				if _G._iso9660 and _G.EMU.diskData then
					local pvd_s = _G._iso9660.read_sector(_G.EMU.diskData, 16)
					if pvd_s and pvd_s:byte(1)==1 then
						local rl = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd_s, 157+1)
						local rs = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd_s, 157+9)
						local fl, fs = _G._iso9660.find_file(_G.EMU.diskData, rl, rs, "ISOLINUX.BIN")
						if fl and fs and fs > 0 then
							actual_size = fs
							emu_debug(1, string.format("[El Torito] ISO9660 ISOLINUX.BIN size=%d", actual_size))
						end
					end
				end
				-- Load full isolinux.bin: minimum 32KB, cap at 64KB
				local load_size = math.max(actual_size, sec_count * 512, 32768)
				load_size = math.min(load_size, 65536)
				f:seek("set", img_lba * 2048)
				local bootsec = f:read(load_size)
				if bootsec then
					local RAM_BUF_load = _G.EMU.MEM
					local bootsec_len = math.min(load_size-1, #bootsec-1)
					for i=0,bootsec_len do
						local b = bootsec:byte(i+1)
						if RAM_BUF_load and load_base+i < 134217728 then
							buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF_load, load_base+i, b)
						else
							RAM[load_base+i] = b
						end
					end
					-- ⭐⭐ CRITICAL FIX: Pre-copy isolinux.bin to 0x9BF00 (isolinux relocation target)
					-- isolinux REP MOVSW copies itself from 0x7C00 -> 0x9BF00 during boot.
					-- Pre-populating 0x9BF00 ensures correct execution even if CPU MOVSW
					-- result is not visible in buffer due to metatable vs buffer mismatch.
					local reloc_base = 0x9BF00
					for i=0,bootsec_len do
						local b = bootsec:byte(i+1)
						if RAM_BUF_load and reloc_base+i < 134217728 then
							buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF_load, reloc_base+i, b)
						else
							RAM[reloc_base+i] = b
						end
					end
					print(string.format("[El Torito] Pre-copied %d bytes to 0x9BF00 (isolinux reloc target)", bootsec_len+1))
					loaded = true
					boot_cs = load_seg
					boot_ip = 0x0000
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[El Torito] Loaded %d bytes at %04X:0000 + pre-copied to 9BF00", #bootsec, load_seg))
					-- Dump first 16 bytes to verify isolinux.bin content
					local dbg = {}
					for di=0,math.min(15,#bootsec-1) do dbg[di+1]=string.format("%02X",bootsec:byte(di+1)) end
					emu_debug(1, "[El Torito] first16: "..table.concat(dbg," "))
					-- Also dump bytes at offset 0xBF0 (where CS=9BF0 code may start)
					local dbg2 = {}
					for di=0xBF0,math.min(0xBFF,#bootsec-1) do dbg2[#dbg2+1]=string.format("%02X",bootsec:byte(di+1)) end
					emu_debug(1, "[El Torito] @0xBF0: "..table.concat(dbg2," "))
					-- Verify 0x9BF00 was pre-populated
					local rbuf={}
					for di=0,15 do
						if RAM_BUF_load then
							rbuf[di+1]=string.format("%02X",buffer.readu8(RAM_BUF_load, reloc_base+di))
						else
							rbuf[di+1]=string.format("%02X",RAM[reloc_base+di] or 0)
						end
					end
					emu_debug(1, "[El Torito] RAM@9BF00 (pre-copy verify): "..table.concat(rbuf," "))
				end
				if media_type == 0 then
					-- No-emulation: virtual CD drive at 0x9F
					boot_dl = 0x9F
					if not drives[0x9F] then
						-- ⭐ FIX: Give drives[0x9F] its own ptr() that reads 2048-byte ISO sectors
						-- The parent drives[id].ptr reads from "drive:80" with sector_size=512,
						-- which is WRONG for CD-ROM. We need raw byte-offset reads at 2048/sector.
						local cd_data = _G.EMU.diskData  -- use the in-memory ISO string directly
						local cd_total_sectors = math.ceil(#cd_data / 2048)
						local cd_obj = {
							sector_size = 2048,
							id = 0x9F,
							sectors = cd_total_sectors,
							heads = 1,
							cylinders = cd_total_sectors,
							floppy = false,
							inserted = true,
						}
						-- FIXED: ptr() returns a NEW independent handle each call (no shared seek state)
						-- This prevents seek position conflicts when INT 13h calls ptr() multiple times
						cd_obj.ptr = function(_, mode)
							local cd_pos = 0
							local cd_sz = #cd_data
							return {
								seek = function(_, w, off)
									off = off or 0
									if     w == "set" then cd_pos = off
									elseif w == "cur" then cd_pos = cd_pos + off
									elseif w == "end" then cd_pos = cd_sz + off end
									if cd_pos < 0 then cd_pos = 0 end
									return cd_pos
								end,
								read = function(_, n)
									if type(n) == "number" then
										local s = string.sub(cd_data, cd_pos+1, cd_pos+n)
										cd_pos = math.min(cd_pos + n, cd_sz)
										return s
									end
									local s = string.sub(cd_data, cd_pos+1)
									cd_pos = cd_sz
									return s
								end,
								write = function() end,
								close = function() end,
							}
						end
						drives[0x9F] = cd_obj
						drives[0xFF] = cd_obj  -- alias for DX=FFFF
						if not drives[0x80] then drives[0x80] = cd_obj end  -- 0x80 alias
					end
					-- Store for INT 13h AH=0x4B AL=0x01 query
					_G.eltorito_params = {media_type=0, dl=0x9F, img_lba=img_lba, sec_count=sec_count}
					emu_debug(1, "[El Torito] No-emulation boot → DL=0x9F, CD sector_size=2048 (in-memory)")
				else
					-- Floppy emulation: the boot image IS the floppy image
					boot_dl = 0x00
					-- Register the floppy image as drive 0x00
					-- (img_lba * 2048 = byte offset of floppy image inside ISO)
					if not drives[0x00] then
						drives[0x00] = setmetatable({
							sector_size=512, id=0x00, floppy=true,
							sectors=18, heads=2, cylinders=80,
							_iso_base = img_lba * 2048  -- byte offset of floppy image in ISO
						}, {__index=drives[id]})
					end
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[El Torito] Floppy-emulation (type=%d) → DL=0x00, floppy_base=0x%X",
						media_type, img_lba * 2048))
				end
			end
		end
	end

	-- Fallback: MBR boot (first 512 bytes of image)
	if not loaded then
		f:seek("set", 0)
		local bootsector = f:read(512)
		if bootsector and #bootsector >= 512 then
			local RAM_BUF = _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM
			for i=0,511 do
				local b = bootsector:byte(i+1)
				if RAM_BUF and (0x7C00+i) < 134217728 then
					buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF, 0x7C00+i, b)
				end
				RAM[0x7c00+i] = b  -- keep table in sync too
			end
			-- Also load first 32KB to catch larger boot images
			f:seek("set", 0)
			local full_boot = f:read(32768)
			if full_boot and RAM_BUF then
				for i=0,math.min(#full_boot-1, 32767) do
					if (0x7C00+i) < 134217728 then
						buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF, 0x7C00+i, full_boot:byte(i+1))
					end
				end
			end
			print(string.format("[disk_boot] MBR fallback: loaded %d bytes at 0x7C00 (first byte=%02X)", #bootsector, bootsector:byte(1)))
		else
			print("[disk_boot] WARNING: MBR read failed! bootsector is nil/short")
		end
		emu_debug(1, "[disk_boot] MBR boot (no El Torito)")
		boot_cs = 0x0000
		boot_ip = 0x7C00
	end

	cpu_set_ip(boot_cs, boot_ip)
	CPU["regs"][3] = 0x0000 -bor- boot_dl
	CPU["regs"][5] = 0x8000
end

-- ⭐⭐⭐ ISO 9660 Pre-loader (flat, no nested closures to avoid local register limit)
-- Reads ldlinux.sys from ISO and loads into RAM before CPU starts
_G._iso9660 = {}
_G._iso9660.read_u32le = function(s, off)
	return s:byte(off+1) + s:byte(off+2)*256 + s:byte(off+3)*65536 + s:byte(off+4)*16777216
end
_G._iso9660.read_sector = function(iso, lba)
	local off = lba * 2048 + 1
	if off + 2047 > #iso then return nil end
	return iso:sub(off, off + 2047)
end
_G._iso9660.find_file = function(iso, dir_lba, dir_size, target, depth, _visited)
	-- target is already uppercased; depth prevents infinite recursion
	depth = depth or 0
	if depth > 5 then return nil, nil end
	-- ⭐ FIX: Track visited LBAs to prevent infinite recursion (. and .. loop)
	_visited = _visited or {}
	if _visited[dir_lba] then return nil, nil end
	_visited[dir_lba] = true

	local lba = dir_lba
	local read_u32le = _G._iso9660.read_u32le
	local read_sector = _G._iso9660.read_sector
	local bytes = 0
	local subdirs = {}
	while bytes < dir_size do
		local sec = read_sector(iso, lba)
		if not sec then break end
		local pos = 0
		while pos < 2048 do
			local rec = sec:byte(pos+1)
			if rec == 0 then break end
			-- ⭐ FIX: rec must be even and at least 34 to be a valid directory record
			if rec < 34 then break end

			local flags = sec:byte(pos+26)
			local is_dir = (flags % 4) >= 2
			local nlen = sec:byte(pos+33)

			-- ⭐ FIX: Skip dot (.) and dotdot (..) by raw file identifier byte, not by uppercased string
			-- ISO9660 spec: nlen=1 and name byte is 0x00 (.) or 0x01 (..)
			local is_dot_entry = (nlen == 1) and (sec:byte(pos+34) == 0x00 or sec:byte(pos+34) == 0x01)

			if not is_dot_entry then
				local nm = sec:sub(pos+34, pos+33+nlen)
				local base = nm:match("^([^;]+)") or nm
				local entryType = is_dir and "DIR" or "FILE"
				-- Print at depth 0 or 1 to see BOOT contents
				if depth <= 1 then
					print(string.format("[ISO9660] depth=%d lba=%d %s '%s' (raw len=%d)", depth, lba, entryType, base, nlen))
				end
				local base_up = base:upper()
				-- ⭐ FIX: prefix match도 지원 (vmlinuz-5.x.x 같은 버전 포함 파일명)
				local is_match = (base_up == target)
				if not is_match then
					-- target이 prefix인지 확인 (VMLINUZ, BZIMAGE, CORE, INITRD)
					local prefixes = {"VMLINUZ", "BZIMAGE", "CORE", "INITRD", "ROOTFS"}
					for _, pfx in ipairs(prefixes) do
						if target == pfx and base_up:sub(1,#pfx) == pfx then
							is_match = true; break
						end
					end
				end
				if not is_dir and is_match then
					return read_u32le(sec, pos+3), read_u32le(sec, pos+11)
				end
				if is_dir then
					local dn = base:upper()
					local sl = read_u32le(sec, pos+3)
					local ss = read_u32le(sec, pos+11)
					-- Prioritize known boot dirs, collect others for later
					if dn == "ISOLINUX" or dn == "BOOT" or dn == "SYSLINUX" then
						local fl, fs = _G._iso9660.find_file(iso, sl, ss, target, depth+1, _visited)
						if fl then return fl, fs end
					else
						table.insert(subdirs, {sl, ss})
					end
				end
			end
			pos = pos + rec
		end
		lba = lba + 1; bytes = bytes + 2048
	end
	-- Search remaining subdirs if not found in priority dirs
	for _, sd in ipairs(subdirs) do
		local fl, fs = _G._iso9660.find_file(iso, sd[1], sd[2], target, depth+1, _visited)
		if fl then return fl, fs end
	end
	return nil, nil
end
function iso9660_preload_ldlinux(iso)
	if not iso or #iso < 36864 then return false end
	local rs = _G._iso9660.read_sector
	local ru = _G._iso9660.read_u32le
	local ff = _G._iso9660.find_file
	local pvd = rs(iso, 16)
	if not pvd or pvd:byte(1) ~= 1 or pvd:sub(2,6) ~= "CD001" then
		print("[ISO9660] no PVD"); return false
	end
	local root_lba  = ru(pvd, 157 + 1)
	local root_size = ru(pvd, 157 + 9)
	print(string.format("[ISO9660] Root dir lba=%d size=%d", root_lba, root_size))
	-- ⭐ FIX: Extended target list — TinyCore uses vmlinuz+core.gz (not ldlinux.sys)
	-- Priority order: ldlinux files first (for ISOLINUX), then TinyCore kernel files
	local TARGETS = {
		"LDLINUX.SYS", "LDLINUX.C32", "ISOLINUX.BIN",
		"VMLINUZ", "BZIMAGE", "VMLINUX",           -- Linux kernel images
		"CORE.GZ", "ROOTFS.GZ", "INITRD.GZ", "INITRD",  -- initrd/rootfs
	}
	local found_any = false
	-- ⭐ Load addresses for each file type (above 0x10000 to not conflict with boot)
	local load_addrs = {
		["LDLINUX.SYS"]  = 0x10000,
		["LDLINUX.C32"]  = 0x10000,
		["ISOLINUX.BIN"] = 0x10000,
		["VMLINUZ"]      = 0x100000,  -- kernel loads at 1MB
		["BZIMAGE"]      = 0x100000,
		["VMLINUX"]      = 0x100000,
		["CORE.GZ"]      = 0x800000,  -- initrd at 8MB
		["ROOTFS.GZ"]    = 0x800000,
		["INITRD.GZ"]    = 0x800000,
		["INITRD"]       = 0x800000,
	}
	-- ⭐ FIX: Always load ALL targets — never early-return after finding LDLINUX.
	-- ldlinux.c32 needs vmlinuz+core.gz pre-loaded in RAM to boot TinyCore.
	local found_kernel = false
	local found_initrd = false
	for _, tgt in ipairs(TARGETS) do
		local fl, fs = ff(iso, root_lba, root_size, tgt)
		if fl and fs and fs > 0 then
			print(string.format("[ISO9660] %s lba=%d size=%d", tgt, fl, fs))
			local addr = load_addrs[tgt] or 0x10000
			local done = 0
			local secs = math.ceil(fs/2048)
			for s = 0, secs-1 do
				local sec = rs(iso, fl+s)
				if not sec then break end
				local chunk = math.min(2048, fs-done)
				local RAM_BUF = _G.EMU.MEM
				if RAM_BUF and addr+done+chunk <= 134217728 then
					for i = 0, chunk-1 do
						buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF, addr+done+i, sec:byte(i+1) or 0)
					end
				else
					for i = 0, chunk-1 do RAM[addr+done+i] = sec:byte(i+1) or 0 end
				end
				done = done + chunk
			end
			print(string.format("[ISO9660] Loaded %s -> RAM[%05X] %d bytes", tgt, addr, done))
			if tgt == "VMLINUZ" or tgt == "BZIMAGE" or tgt == "VMLINUX" then
				_G._kernel_lba  = fl
				_G._kernel_size = fs
				_G._kernel_addr = addr
				found_kernel = true
				print(string.format("[ISO9660] Kernel metadata: lba=%d size=%d addr=0x%X", fl, fs, addr))
			elseif tgt == "CORE.GZ" or tgt == "ROOTFS.GZ" or tgt == "INITRD.GZ" or tgt == "INITRD" then
				_G._initrd_lba  = fl
				_G._initrd_size = fs
				_G._initrd_addr = addr
				found_initrd = true
