				print(string.format("[ISO9660] Initrd metadata: lba=%d size=%d addr=0x%X", fl, fs, addr))
			end
			found_any = true
			-- ⭐ DO NOT early-return even for LDLINUX — always load kernel+initrd too
		end
	end
	if found_kernel and found_initrd then
		print("[ISO9660] Pre-load complete: kernel + initrd loaded into RAM")
		-- Write kernel/initrd locations to BIOS scratch area (0x9000) for reference
		local function w32(addr, val)
			if _G.EMU.MEM then
				buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr,   val % 256)
				buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr+1, math.floor(val/256) % 256)
				buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr+2, math.floor(val/65536) % 256)
				buffer.writeu8(_G.EMU.MEM, addr+3, math.floor(val/16777216) % 256)
			end
		end
		w32(0x9000, _G._kernel_addr or 0x100000)
		w32(0x9004, _G._kernel_size or 0)
		w32(0x9008, _G._initrd_addr or 0x800000)
		w32(0x900C, _G._initrd_size or 0)
	end
	if not found_any then
		print("[ISO9660] ldlinux.sys not found — INT 13h will handle it")
		-- ⭐ EMERGENCY: Exhaustive scan of ALL files in ISO to find kernel+initrd anywhere
		print("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY SCAN: listing all files in BOOT dir")
		local function list_dir(iso, lba, size, prefix, maxdepth)
			if maxdepth <= 0 then return end
			local bytes = 0
			while bytes < size do
				local sec = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, lba)
				if not sec then break end
				local pos = 0
				while pos < 2048 do
					local rec = sec:byte(pos+1)
					if rec == 0 then break end
					if rec < 34 then break end
					local flags = sec:byte(pos+26)
					local is_dir = (flags % 4) >= 2
					local nlen = sec:byte(pos+33)
					local is_dot = (nlen == 1) and (sec:byte(pos+34) == 0x00 or sec:byte(pos+34) == 0x01)
					if not is_dot then
						local nm = sec:sub(pos+34, pos+33+nlen)
						local fl = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(sec, pos+3)
						local fs = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(sec, pos+11)
						print(string.format("[ISO9660-LS] %s%s %s lba=%d size=%d", prefix, is_dir and "[DIR] " or "[FILE] ", nm, fl, fs))
						if is_dir and maxdepth > 1 then
							list_dir(iso, fl, fs, prefix.."..", maxdepth-1)
						end
					end
					pos = pos + rec
				end
				lba = lba + 1; bytes = bytes + 2048
			end
		end
		local pvd = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, 16)
		if pvd then
			local rl = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd, 158)
			local rs2 = _G._iso9660.read_u32le(pvd, 166)
			list_dir(iso, rl, rs2, "", 3)
			-- ⭐ EMERGENCY LOAD: Try harder with additional kernel/initrd names (TinyCore uses vmlinuz + core.gz)
			-- TinyCore Core ISO layout: /boot/vmlinuz  /boot/core.gz
			print("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY: attempting deep kernel+initrd recovery...")
			local extra_targets = {
				{"VMLINUZ", 0x100000}, {"BZIMAGE", 0x100000}, {"VMLINUX", 0x100000},
				{"CORE.GZ", 0x800000}, {"ROOTFS.GZ", 0x800000}, {"INITRD.GZ", 0x800000},
				{"INITRD", 0x800000}, {"CORE", 0x800000},
				-- TinyCore specific: sometimes named without extension
				{"VMLINUZ64", 0x100000}, {"KERNEL", 0x100000},
			}
			local em_found_k, em_found_i = false, false
			for _, tv in ipairs(extra_targets) do
				local tgt, addr = tv[1], tv[2]
				local fl, fs2 = _G._iso9660.find_file(iso, rl, rs2, tgt)
				if fl and fs2 and fs2 > 0 then
					print(string.format("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY found %s lba=%d size=%d", tgt, fl, fs2))
					local done = 0
					local RAM_BUF = _G.EMU.MEM
					for s = 0, math.ceil(fs2/2048)-1 do
						local sec = _G._iso9660.read_sector(iso, fl+s)
						if not sec then break end
						local chunk = math.min(2048, fs2-done)
						if RAM_BUF and addr+done+chunk <= 134217728 then
							for i = 0, chunk-1 do
								buffer.writeu8(RAM_BUF, addr+done+i, sec:byte(i+1) or 0)
							end
						end
						done = done + chunk
					end
					print(string.format("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY loaded %s → RAM[%05X] %d bytes", tgt, addr, done))
					if addr == 0x100000 then
						_G._kernel_lba = fl; _G._kernel_size = fs2; _G._kernel_addr = addr
						em_found_k = true
					else
						_G._initrd_lba = fl; _G._initrd_size = fs2; _G._initrd_addr = addr
						em_found_i = true
					end
					found_any = true
				end
			end
			if em_found_k and em_found_i then
				print("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY recovery complete: kernel+initrd loaded!")
			elseif em_found_k then
				print("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY: kernel found but initrd missing — boot may fail")
			else
				print("[ISO9660] EMERGENCY: no kernel/initrd found — relying purely on El Torito + INT13h")
			end
		end
	end
	return found_any
end

-- ===== keyboard.lua =====

-- TODO: The keyboard code is a massive hack which in no way reflects real hardware.

-- joysticks (for now)
cpu_port_set(0x201, function(cond,val)
	if not val then
		return 0
	end
end)

local charqueue = {}
local kbd_data_queue = {}

local function populate_bitmask(kz)
	local keys = 0
	for i,k in ipairs(kz) do
		if k >= 0 and platform_key_down(k) then
			keys = keys -bor- (1 -blshift- (i - 1))
		end
	end
	return keys
end

function keyboard_update()
	RAM[0x417] = populate_bitmask({0x36, 0x2A, 0x1D, 0x38, 0x46, -1, 0x3A, 0x52})
	RAM[0x418] = populate_bitmask({-1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1})
end

function kbd_send_ibm(code, chr)
	while #kbd_data_queue > 0 do table.remove(kbd_data_queue, 1) end
	if code <= 0x7F then
		table.insert(charqueue, {code, chr or 0})
	end
	table.insert(kbd_data_queue, code)
	-- emu_debug removed: logging every key causes lag
	if pic_interrupt_enabled(PIC_INTERRUPT_KEYBOARD) then
		cpu_emit_interrupt(9, false)
	end
end

RAM[0x471] = 0 -- break key check
RAM[0x496] = 0 -- keyboard mode/type
RAM[0x497] = 0 -- keyboard LED flags
RAM[0x417] = 0 -- keyboard flags 1
RAM[0x418] = 0 -- keyboard flags 2

local kbd_port_b = 0x03
local kbd_spkr_latch = 0

function kbd_get_spkr_latch()
	local v = kbd_spkr_latch
	kbd_spkr_latch = 0
	return v
end

function kbd_get_port_b()
	return kbd_port_b
end

local kbd_status = 0x10
local kbd_a2 = 0
local kbd_cmd = 0       -- last command written to port 0x64
-- a20_enabled은 emu_core.lua 상단에서 글로벌로 선언됨 (RAM 메타테이블과 공유)

-- keyboard I/O
cpu_port_set(0x60, function(cond,val)
	if not val then
		-- port 0x60 read
		if #kbd_data_queue > 0 then
			local v = kbd_data_queue[1]
			table.remove(kbd_data_queue, 1)
			if type(v) == "table" then return v[1] end
			return v
		end
		return 0x00
	else
		-- port 0x60 write: data byte for last 0x64 command
		if kbd_cmd == 0xD1 then
			-- Write Output Port: bit1 = A20 enable
			a20_enabled = (val -band- 0x02) ~= 0
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[KBD] A20 via 0xD1: %s (val=%02X)", tostring(a20_enabled), val))
			kbd_cmd = 0
		elseif kbd_cmd == 0xD2 then
			-- Write Keyboard Output Buffer
			table.insert(kbd_data_queue, val)
			kbd_cmd = 0
		else
			kbd_a2 = 0
			if val == 5 then
				kbd_data_queue = {}
				table.insert(kbd_data_queue, 0x00)
				table.insert(kbd_data_queue, 0x00)
				table.insert(kbd_data_queue, 0x00)
			end
		end
	end
end)

cpu_port_set(0x61, function(cond,val)
	if not val then
		return kbd_port_b
	else
		kbd_port_b = val
		kbd_spkr_latch = kbd_spkr_latch -bor- val
	end
end)

cpu_port_set(0x64, function(cond,val)
	if not val then
		-- port 0x64 read: status register
		-- bit0=output buffer full, bit1=input buffer full, bit2=system, bit5=output full (IBF)
		local ibf = (#kbd_data_queue > 0) and 1 or 0
		local v = 0x10 -bor- (kbd_a2 -blshift- 3) -bor- ibf
		return v
	else
		-- port 0x64 write: controller command
		kbd_cmd = val
		kbd_a2 = 1
		if val == 0xAD then
			-- Disable keyboard — ignore
		elseif val == 0xAE then
			-- Enable keyboard — ignore
		elseif val == 0xD0 then
			-- Read Output Port → queue result (bit1=A20)
			local outport = 0xDC -bor- (a20_enabled and 0x02 or 0x00)
			table.insert(kbd_data_queue, outport)
		elseif val == 0xD1 then
			-- Write Output Port (data comes next via port 0x60)
			-- handled above when 0x60 is written
		elseif val == 0xDF then
			-- Enable A20 (Fast Gate via KBC)
			a20_enabled = true
			emu_debug(1, "[KBD] A20 enabled via 0xDF")
			kbd_cmd = 0
		elseif val == 0xDD then
			-- Disable A20 (Fast Gate via KBC)
			a20_enabled = false
			emu_debug(1, "[KBD] A20 disabled via 0xDD")
			kbd_cmd = 0
		elseif val == 0xFE then
			-- Pulse output port (system reset)
			emu_debug(1, "[KBD] System reset pulse (0xFE) — ignored")
			kbd_cmd = 0
		else
			kbd_cmd = 0
		end
	end
end)

-- Port 0x92: Fast A20 Gate (PS/2 system port)
local port92 = 0x02  -- bit1=A20 enabled, bit0=reset (0=normal)
cpu_port_set(0x92, function(cond,val)
	if not val then
		-- read: bit1=A20 state, bit0=reset status
		return (a20_enabled and 0x02 or 0x00) -bor- 0x00
	else
		-- write: bit1=A20 enable/disable, bit0=reset (if set, triggers reset)
		if (val -band- 0x01) ~= 0 then
			emu_debug(1, "[PORT92] System reset bit set — ignored")
		end
		local new_a20 = (val -band- 0x02) ~= 0
		if new_a20 ~= a20_enabled then
			a20_enabled = new_a20
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[PORT92] A20 %s", a20_enabled and "enabled" or "disabled"))
		end
		port92 = val -band- 0xFE  -- clear reset bit
	end
end)

-- ── IDE ATA PIO Controller (Primary: 0x1F0-0x1F7, 0x3F6) ───────────────
-- Supports: IDENTIFY (0xEC), READ SECTORS (0x20), WRITE SECTORS (0x30)
-- Data is stored as word array (256 words = 512 bytes per sector)
do
	local ide_d = {
		cmd=0, status=0x50, error=0,  -- status: DRDY=0x40, DSC=0x10, DRQ=0x08, ERR=0x01
		features=0, sec_count=1, sec_num=1, cyl_lo=0, cyl_hi=0, head=0xA0,
		data_buf={}, buf_pos=0, buf_len=0,
		drive=0, lba_mode=false,
		packet_phase=nil, packet_cdb={},  -- ATAPI PACKET state
	}

	-- Read 512 bytes from disk into ide_d.data_buf (as bytes, 1-indexed)
	-- ⭐ FIX: drives[0x80] may be aliased to CD-ROM (sector_size=2048).
	-- For CD-ROM, lba is in 2048-byte sectors; read 2048 bytes and use 512-byte slice.
	-- For HDD (sector_size=512), read normally.
	local function ide_read_sector_to_buf(lba)
		ide_d.data_buf = {}
		local drive_id = 0x80  -- primary master = HDD 0
		local d = drives and drives[drive_id]
		if d and d:ptr("rb") then
			local f = d:ptr("rb")
			local ss = d.sector_size or 512
			if ss == 2048 then
				-- CD-ROM aliased as HDD: convert 512-byte LBA to 2048-byte CD sector
				local cd_lba = math.floor(lba * 512 / 2048)
				local cd_off = (lba * 512) % 2048
				f:seek("set", cd_lba * 2048)
				local raw = f:read(2048)
				if raw and #raw >= cd_off + 512 then
					for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = raw:byte(cd_off+i) or 0 end
					return true
				end
			else
				f:seek("set", lba * ss)
				local raw = f:read(ss)
				if raw then
					for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = raw:byte(i) or 0 end
					return true
				end
			end
		end
		-- ⭐ Also try ISO diskData directly (in-memory ISO for no-file-io path)
		-- FIX: ISO is 2048-byte sector format; ATA uses 512-byte LBA.
		-- Map: ATA lba*512 byte offset into the ISO data correctly.
		-- We interpret the ISO as a flat byte array and serve any 512-byte slice.
		if _G.EMU and _G.EMU.diskData then
			local iso = _G.EMU.diskData
			local byte_off = lba * 512  -- treat ISO as flat byte array for ATA reads
			if byte_off >= 0 and byte_off + 512 <= #iso then
				for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = iso:byte(byte_off+i) or 0 end
				emu_debug(2, string.format("[IDE] diskData READ lba=%d off=%d", lba, byte_off))
				return true
			end
		end
		for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = 0 end
		return false
	end

	-- Write 512 bytes from ide_d.data_buf to disk
	local function ide_write_sector_from_buf(lba)
		local drive_id = 0x80
		local d = drives and drives[drive_id]
		if d and d:ptr("ab") then
			local f = d:ptr("ab")
			f:seek("set", lba * (d.sector_size or 512))
			for i=1,512 do f:write(string.char(ide_d.data_buf[i] or 0)) end
			return true
		end
		return false
	end

	-- Compute LBA from current registers
	local function ide_get_lba()
		if ide_d.lba_mode or (ide_d.head -band- 0x40) ~= 0 then
			return (ide_d.sec_num) -bor- (ide_d.cyl_lo -blshift- 8) -bor-
				(ide_d.cyl_hi -blshift- 16) -bor- ((ide_d.head -band- 0x0F) -blshift- 24)
		else
			local cyl = ide_d.cyl_lo -bor- (ide_d.cyl_hi -blshift- 8)
			local head = ide_d.head -band- 0x0F
			local s = (ide_d.sec_num < 1) and 1 or ide_d.sec_num
			return cyl * 16 * 63 + head * 63 + (s - 1)
		end
	end

	-- Execute IDE command
	local function ide_exec()
		if ide_d.cmd == 0xEC then  -- IDENTIFY DEVICE
			-- Fill 512-byte identify data (256 words stored as bytes)
			ide_d.data_buf = {}
			for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = 0 end
			-- word 0: general config = fixed drive
			ide_d.data_buf[1]=0x40; ide_d.data_buf[2]=0x00
			-- word 1: cylinders = 16383
			ide_d.data_buf[3]=0xFF; ide_d.data_buf[4]=0x3F
			-- word 3: heads = 16
			ide_d.data_buf[7]=0x10; ide_d.data_buf[8]=0x00
			-- word 6: sectors/track = 63
			ide_d.data_buf[13]=0x3F; ide_d.data_buf[14]=0x00
			-- word 27-46: model string "RBLX VIRTUAL DISK 1.0"
			local mdl="RBLX VIRTUAL DISK 1.0               " -- 40 chars
			for i=1,20 do
				local ci=(i-1)*2
				ide_d.data_buf[55+ci]=mdl:byte(ci+2) or 0x20
				ide_d.data_buf[56+ci]=mdl:byte(ci+1) or 0x20
			end
			-- word 47 (0-indexed: bytes 95-96): R/W multiple sectors max = 1
			ide_d.data_buf[95]=0x01; ide_d.data_buf[96]=0x80
			-- word 49: capabilities = LBA+DMA
			ide_d.data_buf[99]=0x00; ide_d.data_buf[100]=0x03
			-- word 60-61: total LBA addressable sectors (~512MB = 0x100000)
			ide_d.data_buf[121]=0x00; ide_d.data_buf[122]=0x00
			ide_d.data_buf[123]=0x10; ide_d.data_buf[124]=0x00
			-- word 80: ATA version 4
			ide_d.data_buf[161]=0x10; ide_d.data_buf[162]=0x00
			ide_d.buf_pos = 1
			ide_d.buf_len = 512
			ide_d.status = 0x58  -- DRDY|DRQ
			emu_debug(1, "[IDE] IDENTIFY device")
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0x20 or ide_d.cmd == 0x21 then  -- READ SECTOR(S)
			local lba = ide_get_lba()
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] READ SECTOR lba=%d count=%d", lba, ide_d.sec_count))
			if ide_read_sector_to_buf(lba) then
				ide_d.status = 0x58
			else
				ide_d.status = 0x51  -- DRDY|ERR
				ide_d.error = 0x04   -- ABRT
			end
			ide_d.buf_pos = 1
			ide_d.buf_len = 512
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0x30 or ide_d.cmd == 0x31 then  -- WRITE SECTOR(S)
			-- Prepare for data write: host will write 512 bytes then we commit
			for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = 0 end
			ide_d.buf_pos = 1
			ide_d.buf_len = 512
			ide_d.status = 0x58  -- DRQ ready for data
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0x08 then  -- DEVICE RESET
			ide_d.status = 0x50; ide_d.error = 0x01
			emu_debug(1, "[IDE] DEVICE RESET")
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0xE0 or ide_d.cmd == 0xE1 then  -- STANDBY/IDLE
			ide_d.status = 0x50
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0xEF then  -- SET FEATURES (stub OK)
			ide_d.status = 0x50
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0xA0 then  -- ATAPI PACKET command
			-- Accept PACKET command: host will send 12-byte CDB via port 0x1F0
			-- We collect the CDB, then handle READ(12) = 0xA8
			ide_d.packet_cdb = {}
			ide_d.packet_phase = "cdb"  -- collecting CDB bytes
			ide_d.buf_pos = 1
			ide_d.buf_len = 12  -- CDB is 12 bytes = 6 words
			ide_d.data_buf = {}
			for i=1,12 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = 0 end
			ide_d.status = 0x58  -- DRQ: ready to receive CDB
			emu_debug(1, "[IDE] ATAPI PACKET command received")
		elseif ide_d.cmd == 0xA1 then  -- IDENTIFY PACKET DEVICE
			-- Return ATAPI CD-ROM identity
			ide_d.data_buf = {}
			for i=1,512 do ide_d.data_buf[i] = 0 end
			ide_d.data_buf[1] = 0x85  -- ATAPI, CD-ROM, packet size=12
			ide_d.data_buf[2] = 0xC0
			local mdl = "RBLX ATAPI CD-ROM 1.0           "
			for i=1,16 do
				local ci=(i-1)*2
				ide_d.data_buf[55+ci]=mdl:byte(ci+2) or 0x20
				ide_d.data_buf[56+ci]=mdl:byte(ci+1) or 0x20
			end
			ide_d.buf_pos = 1; ide_d.buf_len = 512
			ide_d.status = 0x58
			emu_debug(1, "[IDE] IDENTIFY PACKET DEVICE")
		else
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] UNKNOWN CMD %02X", ide_d.cmd))
			ide_d.status = 0x51; ide_d.error = 0x04
		end
		-- ⭐ FIX: Raise IRQ14 (IDE primary channel interrupt) after every command.
		-- ldlinux.c32 (COM32) uses interrupt-driven I/O completion.
		-- Without IRQ14, the COM32 interrupt handler never fires and ldlinux
		-- stays in its disk-ready polling loop forever (CS=278E IP=216D).
		-- IRQ14 = slave PIC line 6 (14-8=6 on slave).
		if pic_raise_irq then
			pic_raise_irq(14)
			CPU_HASINT = true
			CPU_HALTED = false
			emu_debug(2, "[IDE] IRQ14 raised after command")
		end
	end

	-- Port 0x1F0: DATA (16-bit R/W)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F0, function()
		-- ⭐ FIX: ATA PIO DATA port is 16-bit (IN AX, 0x1F0 reads 2 bytes as a word).
		-- Return low byte; the emulator will call this twice per word (once per byte).
		-- BUT: real hardware returns a 16-bit word per IN AX. Our port handler returns
		-- 1 byte per call, so we advance buf_pos by 1 each call = correct behavior.
		if ide_d.buf_pos <= ide_d.buf_len then
			local b = ide_d.data_buf[ide_d.buf_pos] or 0
			ide_d.buf_pos = ide_d.buf_pos + 1
			if ide_d.buf_pos > ide_d.buf_len then
				-- ⭐ FIX: Multi-sector read — if sec_count > 1, load next sector
				if (ide_d.cmd == 0x20 or ide_d.cmd == 0x21) and ide_d.sec_count > 1 then
					ide_d.sec_count = ide_d.sec_count - 1
					-- Advance LBA by 1
					if ide_d.lba_mode or (ide_d.head -band- 0x40) ~= 0 then
						local cur_lba = (ide_d.sec_num) -bor- (ide_d.cyl_lo -blshift- 8) -bor-
							(ide_d.cyl_hi -blshift- 16) -bor- ((ide_d.head -band- 0x0F) -blshift- 24)
						cur_lba = cur_lba + 1
						ide_d.sec_num  = cur_lba -band- 0xFF
						ide_d.cyl_lo   = (cur_lba -brshift- 8) -band- 0xFF
						ide_d.cyl_hi   = (cur_lba -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFF
						ide_d.head     = (ide_d.head -band- 0xF0) -bor- ((cur_lba -brshift- 24) -band- 0x0F)
					else
						ide_d.sec_num = ide_d.sec_num + 1
					end
					if ide_read_sector_to_buf(ide_get_lba()) then
						ide_d.buf_pos = 1; ide_d.buf_len = 512
						ide_d.status = 0x58  -- still DRQ
					else
						ide_d.status = 0x50  -- done (or error)
					end
				else
					ide_d.status = 0x50  -- clear DRQ when done
					-- ⭐ FIX: Raise IRQ14 at end of sector transfer
					-- This signals COM32 that the sector read is complete.
					if pic_raise_irq then
						pic_raise_irq(14)
						CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
					end
				end
			end
			return b
		end
		return 0xFF
	end, function(p, v)
		-- Write data for WRITE SECTORS or ATAPI PACKET CDB
		if ide_d.packet_phase == "cdb" then
			-- Collecting ATAPI CDB bytes (12 bytes, written as words = 6 word writes = 12 byte calls)
			-- ⭐ FIX: Since OUT AX is now split into 2 byte calls (lo then hi),
			-- each byte call stores one byte. buf_len=12 means 12 byte calls = correct.
			if ide_d.buf_pos <= ide_d.buf_len then
				ide_d.data_buf[ide_d.buf_pos] = v -band- 0xFF
				ide_d.buf_pos = ide_d.buf_pos + 1
			end
			if ide_d.buf_pos > ide_d.buf_len then
				-- CDB complete: parse and execute
				ide_d.packet_phase = "exec"
				local cmd_code = ide_d.data_buf[1]
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] ATAPI CDB cmd=%02X", cmd_code))
				if cmd_code == 0xA8 or cmd_code == 0x28 then
					-- READ(12) / READ(10): read CD-ROM sectors
					local lba_hi = ide_d.data_buf[3] or 0
					local lba_mh = ide_d.data_buf[4] or 0
					local lba_ml = ide_d.data_buf[5] or 0
					local lba_lo = ide_d.data_buf[6] or 0
					local lba = lba_hi*16777216 + lba_mh*65536 + lba_ml*256 + lba_lo
					local cnt
					if cmd_code == 0xA8 then
						cnt = (ide_d.data_buf[7] or 0)*16777216 + (ide_d.data_buf[8] or 0)*65536
						    + (ide_d.data_buf[9] or 0)*256 + (ide_d.data_buf[10] or 0)
					else  -- READ(10)
						cnt = (ide_d.data_buf[8] or 0)*256 + (ide_d.data_buf[9] or 0)
					end
					emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] ATAPI READ lba=%d cnt=%d", lba, cnt))
					local cd = drives and (drives[0x9F] or drives[0x80])
					local raw = nil
					if cd then
						local fh = cd:ptr("rb")
						fh:seek("set", lba * 2048)
						raw = fh:read(cnt * 2048)
					end
					-- ⭐ Fallback: read directly from in-memory ISO string
					if (not raw or #raw == 0) and _G.EMU and _G.EMU.diskData then
						local iso = _G.EMU.diskData
						local byte_off = lba * 2048 + 1
						local byte_end = math.min(byte_off + cnt * 2048 - 1, #iso)
						if byte_off <= #iso then
							raw = iso:sub(byte_off, byte_end)
							emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] ATAPI READ from diskData lba=%d cnt=%d got=%d", lba, cnt, #raw))
						end
					end
					if raw and #raw > 0 then
						ide_d.data_buf = {}
						for i=1,#raw do ide_d.data_buf[i] = raw:byte(i) or 0 end
						ide_d.buf_pos = 1; ide_d.buf_len = #raw
						ide_d.status = 0x58  -- DRQ
						-- ⭐ FIX: Raise IRQ14 immediately after ATAPI READ data is ready
						-- ldlinux.c32 COM32 waits for this interrupt to know data is available
						if pic_raise_irq then
							pic2.imr = bit32.band(pic2.imr, 0xBF)
							pic.imr  = bit32.band(pic.imr,  0xFB)
							pic_raise_irq(14)
							CPU_HASINT = true; CPU_HALTED = false
						end
					else
						emu_debug(1, string.format("[IDE] ATAPI READ FAILED lba=%d cnt=%d", lba, cnt))
						ide_d.status = 0x51; ide_d.error = 0x04
					end
				elseif cmd_code == 0x43 then
					-- READ TOC: return minimal valid TOC
					ide_d.data_buf = {0,18, 1,1, 0,0x14,1,0, 0,0,0,0, 0,0x14,0xAA, 0,0,0,0,0}
					ide_d.buf_pos = 1; ide_d.buf_len = 20
					ide_d.status = 0x58
				elseif cmd_code == 0x25 then
					-- READ CAPACITY
					local cd2 = drives and (drives[0x9F] or drives[0x80])
					local total_sectors = cd2 and cd2.sectors or 0
					ide_d.data_buf = {
						(total_sectors -brshift- 24) -band- 0xFF,
						(total_sectors -brshift- 16) -band- 0xFF,
						(total_sectors -brshift- 8)  -band- 0xFF,
						total_sectors -band- 0xFF,
						0, 0, 0x08, 0  -- block size = 2048
					}
					ide_d.buf_pos = 1; ide_d.buf_len = 8
					ide_d.status = 0x58
				else
					ide_d.status = 0x51; ide_d.error = 0x04
				end
			end
		elseif ide_d.buf_pos <= ide_d.buf_len then
			ide_d.data_buf[ide_d.buf_pos] = v -band- 0xFF
			ide_d.buf_pos = ide_d.buf_pos + 1
			if ide_d.buf_pos > ide_d.buf_len then
				-- All data received: commit to disk
				ide_write_sector_from_buf(ide_get_lba())
				ide_d.status = 0x50
			end
		end
	end)

	cpu_port_set(0x1F1, function() return ide_d.error end,
		function(p,v) ide_d.features = v end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F2, function() return ide_d.sec_count end,
		function(p,v) ide_d.sec_count = (v==0) and 256 or v end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F3, function() return ide_d.sec_num end,
		function(p,v) ide_d.sec_num = v end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F4, function() return ide_d.cyl_lo end,
		function(p,v) ide_d.cyl_lo = v end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F5, function() return ide_d.cyl_hi end,
		function(p,v) ide_d.cyl_hi = v end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F6, function()
		return ide_d.head -bor- 0xA0  -- always report as ready, LBA capable
	end, function(p,v)
		ide_d.head = v
		ide_d.drive = (v -band- 0x10) ~= 0 and 1 or 0
		ide_d.lba_mode = (v -band- 0x40) ~= 0
	end)
	cpu_port_set(0x1F7,
		function()
			-- ⭐ FIX: If stall-detected, force status READY so ldlinux unblocks
			if _G._ide_status_override then
				-- ⭐ FIX: Keep returning READY until COM32 loop exits (persistent override)
				-- ldlinux polls 0x1F7 millions of times; one-shot nil was not enough.
				ide_d.status = 0x50  -- DRDY|DSC (no DRQ, no BSY, no BSY)
				-- Only clear override when COM32 loop has actually exited
				if not (_G._ldlinux_loaded and CPU_SEGMENTS and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] and
						CPU_SEGMENTS[2] >= 0x1000 and CPU_SEGMENTS[2] < 0xA000) then
					_G._ide_status_override = nil  -- COM32 exited, safe to clear
				end
			end
			return ide_d.status
		end,
		function(p,v)
			ide_d.cmd = v
			ide_exec()
		end)
	-- Alt status / device control port
	cpu_port_set(0x3F6, function() return ide_d.status end,
		function(p,v)
			if (v -band- 0x04) ~= 0 then  -- SRST
				ide_d.status=0x50; ide_d.error=0x01
				emu_debug(1, "[IDE] SRST via 0x3F6")
			end
		end)
	-- Secondary channel stub: always returns 0x7F (no device)
	for _, p in ipairs({0x170,0x171,0x172,0x173,0x174,0x175,0x176,0x177,0x376}) do
		cpu_port_set(p, function() return 0x7F end, function() end)
	end
	emu_debug(1, "[IDE] Primary ATA PIO controller initialized (0x1F0-0x1F7)")
end  -- IDE ATA do-block

-- ── PS/2 Mouse (IRQ12, via 8042 controller port 0x60/0x64) ─────────────
do
	local mouse_enabled    = false
	local mouse_streaming  = false
	local kbd_next_mouse   = false   -- next byte to port 0x60 goes to mouse
	local mouse_pkt_queue  = {}      -- pending mouse packets {flags,dx,dy}
	local mouse_sample_rate= 100
	local mouse_resolution = 2

	-- Inject mouse IRQ (IRQ12 = PIC2 line 4 → vector 0x74)
	local function mouse_irq()
		if pic_trigger then pic_trigger(12)
		elseif pic1 then picint(1 -blshift- (12-8)) end
	end

	-- Push a byte into the keyboard data queue (shared output buffer)
	local function mouse_push(v)
		table.insert(kbd_data_queue, v)
	end

	-- Handle mouse command (sent via 0xD4→0x60)
	local function mouse_cmd(v)
		if v == 0xFF then  -- reset
			mouse_enabled = false; mouse_streaming = false
			mouse_push(0xFA); mouse_push(0xAA); mouse_push(0x00)
		elseif v == 0xF6 then  -- set defaults
			mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xF5 then  -- disable streaming
			mouse_streaming = false; mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xF4 then  -- enable streaming
			mouse_streaming = true; mouse_enabled = true; mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xF3 then  -- set sample rate (next byte)
			mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xF2 then  -- get device ID
			mouse_push(0xFA); mouse_push(0x00)  -- standard mouse
		elseif v == 0xE8 then  -- set resolution
			mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xE7 then  -- set 2:1 scaling
			mouse_push(0xFA)
		elseif v == 0xE6 then  -- set 1:1 scaling
			mouse_push(0xFA)
		else
			mouse_push(0xFA)  -- ACK unknown
		end
	end

	-- Hook into port 0x64 write: detect 0xD4 (next byte to mouse)
	local orig_64_handler = io_ports[0x64+1]
	cpu_port_set(0x64, function(cond,val)
		if not val then
			local ibf = (#kbd_data_queue > 0) and 1 or 0
			-- bit5=mouse data if packet in queue from mouse
			local v = 0x10 -bor- (kbd_a2 -blshift- 3) -bor- ibf
			return v
		else
			if val == 0xD4 then
				kbd_next_mouse = true
				kbd_cmd = val
				kbd_a2 = 1
			elseif orig_64_handler then
				orig_64_handler(cond, val)
			else
				kbd_cmd = val; kbd_a2 = 1
			end
		end
	end)

	-- Hook into port 0x60 write: handle mouse sub-commands
	local orig_60_handler = io_ports[0x60+1]
	cpu_port_set(0x60, function(cond,val)
		if not val then
			-- read: return pending byte
			if #kbd_data_queue > 0 then
				local v = kbd_data_queue[1]
				table.remove(kbd_data_queue, 1)
				if type(v) == "table" then return v[1] end
				return v
			end
			return 0x00
		else
			if kbd_next_mouse then
				kbd_next_mouse = false
				mouse_cmd(val)
			elseif orig_60_handler then
				orig_60_handler(cond, val)
			else
				if kbd_cmd == 0xD1 then
					a20_enabled = (val -band- 0x02) ~= 0
					kbd_cmd = 0
				end
			end
		end
	end)

	-- Drain mouse packet queue each frame (called from cpu_execute tick)
	function mouse_tick()
		if not mouse_streaming or not mouse_enabled then return end
		if #mouse_pkt_queue > 0 then
			local pkt = mouse_pkt_queue[1]
			table.remove(mouse_pkt_queue, 1)
			mouse_push(pkt[1])  -- flags
			mouse_push(pkt[2])  -- dx
			mouse_push(pkt[3])  -- dy
			mouse_irq()
		end
	end

	-- Inject mouse events from UserInputService (must run during emulator init)
	-- This is registered when the port setup runs (inside emulator coroutine)
	function mouse_inject_move(dx, dy, btn)
		if not mouse_enabled then return end
		local flags = 0x08  -- always-1 bit
		if btn then flags = flags -bor- 0x01 end
		if dx < 0 then flags = flags -bor- 0x10 end
		if dy < 0 then flags = flags -bor- 0x20 end
		dx = dx -band- 0xFF; dy = dy -band- 0xFF
		table.insert(mouse_pkt_queue, {flags, dx, dy})
	end

	emu_debug(1, "[MOUSE] PS/2 mouse controller initialized (IRQ12)")
end  -- PS/2 mouse do-block

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x16, function(ax,ah,al)
	if (ah == 0x00) then
		local bios, ascii = nil, nil
		local dd = nil
		if type(charqueue[1]) == "table" then
			dd = charqueue[1]
			table.remove(charqueue, 1)
		end

		if dd ~= nil then
			bios = dd[1]
			ascii = dd[2]
		end

		if bios == nil then
			cpu_set_flag(6)
			return "block"
		else
			cpu_clear_flag(6)
			CPU["regs"][1] = ((bios -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8) -bor- (ascii -band- 0xFF)
			return true
		end
	elseif (ah == 0x01) then
		-- check for keystroke
		local ascii, bios = nil, nil
		if (#charqueue > 0) and type(charqueue[1]) == "table" then
			ascii = charqueue[1][2]
			bios = charqueue[1][1]
		end

		if bios == nil then
			cpu_set_flag(6)
			return true
		else
			cpu_clear_flag(6)
			CPU["regs"][1] = ((bios -band- 0xFF) -blshift- 8) -bor- (ascii -band- 0xFF)
			return true
		end
	elseif (ah == 0x02) then
		-- query shift flags
		if ah == 0x12 then
			ah = RAM[0x418]
		end
		al = RAM[0x417]
		CPU["regs"][1] = (ah -blshift- 8) -bor- al
		return true
	else
		cpu_set_flag(0)
	end
end)

-- ===== sysconf.lua =====

-- machine info
cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x11, function()
	-- equipment list
	CPU["regs"][1] = RAM:r16(0x410)
	return true
end)

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x12, function()
	-- get memory size
	CPU["regs"][1] = RAM:r16(0x413)
	return true
end)

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x15, function(ax,ah,al)
	emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] AX=%04X CS=%04X IP=%04X", ax, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))
	if ax == 0xE820 then
		-- Get System Memory Map (E820h) — correct BIOS spec implementation
		-- EDX must be 'SMAP' (0x534D4150), EBX=0 to start, EBX=0 on last entry
		-- CF=1 means "no more entries" or "not supported"
		-- Memory map:
		--   entry 0 (EBX=0→1): 0x00000000 - 0x0009FFFF  640KB conventional (usable)
		--   entry 1 (EBX=1→2): 0x000F0000 - 0x000FFFFF  384KB BIOS ROM      (reserved)
		--   entry 2 (EBX=2→3): 0x00100000 - 0x00FFFFFF  15MB extended       (usable)
		--   entry 3 (EBX=3→0): 0x00FF0000 - 0x00FFFFFF  ACPI area           (reserved)
		--   EBX=0 after last valid entry → caller knows to stop
		--   next call with EBX=0 but we already returned EBX=0 → CF=1

		local ebx = _G.EMU.CPU.cpu_get32(4)  -- EBX continuation value
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] E820 EBX=%d ES:DI=%04X:%04X", ebx, CPU_SEGMENTS[1], CPU["regs"][8]))

		-- ⭐ FIX: E820 infinite loop — if last entry returned EBX=0, next call with EBX=0 → CF=1
		if ebx == 0 and _G._e820_done then
			_G._e820_done = false
			cpu_set_flag(0)  -- CF=1 = no more entries
			emu_debug(1, "[INT15] E820 EBX=0 (done flag) -> CF=1 end")
			return true
		end

		-- E820 map table: {base_lo, base_hi, len_lo, len_hi, type, next_ebx}
		-- BIOS spec: return EBX=0 on LAST valid entry; subsequent call with EBX=0 → CF=1
                local ramMB = _G.AUTO_RAM_MB or 128
                local ramBytes = ramMB * 1024 * 1024
                local usable = ramBytes - 0x100000  -- extended RAM above 1MB

                local e820_map = {
                                -- entry 0 (EBX=0→1): 0 ~ 639KB conventional RAM (usable)
                                {0x00000000, 0, 0x9FC00,  0, 1, 1},
                                -- entry 1 (EBX=1→2): 0x9FC00 ~ 0x9FFFF EBDA (reserved)
                                {0x0009FC00, 0, 0x400,    0, 2, 2},
                                -- entry 2 (EBX=2→3): 0xA0000 ~ 0xFFFFF video/BIOS (reserved)
                                {0x000A0000, 0, 0x60000,  0, 2, 3},
                                -- entry 3 (EBX=3→0): extended RAM above 1MB (last entry → EBX=0)
                                {0x00100000, 0, usable,   0, 1, 0},
                }
		local entry = e820_map[ebx + 1]
		if entry == nil then
			-- EBX out of range → done
			cpu_set_flag(0)  -- CF=1
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] E820 EBX=%d -> end/CF=1", ebx))
			return true
		end
		-- ⭐ FIX: If this is the last entry (next_ebx=0), set done flag
		if entry[6] == 0 then
			_G._e820_done = true
		end

		local di = CPU["regs"][8]
		local physdi = (CPU_SEGMENTS[1] -blshift- 4) + di
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physdi,     entry[1])  -- base low
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physdi+4,   entry[2])  -- base high
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physdi+8,   entry[3])  -- length low
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physdi+12,  entry[4])  -- length high
		_G.EMU.CPU.ram_w32(physdi+16,  entry[5])  -- type (1=usable, 2=reserved)
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(4, entry[6])         -- EBX = next continuation (0 = last)
		CPU["regs"][2] = 20            -- ECX = bytes written
		_G.EMU.CPU.cpu_set32(1, 0x534D4150)       -- EAX = 'SMAP'
		cpu_clear_flag(0)              -- CF=0 (success)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] E820 entry%d: base=%08X len=%08X type=%d next_ebx=%d",
			ebx, entry[1], entry[3], entry[5], entry[6]))
		return true
        elseif ah == 0x88 then
		-- Get Extended Memory Size (KB above 1MB), use AUTO_RAM_MB
		local ramMB88 = _G.AUTO_RAM_MB or 128
		local extKB = (ramMB88 - 1) * 1024  -- KB above 1MB (max 65535 KB = ~64MB)
		if extKB > 65535 then extKB = 65535 end  -- AH=88 saturates at 65535
		CPU["regs"][1] = extKB
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] AH=88 -> %dMB extended (%dKB)", ramMB88-1, extKB))
		return true
       elseif ax == 0xE801 then
		-- Get memory size for >64MB, use AUTO_RAM_MB
		local ramMB801 = _G.AUTO_RAM_MB or 128
		-- AX = KB between 1M-16M (max 15360 KB = 15MB)
		local ax801 = math.min((ramMB801 - 1) * 1024, 15 * 1024)
		-- BX = 64KB blocks above 16M
		local bx801 = math.max(0, ramMB801 - 16) * 16  -- MB above 16M → 64KB blocks
		CPU["regs"][1] = ax801
		CPU["regs"][2] = bx801
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] E801 -> %dMB (AX=%d BX=%d)", ramMB801, ax801, bx801))
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x87 then
		-- Move Block: CX = word count, ES:SI → GDT table
		-- GDT+0x10: source descriptor (bytes 2-4 = 24-bit base)
		-- GDT+0x18: dest   descriptor (bytes 2-4 = 24-bit base)
		local cx = CPU["regs"][2]  -- word count
		local si = CPU["regs"][7]  -- SI (DI index=8, SI=7)
		local es_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] -blshift- 4  -- ES segment base
		local gdt_base = es_base + si
		-- Read source base address from GDT+0x10 (descriptor bytes 2-4)
		local src_lo = RAM[gdt_base + 0x12]
		local src_mid = RAM[gdt_base + 0x13]
		local src_hi  = RAM[gdt_base + 0x14]
		local src_addr = src_lo -bor- (src_mid -blshift- 8) -bor- (src_hi -blshift- 16)
		-- Read dest base address from GDT+0x18
		local dst_lo = RAM[gdt_base + 0x1A]
		local dst_mid = RAM[gdt_base + 0x1B]
		local dst_hi  = RAM[gdt_base + 0x1C]
		local dst_addr = dst_lo -bor- (dst_mid -blshift- 8) -bor- (dst_hi -blshift- 16)
		-- Copy CX words (CX*2 bytes)
		local byte_count = cx * 2
		-- ⭐ FIX: Use EMU.MEM buffer for addresses ≥ 0x100000 (above 1MB)
		-- RAM[] metatable may not cover extended memory; buffer.readu8/writeu8 always works
		local mem_buf = _G.EMU.MEM
		if mem_buf then
			local src_limit = math.min(src_addr + byte_count, 134217728)
			local dst_limit = math.min(dst_addr + byte_count, 134217728)
			for i = 0, byte_count - 1 do
				local s = src_addr + i
				local d = dst_addr + i
				if s < 134217728 and d < 134217728 then
					buffer.writeu8(mem_buf, d, buffer.readu8(mem_buf, s))
				end
			end
		else
			for i = 0, byte_count - 1 do
				RAM[dst_addr + i] = RAM[src_addr + i]
			end
		end
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AH=0 (success)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] AH=87 Move Block CX=%04X src=%06X dst=%06X -> OK", cx, src_addr, dst_addr))
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x89 then
		-- Switch to protected mode via BIOS
		-- ⭐ FIX: Previously returned CF=1 (unsupported), which caused vmlinuz setup to hang.
		-- vmlinuz (TinyCore) uses INT 15h AH=89 to request BIOS-assisted pmode switch.
		-- We simulate success: AH=0, CF=0. The actual CR0.PE is NOT set here because
		-- ldlinux.c32 will do MOV CR0 itself; we just tell vmlinuz "BIOS approved the switch".
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AH=0 (success)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)  -- CF=0
		a20_enabled = true  -- A20 is enabled by pmode
		emu_debug(1, "[INT15] AH=89 pmode switch -> simulated OK (CF=0, A20 forced on)")
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x90 then
		-- Device busy / callback (stub)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		return true
	elseif ah == 0x91 then
		-- Interrupt complete (stub)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x2400 then
		-- Disable A20 line
		a20_enabled = false
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AH=0 (success)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, "[INT15] A20 disable (2400) -> OK")
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x2401 then
		-- Enable A20 line
		a20_enabled = true
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AH=0 (success)
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, "[INT15] A20 enable (2401) -> OK")
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x2402 then
		-- Query A20 state: AH=0 success, AL=0 disabled / AL=1 enabled
		CPU["regs"][1] = (a20_enabled and 0x01 or 0x00)  -- AH=0, AL=state
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] A20 query (2402) -> AL=%d", a20_enabled and 1 or 0))
		return true
	elseif ax == 0x2403 then
		-- Query A20 support methods
		-- BX bitmask: bit0=BIOS(INT15), bit1=KBC, bit2=Port92, bit3=CPUID
		-- CPU["regs"]: 1=AX,2=CX,3=DX,4=BX,5=SP,6=BP,7=SI,8=DI
		CPU["regs"][4] = 0x0007  -- BX: bit0(BIOS)+bit1(KBC)+bit2(Port92) 지원
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0x00FF  -- AH=0
		cpu_clear_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, "[INT15] A20 query methods (2403) -> BX=0007")
		return true
	elseif ah == 0xC0 then
		-- Get system configuration (stub)
		CPU["regs"][1] = (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF) -bor- (0x80 -blshift- 8)
		cpu_set_flag(0)
		emu_debug(1, "[INT15] AH=C0 sys config -> unsupported CF=1")
		return true
	else
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT15] UNKNOWN AX=%04X -> CF=1", ax))
		CPU["regs"][1] = 0x8600 -bor- (CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF)
		cpu_set_flag(0)
		return true
	end
end)

function sysconf_init()
	local equipment = 0x0021  -- bit0=floppy, bits4-5=10(80x25 color), bits6-7=0(count-1)
	local fdd_count = 1

	for i=0,3 do
		if disk_has(i) and fdd_count == i then
			fdd_count = i + 1
		end
	end

	equipment = equipment -bor- ((fdd_count - 1) -blshift- 6)

	-- BIOS conventional memory (INT 12h)
	-- Linux는 여기서 640KB 기대함 → 유지
	local ramMB = _G.AUTO_RAM_MB or 128
	local ramKB = ramMB * 1024

	RAM:w16(0x410, equipment) -- equipment list
	RAM:w16(0x413, math.min(640, ramKB)) -- conventional memory
end

-- CPU reset vector
RAM[0xFFFFE] = 0xFB

do local rdate = "07/06/98"
for i=1,#rdate do RAM[0xFFFF4 + i] = string.byte(rdate, i, i) end
end

-- ===== comms.lua =====

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x14, function(ax,ah,al)
	-- serial
	if (ah == 0x00) or (ah == 0x03) then
		CPU["regs"][1] = 0x0000
		emu_debug(0, "serial: get port status/init\n")
		return true
	else
		cpu_set_flag(0)
	end
end)

cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x17, function(ax,ah,al)
	-- printer
	if (ah == 0x01) or (ah == 0x02) then
		CPU["regs"][1] = CPU["regs"][1] -band- 0xFF
		emu_debug(0, "printer: get port status/init\n")
		return true
	else
		cpu_set_flag(0)
	end
end)

-- ── INT 70h-77h: IRQ8-15 Hardware Interrupt Handlers ──────────
-- These are the interrupt vectors for slave PIC IRQs (8-15).
-- IRQ14 (INT 76h) = IDE Primary Channel interrupt (used by ldlinux.c32 for disk I/O).
-- Without a handler, cpu_int(0x76) reads IVT[0x76*4]=0:0 and crashes to 0000:0000.
-- Install minimal "send EOI + IRET" handlers so ldlinux COM32 disk waits resolve.
for _irq8 = 0, 7 do
	local _irqn = 0x70 + _irq8  -- INT 70h..77h
	local _irq_real = _irq8 + 8  -- IRQ 8..15
	cpu_register_interrupt_handler(_irqn, function()
		-- Send EOI to slave PIC (port 0xA0) then master PIC (port 0x20)
		-- In our emulator, call pic_lower_irq to clear the IRQ line.
		if _irqn == 0x76 then
			emu_debug(2, string.format("[INT76] IDE IRQ14 interrupt handler: EOI+return"))
			-- Lower IRQ14 in slave PIC
			if pic_lower_irq then pic_lower_irq(14) end
		end
		-- Return true = handler consumed interrupt; cpu_int will IRET automatically
		return true
	end)
end
emu_debug(1, "[BIOS] INT 70h-77h hardware interrupt handlers installed")

-- ── INT 22h: syslinux/ISOLINUX COMBOOT API ───────────────────────────────
-- ldlinux.c32 uses INT 22h to load vmlinuz/core.gz via syslinux file API.
-- Without this handler, ldlinux.c32 spins forever trying to load the kernel.
-- We implement the minimal subset needed to boot TinyCore Linux.
do
	local _sl_files = {}   -- open file handles: handle_id → {lba, size, pos}
	local _sl_next_handle = 1

	cpu_register_interrupt_handler(0x22, function(ax)
		_G._int22_call_count = (_G._int22_call_count or 0) + 1
		local ah = bit32.rshift(ax, 8)
		local al = bit32.band(ax, 0xFF)
		emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] AX=%04X CS=%04X IP=%04X", ax, CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP))

		if ax == 0x0000 then
			-- Terminate COMBOOT program (return to loader)
			CPU["regs"][1] = 0; cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x000A then
			-- Final cleanup / prepare to boot (no-op in emulator)
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0014 or ax == 0x006B then
			-- AX=0014h/006Bh: Open file by name
			-- ES:SI = filename (null-terminated), CX = mode
			-- Returns: SI = file handle (0=not found), EAX = file size (bytes), DX = blocks
			local es_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] * 16
			local si = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][7], 0xFFFF)
			local fname = ""
			local i = 0
			while i < 64 do
				local b = RAM[es_base + si + i] or 0
				if b == 0 then break end
				fname = fname .. string.char(b)
				i = i + 1
			end
			fname = fname:upper()
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] OpenFile: '%s'", fname))
			-- Look up in ISO9660 pre-loaded metadata
			local lba, sz = nil, nil
			if fname:find("VMLINUZ") or fname:find("BZIMAGE") then
				lba = _G._kernel_lba; sz = _G._kernel_size
			elseif fname:find("CORE%.GZ") or fname:find("ROOTFS") or fname:find("INITRD") then
				lba = _G._initrd_lba; sz = _G._initrd_size
			elseif fname:find("LDLINUX%.C32") or fname:find("LDLINUX%.SYS") then
				-- Already loaded; return dummy handle pointing to RAM
				CPU["regs"][7] = 1  -- handle=1
				CPU["regs"][1] = 65536  -- EAX low = 64KB
				CPU["regs"][3] = 0   -- DX=0
				cpu_clear_flag(0)
				print(string.format("[INT22] OpenFile '%s' → ldlinux handle (pre-loaded)", fname))
				return true
			end
			if lba and sz and sz > 0 then
				local handle = _sl_next_handle
				_sl_next_handle = _sl_next_handle + 1
				_sl_files[handle] = {lba=lba, size=sz, pos=0}
				CPU["regs"][7] = handle  -- SI = file handle
				-- Return EAX = file size (32-bit, stored in AX+DX for 16-bit code)
				CPU["regs"][1] = sz % 65536   -- AX = low 16 bits of size
				CPU["regs"][3] = math.floor(sz / 65536)  -- DX = high 16 bits
				cpu_clear_flag(0)
				print(string.format("[INT22] OpenFile '%s' → handle=%d size=%d lba=%d", fname, handle, sz, lba))
			else
				-- File not found
				CPU["regs"][7] = 0   -- SI=0 = not found
				CPU["regs"][1] = 0
				cpu_set_flag(0)  -- CF=1
				print(string.format("[INT22] OpenFile '%s' → NOT FOUND", fname))
			end
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0016 or ax == 0x006C then
			-- AX=0016h/006Ch: Read file
			-- SI = file handle, ES:BX = buffer, CX = # 512-byte sectors to read
			-- Returns: CF=0 ok, SI=updated handle, AX=# sectors read, DX=EOF flag
			local handle = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][7], 0xFFFF)  -- SI
			local cx = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][2], 0xFFFF)
			local bx = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][4], 0xFFFF)
			local f = _sl_files[handle]
			if not f then
				CPU["regs"][1] = 0; cpu_set_flag(0)
				emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] ReadFile bad handle=%d", handle))
				return true
			end
			local bytes_req = cx * 512
			local bytes_left = f.size - f.pos
			local bytes_read = math.min(bytes_req, bytes_left)
			local dest_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[1] * 16 + bx
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] ReadFile handle=%d lba=%d pos=%d req=%d", handle, f.lba, f.pos, bytes_req))
			-- Read from ISO data
			local iso = _G.EMU and _G.EMU.diskData
			local mem_buf = _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM
			if iso and bytes_read > 0 then
				local iso_byte_off = f.lba * 2048 + f.pos
				if mem_buf then
					for i = 0, bytes_read - 1 do
						local src = iso_byte_off + i
						local dst = dest_base + i
						local b = (src >= 0 and src < #iso) and iso:byte(src+1) or 0
						if dst >= 0 and dst < 134217728 then
							buffer.writeu8(mem_buf, dst, b)
						end
					end
				else
					for i = 0, bytes_read - 1 do
						RAM[dest_base + i] = iso:byte(iso_byte_off + i + 1) or 0
					end
				end
				f.pos = f.pos + bytes_read
			end
			local secs_read = math.ceil(bytes_read / 512)
			CPU["regs"][1] = secs_read   -- AX = sectors read
			CPU["regs"][3] = (f.pos >= f.size) and 1 or 0  -- DX: 0=more data, 1=EOF
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			print(string.format("[INT22] ReadFile handle=%d read=%d pos=%d/%d EOF=%s", handle, bytes_read, f.pos, f.size, tostring(f.pos >= f.size)))
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0018 or ax == 0x006D then
			-- Close file handle
			local handle = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][7], 0xFFFF)
			_sl_files[handle] = nil
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] CloseFile handle=%d", handle))
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0009 then
			-- Check serial port (stub)
			CPU["regs"][3] = 0; cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x001C then
			-- Write character to screen (DL = char)
			local ch = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][3], 0xFF)
			if ch >= 32 or ch == 10 or ch == 13 then
				term_putchar(ch)
			end
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0001 then
			-- Print string DS:SI
			local ds_base = CPU_SEGMENTS[4] * 16
			local si2 = bit32.band(CPU["regs"][7], 0xFFFF)
			local s = ""; local j = 0
			while j < 256 do
				local b = RAM[ds_base + si2 + j] or 0
				if b == 0 then break end
				s = s .. string.char(b); j = j + 1
			end
			print("[INT22] Print: " .. s)
			for k = 1, #s do term_putchar(s:byte(k)) end
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x0020 or ax == 0x0023 then
			-- AX=0020h: RunKernelImage — ldlinux.c32가 커널을 부팅할 때 호출
			-- AX=0023h: RunDefaultCommand — 기본 부팅 커맨드 실행
			-- ⭐ 이것이 핵심! ldlinux.c32가 vmlinuz를 찾아서 실행하려 할 때 사용
			print(string.format("[INT22] RunKernelImage/RunDefaultCommand AX=%04X — forcing kernel boot!", ax))
			_G._int22_boot_called = true
			local kernel_addr = _G._kernel_addr or 0x100000
			local initrd_addr = _G._initrd_addr or 0x800000
			local initrd_size = _G._initrd_size or 0
			local kernel_size = _G._kernel_size or 0
			-- boot_params (linux x86 boot protocol) at 0x90000
			local bp = 0x90000
			local mem = _G.EMU and _G.EMU.MEM
			local function wb(a, v)
				if mem then buffer.writeu8(mem, a, v % 256)
				else RAM[a] = v % 256 end
			end
			local function ww(a, v)
				wb(a, v%256); wb(a+1, math.floor(v/256)%256)
			end
			local function wd(a, v)
				ww(a,v%65536); ww(a+2,math.floor(v/65536)%65536)
			end
			if kernel_size > 0 then
				-- Linux bzImage boot protocol v2.13
				-- setup_sects at kernel+0x1F1
				local setup_sects = 0
				if mem then
					setup_sects = buffer.readu8(mem, kernel_addr + 0x1F1)
				else
					setup_sects = RAM[kernel_addr + 0x1F1] or 0
				end
				if setup_sects == 0 then setup_sects = 4 end
				local setup_size = (setup_sects + 1) * 512
				-- boot_params at 0x90000 — copy setup code there
				if mem then
					for i = 0, math.min(setup_size, 8192) - 1 do
						buffer.writeu8(mem, bp + i, buffer.readu8(mem, kernel_addr + i))
					end
				end
				-- Populate boot_params fields
				ww(bp + 0x210, 0xB1)           -- type_of_loader = 0xB1 (custom)
				wb(bp + 0x211, 0x81)            -- loadflags = LOADED_HIGH | CAN_USE_HEAP
				ww(bp + 0x218, initrd_addr % 65536)
				ww(bp + 0x21A, math.floor(initrd_addr / 65536) % 65536)  -- ramdisk_image
				ww(bp + 0x21C, initrd_size % 65536)
				ww(bp + 0x21E, math.floor(initrd_size / 65536) % 65536)  -- ramdisk_size
				-- cmdline: "auto\0" at 0x91000
				local cmdline = "auto"
				for i = 1, #cmdline do wb(0x91000 + i - 1, cmdline:byte(i)) end
				wb(0x91000 + #cmdline, 0)
				ww(bp + 0x228, 0x1000)  -- cmd_line_ptr low
				ww(bp + 0x22A, 0x0009)  -- cmd_line_ptr high (0x00091000)
				-- Jump to kernel setup code entry
				-- Real-mode entry: (setup_size/16):0x0000 from kernel_addr
				-- But typically linux jumps to CS:0x0200 (start of protected-mode loader)
				-- For real-mode: CS = (kernel_addr >> 4), IP = 0
				-- kernel setup is copied to 0x90000, entry = 0x9020:0000
				CPU_SEGMENTS[2] = 0x9020  -- CS
				CPU_IP = 0x0000
				CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000  -- SS
				CPU_REGS[5] = 0xFF00      -- SP
				CPU_SEGMENTS[4] = 0x9000  -- DS
				CPU_SEGMENTS[1] = 0x9000  -- ES
				CPU_SEGMENTS[3] = 0x9000  -- FS
				CPU_SEGMENTS[6] = 0x9000  -- GS
				CPU_FLAGS = bit32.bor(CPU_FLAGS, 0x200)  -- STI
				CPU_HALTED = false
				CPU_HASINT = false
				print(string.format("[INT22] Jumping to kernel setup CS=9020:0000 (kernel@%X setup_sects=%d)", kernel_addr, setup_sects))
			else
				-- 커널 없음 - 오류 메시지
				print("[INT22] RunKernelImage: NO KERNEL LOADED! Check ISO9660 preload.")
				CPU_REGS[1] = 0; cpu_set_flag(0)
			end
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x000E then
			-- GetKernelName: return empty string (use default)
			CPU_REGS[7] = 0  -- SI=0
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		elseif ax == 0x000F or ax == 0x0010 or ax == 0x0011 or ax == 0x0013 or ax == 0x001F then
			-- Various info stubs
			CPU_REGS[1] = 0; CPU_REGS[3] = 0
			cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true

		else
			emu_debug(1, string.format("[INT22] UNKNOWN AX=%04X", ax))
			CPU["regs"][1] = 0; cpu_clear_flag(0)
			return true
		end
	end)
end  -- INT 22h syslinux COMBOOT API

-- ===== kbdmaps.lua =====

map_char_to_key = {}
map_char_to_key[258] = 0x50 -- down
map_char_to_key[260] = 0x4B -- left
map_char_to_key[259] = 0x48 -- up
map_char_to_key[261] = 0x4D -- right
map_char_to_key[13] = 0x1C -- enter
map_char_to_key[0] = 0
map_char_to_key[0x1C] = 1 -- esc
for i=1,9 do map_char_to_key[i + 48] = i + 1 end
do -- kbdmaps scope (prevents chrs from consuming main chunk local slots)
local chrs = "!@#$%^&*()"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs, i, i)] = i + 1 end
map_char_to_key[48] = 11 -- numbers
map_char_to_key[45] = 12 -- -
map_char_to_key[95] = 12 -- _
map_char_to_key[61] = 13 -- =
map_char_to_key[43] = 12 -- +
map_char_to_key[8] = 14 -- backspace
map_char_to_key[9] = 15 -- tab
local chrs = "qwertyuiop[]"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 15 + i end
local chrs = "QWERTYUIOP{}"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 15 + i end
map_char_to_key[13] = 28 -- enter
-- 29?
local chrs = "asdfghjkl;'"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 29 + i end
local chrs = "ASDFGHJKL:\""
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 29 + i end
map_char_to_key[96] = 41 -- `
map_char_to_key[126] = 41 -- ~
-- 42?
map_char_to_key[92] = 43 -- \
map_char_to_key[124] = 43 -- |
local chrs = "zxcvbnm,./"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 43 + i end
local chrs = "ZXCVBNM<>?"
for i=1,#chrs do map_char_to_key[string.byte(chrs,i,i)] = 43 + i end
-- 54?
map_char_to_key[42] = 55 -- *
-- 56?
map_char_to_key[32] = 57 -- space
end -- kbdmaps scope

-- ⭐ FIX v2: disk_init override — register drives[0x80] as CD-ROM ISO (sector_size=2048)
-- BUG FIX: old version shared a single iso_pos across all ptr() callers → corrupted reads.
-- Now ptr() creates a FRESH independent file handle each call (like a real file open).
do -- disk_init override scope (keep _orig_disk_init and make_iso_handle local to here)
local _orig_disk_init = disk_init
local function make_iso_handle(iso)
	local sz = #iso
	local pos = 0
	return {
		seek = function(_, w, off)
			off = off or 0
			if     w == "set" then pos = off
			elseif w == "cur" then pos = pos + off
			elseif w == "end" then pos = sz + off end
			if pos < 0 then pos = 0 end
			return pos
		end,
		read = function(_, n)
			if type(n) == "number" then
				local s = string.sub(iso, pos+1, pos+n)
				pos = math.min(pos + n, sz)
				return s
			end
			local s = string.sub(iso, pos+1)
			pos = sz
			return s
		end,
		write = function() end,
		close = function() end,
	}
end
function disk_init(fn, id)
	-- For drive 0x80 loaded with an ISO, build an in-memory CD drive directly
	if id == 0x80 and _G.EMU.diskData and #_G.EMU.diskData > 0 then
		local iso = _G.EMU.diskData
		local sz  = #iso
		local total_sectors = math.floor(sz / 2048)
		-- IMPORTANT: ptr() must return a NEW handle each call (independent seek position)
		local d = {
			id = 0x80,
			floppy = false,
			inserted = true,
			sector_size = 2048,
			sectors = 1,
			heads = 1,
			cylinders = total_sectors,
			ptr = function(_, mode) return make_iso_handle(iso) end,
		}
		drives[0x80] = d
		-- Also update _ddata so io_seek.open("drive:80",...) returns correct data
		_ddata = _ddata or {}
		_ddata[0x80] = iso
		_handles = _handles or {}
		_handles[0x80] = nil  -- clear cached handles so they get fresh ones
		RAM[0x475] = math.max(RAM[0x475] or 0, 1)
		print(string.format("[disk_init] drive:80 ISO in-memory %dMB, %d sectors (2048b)", math.floor(sz/1048576), total_sectors))
	else
		_orig_disk_init(string.format("drive:%02X", id), id)
	end
end
end -- disk_init override scope

-- ⭐ OPTIMIZED: Download ISO once, reuse everywhere (was downloading 3x!)
_G.EMU.DISK_URL = "https://github.com/csj01csj/freedosimg/raw/refs/heads/main/Core-current.iso"

-- We'll download once in step 3 below. Reserve slot now.
_G.EMU.diskData = nil

print("[AUTO RAM] 128MB RAM reserved (Pentium III mode)")
_G.AUTO_RAM_MB = 128

print("[step 1] script started!")
setStatus("[1/7] initialized")
task.wait(0.1)

print("[step 2] checking DiskLoader RemoteFunction...")
setStatus("[2/7] checking server connection...")
if not DiskLoader then
	setStatus("failed! DiskLoader not found. Make sure ServerScript is running.")
	print("[step 2] failed: DiskLoader RemoteFunction not found")
	return
end
print("[step 2] DiskLoader OK!")

print("[step 3] downloading TinyCore Linux ISO... (10~60 sec)")
setStatus("[3/7] downloading ISO... (please wait)")
task.wait(0.1)

do -- download scope
local dlOk, dlErr = pcall(function()
	local data, err = DiskLoader:InvokeServer(_G.EMU.DISK_URL)
	if data and #data > 0 then
		-- ⭐ Store for reuse — no re-download later
		_G.EMU.diskData = data
		disk_load_data(0x80, data)
		-- auto-detect geometry from size
		local sz = #data
		local geom = "unknown"
		if     sz == 2949120 then geom = "2.88MB (36s/2h/80c)"
		elseif sz == 1761280 then geom = "1.72MB (21s/2h/82c)"
		elseif sz == 1720320 then geom = "1.72MB (21s/2h/80c)"
		elseif sz == 1474560 then geom = "1.44MB (18s/2h/80c)"
		elseif sz == 1228800 then geom = "1.20MB (15s/2h/80c)"
		elseif sz ==  737280 then geom = "720KB  (9s/2h/80c)"
		elseif sz ==  368640 then geom = "360KB  (9s/2h/40c)"
		elseif sz ==  327680 then geom = "320KB  (8s/2h/40c)"
		elseif sz ==  184320 then geom = "180KB  (9s/1h/40c)"
		elseif sz ==  163840 then geom = "160KB  (8s/1h/40c)"
		else geom = "ISO/HDD/custom" end
		print(string.format("[step 3] download complete! %d bytes (%s)", sz, geom))
		setStatus(string.format("[3/7] %d bytes (%s)", sz, geom))
		print("[step 3] first 4 bytes: " .. string.format("%02X %02X %02X %02X", data:byte(1), data:byte(2), data:byte(3), data:byte(4)))
		-- Auto-size RAM based on ISO
		_G.EMU.isoMB = math.max(1, math.ceil(sz / (1024*1024)))
		_G.EMU.ramMB = math.max(128, math.min(256, _G.EMU.isoMB * 6))  -- 6x ISO size, 128~256MB
		_G.AUTO_RAM_MB = _G.EMU.ramMB
		print(string.format("[AUTO RAM] ISO: %dMB → RAM: %dMB", _G.EMU.isoMB, _G.EMU.ramMB))
		-- ⭐ 실제 MEM 버퍼도 새로 할당 (기존 128MB 이상이 필요한 경우)
		local needed_bytes = _G.EMU.ramMB * 1024 * 1024
		if _G.EMU.MEM and buffer.len(_G.EMU.MEM) < needed_bytes then
			local ok_resize, err_resize = pcall(function()
				_G.EMU.MEM = buffer.create(needed_bytes)
			end)
			if ok_resize then
				print(string.format("[AUTO RAM] MEM buffer resized to %dMB", _G.EMU.ramMB))
			else
				print("[AUTO RAM] MEM resize failed (keeping 128MB): " .. tostring(err_resize))
				_G.EMU.ramMB = 128
				_G.AUTO_RAM_MB = 128
			end
		end
	else
		error(tostring(err) or "empty data")
	end
end)
if not dlOk then
	setStatus("download failed: " .. tostring(dlErr))
	print("[step 3] failed: " .. tostring(dlErr))
	_G.EMU._dl_failed = true
end
end -- download scope
if _G.EMU._dl_failed then return end

print("[step 4] calling disk_init...")
setStatus("[4/7] initializing disk... (86Box Mode)")

-- ── Boot Sequence (Tiny Core Linux) ──
function start_boot_sequence()
    print("[86Box] Starting boot sequence via disk_boot()...")

    -- disk_load_data(0x80, ...) was already called in step 3.
    -- Now call disk_init to register drive 0x80 so disk_boot() can use it.
    setStatus("[5/7] registering disk drive...")
    local initOk, initErr = pcall(function()
        disk_init(string.format("drive:%02X", 0x80), 0x80)
    end)
    if not initOk then
        print("[boot] disk_init warning: " .. tostring(initErr))
        -- Non-fatal: continue anyway, drives[0x80] may still be set
    end

    setStatus("[6/7] El Torito boot parsing...")
    -- ⭐ Pre-load ldlinux.sys from ISO 9660 directly into RAM
    -- This ensures isolinux stage2 is available even if INT 13h interception fails
    if _G.EMU.diskData and #_G.EMU.diskData > 0 then
        local preloaded = iso9660_preload_ldlinux(_G.EMU.diskData)
        if preloaded then
            print("[boot] ldlinux.sys pre-loaded from ISO 9660 into RAM[0x10000]")
        end
    end
    -- disk_boot() handles El Torito parsing, registers drives[0x9F] for CD,
    -- loads the isolinux boot image, sets CS:IP, and sets DL correctly.
    local bootOk, bootErr = pcall(function()
        disk_boot(0x80)
    end)
    if not bootOk then
        print("[boot] disk_boot() failed: " .. tostring(bootErr))
        -- Fallback: manually set reset vector to 0x0000:0x7C00
        _G.EMU.IP = 0x7C00
        _G.EMU.SEGS[2] = 0x0000  -- CS
        _G.EMU.SEGS[3] = 0x0000  -- SS
        CPU_REGS[5] = 0x8000      -- SP
        print("[boot] Fallback: jumping to 0000:7C00")
    end

    -- Pentium III BIOS setup: SP, SS, ES, DS all to sane values
    -- (isolinux expects SS:SP to be valid for stack operations)
    if CPU_SEGMENTS[3] == 0 then
        CPU_REGS[5] = 0x8000  -- SP = 0x8000 (top of conventional memory)
    end

    setStatus("[7/7] CPU executing...")
    -- DL = boot drive (set by disk_boot via CPU["regs"][3])
    local dl_val = CPU_REGS and CPU_REGS[3] or 0
    print(string.format("[86Box] Jumping to CS=%04X IP=%04X DL=%02X",
        CPU_SEGMENTS[2], CPU_IP, bit32.band(dl_val, 0xFF)))

    if emu_execute then
        emu_execute()
    elseif cpu_execute then
        cpu_execute()
    else
        print("[error] No execution loop found!")
    end
end
task.spawn(start_boot_sequence)

-- ── 86Box High-Fidelity Hardware Extensions ──

-- Pentium III MSR & CPUID (Coppermine)
_G.EMU.cpuid = function(eax)
    if eax == 0 then
        return 2, 0x756E6547, 0x6C65746E, 0x49656E69 -- GenuineIntel
    elseif eax == 1 then
        return 0x00000686, 0, 0, 0x0387F9FF -- Family 6, Model 8 (PIII), Features
    end
    return 0,0,0,0
end

-- 86Box PIC State Machine (Cascade)
_G.EMU.pic_ack = function(irq)
    local master = _G.EMU.HW.PIC.master
    local slave = _G.EMU.HW.PIC.slave
    if irq >= 8 then
        slave.isr = bit32.bor(slave.isr, bit32.lshift(1, irq-8))
        master.isr = bit32.bor(master.isr, 4) -- IRQ2 cascade
        return slave.icw2 + (irq-8)
    else
        master.isr = bit32.bor(master.isr, bit32.lshift(1, irq))
        return master.icw2 + irq
    end
end
_G.EMU.pic_raise_irq = pic_raise_irq
_G.EMU.pic_lower_irq = pic_lower_irq
_G.EMU.pic_set_level = pic_set_level

-- 86Box PIT Logic (8254)
_G.EMU.pit_tick_catchup = function(cycles)
    local pit = _G.EMU.HW.PIT
    local ch = pit.channels[1]
    ch.count = ch.count - cycles
    while ch.count <= 0 do
        ch.count = ch.count + ch.reload
        _G.EMU.pic_raise_irq(0)
    end
end

-- IDE DMA Transfer (Buffer optimized)
_G.EMU.ide_dma = function(addr, size, read)
    if read then
        buffer.copy(_G.EMU.MEM, addr, _G.EMU.HW.IDE.data_buf, 0, size)
    else
        buffer.copy(_G.EMU.HW.IDE.data_buf, 0, _G.EMU.MEM, addr, size)
    end
end
